### [1] [BackendForge: Benchmarking Agentic End-to-End Code Generation with Backend Services](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11042v1)
*Yuzhe Guo,Mengzhou Wu,Yuan Cao,Jialei Wei,Dezhi Ran,Wei Yang,Tao Xie*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BackendForge基准测试表明，LLM在生成完整后端服务方面仍存在较大差距，从基础到最终预言成功率下降显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估智能体LLM生成可部署且行为正确的端到端软件工件的能力。

Method: 构建BackendForge基准，包含56个基于真实开源应用的后端生成任务，使用测试代理和代码代理共同演化测试和参考实现。

Result: GPT-5.5在基础预言下成功55.4%，在最终预言下仅28.6%。

Conclusion: 当前LLM能实现局部API行为但难以生成完整后端服务。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地用于智能体编码场景，它们可以检查文件、执行命令、运行测试、观察失败并迭代修改代码。这种转变提出了一个核心评估问题：智能体LLM能否生成一个既可部署又在执行上行为正确的端到端软件工件？后端服务为此评估提供了一个可控但现实的基板。它们的API暴露了应用级别的可执行语义，并且可以通过黑盒HTTP交互根据OpenAPI契约确定性地检查部署后的行为。我们引入了BackendForge，这是一个包含56个契约定义的后端生成任务的基准测试，这些任务来自真实的开源应用。给定可见的规范和OpenAPI契约，LLM必须生成一个通过HTTP测试构建、部署和评估的Docker化服务。为了在不引入隐藏要求的情况下加强评估，BackendForge使用测试代理和代码代理共同演化测试预言和参考服务，其中测试代理提出基于规范的后端测试，代码代理修复参考实现。尽管表现最好的模型GPT-5.5在基础预言下成功完成了55.4%的任务，但在最终预言下仅完成了28.6%。这一差距表明，当前的LLM可以实现许多局部API行为，但仍然难以生成完整的后端服务。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in agentic coding settings, where they can inspect files, execute commands, run tests, observe failures, and iteratively revise code. This shift raises a central evaluation question: can an agentic LLM generate an end-to-end software artifact that is both deployable and behaviorally correct under execution? Backend services provide a controlled but realistic substrate for this evaluation. Their APIs expose application-level executable semantics, and deployed behavior can be checked deterministically against an OpenAPI contract through black-box HTTP interactions. We introduce BackendForge, a benchmark of 56 contract-defined backend generation tasks rewritten from real open-source applications. Given a visible specification and an OpenAPI contract, an LLM must generate a Dockerized service that is built, deployed, and evaluated only through HTTP tests. To strengthen evaluation without introducing hidden requirements, BackendForge uses a test agent and a code agent to co-evolve the test oracle and reference service, where the test agent proposes specification-grounded backend tests and the code agent repairs the reference implementation. Although the best-performing model, GPT-5.5, succeeds on 55.4\% of tasks under the base oracle, it succeeds on only 28.6\% under the final oracle. This gap suggests that current LLMs can implement many local API behaviors, but still struggle to produce complete backend services.

</details>


### [2] [Retrieval-Oriented Code Representations in Agentic Bug Localization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11046v1)
*Genevieve Caumartin,Tse-Hsun,Chen,Diego Elias Costa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究代码表示对LLM智能体在仓库级缺陷定位中的影响，发现角色感知摘要实现最佳成本效益平衡，而原始源代码虽有效但成本高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究未充分探索文本代码表示在检索和定位中的作用，需要系统比较不同表示对定位效果和成本的影响。

Method: 在LCA和SWE数据集上，比较文件路径、原始源代码和三种LLM生成的文本表示，采用词汇、语义和LLM检索，以及LLM后排序，并用表示足迹衡量成本。

Result: 角色感知摘要比文件路径提升Hit@5达40%，足迹小10.4-20.9倍；结合互补表示和LLM排序分别再提升31.9%和42.0%；Agentless案例中Hit@6达94%。

Conclusion: 代码表示应作为智能体定位管道的一流设计选择，需根据管道阶段和成本-准确性要求进行权衡，角色感知摘要为最佳折衷方案。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体越来越多地被用于支持软件开发，但它们在仓库级任务中的表现取决于检索到正确的代码上下文。已有研究探索了使用传统信息检索（基于文件路径和原始源代码）进行文件级定位。然而，文本代码表示在检索和定位中的作用仍未得到充分探索。我们将文件级缺陷定位作为一个表示驱动的检索问题进行研究。在Long Code Arena (LCA)和SWE-bench Verified (SWE)数据集上，我们比较了五种代码表示：文件路径、原始源代码和三种LLM生成的文本表示。我们的实验包括词汇、语义和基于LLM的检索，随后是基于LLM的后检索排序。我们通过表示足迹量化了表示带来的成本。我们发现，代码表示的选择会影响定位效果和成本。角色感知摘要比文件路径表示在Hit@5上提高了高达40%，同时所需的表示足迹比原始源代码小10.4到20.9倍。结合互补表示结果并使用LLM对检索到的候选进行排序，分别提供了高达31.9%和42.0%的进一步增益。总体而言，角色感知摘要提供了最佳的成本效益权衡，而原始源代码在某些设置下提供了有效性，但成本显著更高。在与Agentless的案例研究中，我们的技术在知名管道中显示了实用性，在文件定位上达到94%的Hit@6（比基线高4.7%）。我们的发现表明，在智能体定位管道中，代码表示应被视为一流的设计选择，并受管道阶段和成本准确性要求的指导。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly being used to support software development, yet their performance in repository-level tasks depends on retrieving the right code context. Existing studies have explored file-level localization using traditional information retrieval over file paths and raw source code. However, the role of textual code representations in retrieval and localization remains underexplored.
  We study file-level bug localization as a representation-driven retrieval problem. Across the Long Code Arena (LCA) and SWE-bench Verified (SWE) datasets, we compare five code representations: file paths, raw source code, and three LLM-generated textual representations. Our experiments include lexical, semantic, and LLM-based retrieval, followed by LLM-based post-retrieval ranking. We quantify the cost incurred by a representation through the representation footprint. We find that the choice of code representation affects both localization effectiveness and cost. Role-aware summaries outperform file-path representations by up to 40% Hit@5 while requiring a representation footprint 10.4 to 20.9x smaller than raw source code. Combining complementary representation results and ranking retrieved candidates with an LLM provides further gains of up to 31.9% and 42.0%, respectively. Overall, role-aware summaries provide the best cost-effectiveness trade-off, while raw source code offers effectiveness in some settings at a significantly higher cost. A case study with Agentless reveals the utility of our techniques within a well-known pipeline, reaching 94% Hit@6 on file localization (+4.7% against the baseline). Our findings suggest that code representation should be treated as a first-class design choice in agentic localization pipelines, guided by pipeline stage and cost-accuracy requirements.

</details>


### [3] [AgentCheck: A Reproduce-Intervene-Mitigate Workbench for LLM Agents over MCP](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11098v3)
*Aritra Mazumder,Nusrat jahan Lia*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AgentCheck是一个开源工具，通过记录和扰动工具响应来复现、干预和确认LLM代理的故障，帮助开发者在部署前测试和修复问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估假设工具工作正常，但实际部署中工具可能出错，开发者需要可控的方式复现和修复故障。

Method: AgentCheck将MCP服务器作为干预面，记录代理与真实工具的交互，然后用12种故障类型扰动响应，重放匹配调用并在偏离后实时执行，形成复现-干预-确认循环，评分结合确定性和LLM评判。

Result: 五个代理中最佳105/120，最弱77/120；最弱代理上重试缓解将超时故障成功率从30%提到100%，但过时数据故障仍为30-40%。

Conclusion: AgentCheck使故障模式在部署前可复现、可比较、可验证，帮助开发者发现和缓解问题。

中文摘要：使用工具的LLM代理大多在假设所有工具正常工作的条件下进行评估。当工具超时、返回过时一周的值，或在部署中其描述被污染时，开发者需要一种可控的方式复现故障、测试修复，并在部署前确认修复有效。我们提出AgentCheck，一个开源Web工作台，将MCP服务器转变为干预界面。AgentCheck让代理使用真实工具运行并记录每个工具响应，然后使用故障（12种类型）注入器扰动响应后重新运行代理。匹配的工具调用从缓存重放，后续工具调用在代理偏离后实时进行。这产生了一个复现-干预-确认循环：开发者切换缓解措施，对相同故障重新运行，并观察故障是否消失。评分分为两部分：确定性通过/失败规则，以及用于解释性标签的LLM评判器，经人工标注验证。在五个代理中，最佳者通过了105/120个场景，最弱者仅77个。故障通常是静默的、自信地使用错误的工具输出，而非崩溃。在最弱的代理上，重试缓解措施将超时错误故障的成功率从低至30%提升到100%，而过时数据故障无论采用何种缓解措施，成功率仍保持在每10个中约3-4个。AgentCheck使这些故障模式在部署前可复现、可比较、可验证。

Original abstract: Tool-using LLM agents are mostly evaluated assuming all tools work. When a tool times out, returns a week-stale value, or has its description poisoned in deployment, the developer needs a controlled way to reproduce the failure, test a fix, and confirm the fix worked before deployment. We present AgentCheck, an open-source web workbench that turns an MCP server into an intervention surface. AgentCheck runs an agent against its real tools and records every tool response, then re-runs the agent with the response perturbed by a fault (12 types) injector. Matching tool calls are replayed from cache, and later tool calls go live after the agent diverges. This yields a reproduce-intervene-confirm loop: the developer toggles a mitigation, re-runs against the identical fault, and sees if the failure goes away. Scoring has two parts: deterministic pass/fail rules, plus an LLM judge for interpretive labels, validated against human annotations. Across five agents, the best passes 105/120 scenarios and the weakest only 77. The failures are usually silent, confident use of incorrect tool outputs rather than crashes. On the weakest agent, a retry mitigation raises success on timeout error faults from as few as 30% of cases to 100%, whereas stale-data faults remain near 3-4 of 10 regardless of the mitigation. AgentCheck makes these failure modes reproducible, comparable, and verifiable before deployment.

</details>


### [4] [Know Before Fix: QA-Driven Repository Knowledge Acquisition for Software Issue Resolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11111v1)
*Haotian Lin,Silin Chen,Xiaodong Gu,Yuling Shi,Chengxi Pan,Jiaqi Ge,Mengfan Li,Jianghong Huang,Mengchieh Chuang,Beijun Shen,Haibing Guan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ACQUIRE通过显式问答获取仓库知识，提升LLM编码智能体在软件问题修复中的准确性，在SWE-bench上Pass@1提升达4.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM编码智能体因仓库理解不足导致事实错误，而修复前探索策略未能识别知识差距，提供不精确上下文。

Method: 提出ACQUIRE框架，分两阶段：第一阶段提问者与回答者协作获取结构化QA知识；第二阶段解决者利用该知识生成补丁。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上，ACQUIRE的Pass@1比代表性修复前方法提升最多4.4个百分点，且额外成本和时间适中。

Conclusion: 将隐式知识差距显式化为可靠理解，能有效提升修复准确性和效率。

中文摘要：基于LLM的编码智能体在自动化软件问题解决方面取得了显著进展，但它们仍然非常容易因对仓库理解不足而产生事实性错误。最近的方法试图通过修复前的仓库探索来缓解这一限制；然而，它们的修复驱动策略在探索仓库时没有识别智能体的知识差距，往往产生不精确的上下文，无法弥合潜在的理解缺陷。在本文中，我们提出了ACQUIRE，一个基于问答（QA）的软件问题解决框架。模拟经验丰富的开发人员在尝试修复之前先理解不熟悉代码的方式，ACQUIRE在修复之前明确获取仓库知识。该框架通过两个阶段将知识获取与补丁生成解耦：在第一阶段，提问者和回答者协作获取结构化的仓库知识，其中提问者提出有针对性的问题，回答者通过自主探索生成基于证据的回答；在第二阶段，解决者利用得到的QA知识生成有根据的补丁。通过将隐式的知识差距转化为显式的、事实可靠的理解，ACQUIRE加速了知识密集型的修复阶段，并实现了更准确的解决。在SWE-bench Verified上的实验表明，ACQUIRE始终优于代表性的修复前方法，在适度的额外成本和时间下，Pass@1提高了最多4.4个百分点。

Original abstract: LLM-based coding agents have significantly advanced automated software issue resolution, yet they remain highly prone to factual errors caused by insufficient repository understanding. Recent methods attempt to mitigate this limitation through pre-repair repository exploration; however, their fix-driven strategies explore repositories without identifying the agent's knowledge gaps, often yielding imprecise context that fails to bridge the underlying understanding deficit. In this paper, we propose ACQUIRE, a QA-driven framework for software issue resolution. Mirroring how experienced developers first comprehend unfamiliar code before attempting a fix, ACQUIRE explicitly acquires repository knowledge prior to repair. The framework decouples knowledge acquisition from patch generation through two stages: in the first stage, a Questioner and an Answerer collaborate to acquire structured repository knowledge, where the Questioner poses targeted questions and the Answerer produces evidence-grounded answers through autonomous exploration; in the second stage, the Resolver leverages the resulting QA knowledge to generate informed patches. By transforming implicit knowledge gaps into explicit, factually reliable understanding, ACQUIRE accelerates knowledge-intensive repair stages and enables more accurate resolution. Experiments on SWE-bench Verified demonstrate that ACQUIRE consistently outperforms representative pre-repair methods, raising Pass@1 by up to 4.4 percentage points with modest additional cost and time.

</details>


### [5] [Inference Economics of Enterprise Coding Agents: A Case Study of Cloud vs. On-Premise LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13080v1)
*Sheng-Wei Peng,Yi-Hsun Lin,Yi-Pei Lee*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过纵向案例研究对比API模型与本地量化模型，发现提示缓存大幅降低API成本，但本地模型缺陷修复负担更高；共享GPU分配下本地部署节省TCO，但牺牲开发者体验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主编码智能体在API模型（强推理、高成本）与本地模型（低成本、数据主权、弱推理）之间存在权衡，需要量化评估实际成本和代码质量差异。

Method: 单开发者非随机化纵向案例研究，在连续两个28天周期内对比API配置（Claude Opus 4.7/4.8 + Claude Code）和本地配置（GLM-5.1/5.2 + Opencode，NVFP4量化，Blackwell硬件），分析LLM遥测和Git历史。

Result: 提示缓存（命中率99.3%）将API实际成本降至每百万令牌0.57美元，低于共享本地分片的2.83美元；本地配置的修复提交比率（74.9%）远高于API（45.9%），每个难度层级修复几率高2.6-4.9倍；共享GPU分配下本地部署节省40.1% TCO，但专用预留成本高43.8%；共享分配下主要代价是开发者体验下降。

Conclusion: 本地部署在共享资源下可节省总拥有成本，但会显著增加缺陷修复负担并损害开发者体验；混合路由网关在成本与质量间存在权衡，无法完全优于纯API基线。

中文摘要：自主编码智能体迫使工程组织在基于API的前沿模型（强推理能力，高令牌成本）和本地量化开放权重模型（承诺低边际成本扩展和数据主权，但推理保真度有所损失）之间做出选择。我们通过一项在单个开发者、非随机化的纵向案例研究中研究这一权衡，该研究在连续两个28天周期内针对生产环境单体仓库进行：基于API的Claude Opus 4.7/4.8配置（使用Claude Code）与基于本地的GLM-5.1/5.2配置（使用Opencode，量化至NVFP4，运行于NVIDIA Blackwell硬件）。通过分析LLM遥测数据和Git历史，我们发现提示缓存（命中率99.3%）将实际API成本降低了88.6%，降至每百万令牌0.57美元的有效成本——甚至低于共享本地分片的摊销单位成本2.83美元（一个依赖于利用率的反转；实际总支出和总拥有成本（TCO）才是稳健的指标）。在可比的总代码变更量下，本地配置与更高的缺陷修复负担相关：修复提交比率（FCR）为74.9%对比45.9%，在每个难度层级内，提交为修复的几率高出2.6至4.9倍（Mantel-Haenszel OR = 3.61）。在台湾市场参数和对称劳动力模型下，本地部署在共享GPU分配下仍节省了40.1%的真实TCO，而专用预留比缓存API成本高出43.8%。在共享分配下，真正的代价不是金钱，而是可衡量的开发者体验负担——时间戳指标显示更多工作陷入调试循环且提交节奏较慢——离线回放显示混合路由网关沿着成本-质量前沿在缺陷率和基础设施节省之间进行权衡，而非主导纯API基线。

Original abstract: Autonomous coding agents force engineering organizations to choose between API-based frontier models -- strong reasoning at high token cost -- and on-premise quantized open-weights models, which promise low-marginal-cost scaling and data sovereignty at some loss of reasoning fidelity. We study this trade-off through a single-developer, non-randomized longitudinal case study over two contiguous 28-day periods on a production monorepo: an API-based Claude Opus 4.7/4.8 configuration using Claude Code versus an on-premise GLM-5.1/5.2 configuration using Opencode, quantized to NVFP4, on NVIDIA Blackwell hardware. Analyzing LLM telemetry and Git history, we find that prompt caching (99.3% hit rate) cuts realized API cost by 88.6% to an effective \$0.57 per million tokens -- below even the \$2.83 amortized unit cost of the shared on-premise slice (a utilization-dependent inversion; total realized spend and total cost of ownership (TCO) are the robust quantities). At comparable gross code churn, the local configuration was associated with a far higher defect-repair burden: a Fix Commit Ratio (FCR) of 74.9% versus 45.9%, with the odds of a commit being a repair 2.6 to 4.9 times higher within every difficulty tier (Mantel-Haenszel OR = 3.61). Under Taiwan-market parameters and a symmetric labor model, on-premise deployment nonetheless saves 40.1% of true TCO under shared GPU allocation, whereas dedicated reservation costs 43.8% more than the cached API. Under shared allocation, the genuine penalty is not monetary but a measurable developer-experience burden -- timestamp indicators show more work trapped in debugging spirals and a slower commit cadence -- and an offline replay shows hybrid routing gateways trade defect rate for infrastructure savings along a cost-quality frontier rather than dominate the pure-API baseline.

</details>


### [6] [RepTran: Search-Based Repair of Transformer Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11193v2)
*Yuta Ishimoto,Paolo Arcaini,Fuyuki Ishikawa,Masanari Kondo,Naoyasu Ubayashi,Yasutaka Kamei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: RepTran是一种基于搜索的Transformer模型修复方法，针对前馈网络，通过结合方差和双向分数识别可疑权重并用差分进化优化，在18个基准上平均修复率达74.7%，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型在AI软件中广泛集成，但其异常行为缺乏有效的修复方法，现有DNN修复方法忽略了Transformer特定结构。

Method: 提出RepTran，针对Transformer的前馈网络，使用方差分数和双向分数识别可疑权重，并通过差分进化迭代优化这些权重。

Result: 在18个从CIFAR-100和Tiny-ImageNet构建的故障基准上，RepTran平均修复率74.7%，统计上优于随机选择、Arachne和ArachneW。

Conclusion: RepTran能有效修复Transformer模型，提升AI赋能软件的可靠性。

中文摘要：为了确保AI赋能软件的整体质量，不仅需要测试和修复传统软件组件，还需要处理AI组件。在AI组件中，Transformer模型越来越多地集成到软件系统中，这使其异常行为变得至关重要。尽管软件工程领域的先前工作提出了深度神经网络（DNN）修复方法，但大多数忽略了Transformer特定的结构。我们提出了RepTran，一种基于搜索的Transformer模型修复方法。它针对其前馈网络（FFN），这些网络在架构中起着核心作用。RepTran通过结合两种类型的分数来识别可疑权重：基于方差的神经元分数和现有的双向分数。然后，它使用差分进化迭代优化这些权重。我们的评估包括从CIFAR-100和Tiny-ImageNet构建的18个故障基准。我们将RepTran与三个基线进行比较：随机权重选择、Arachne（一种最先进的DNN修复方法）以及ArachneW（使Arachne能够控制所选权重的数量）。RepTran实现了平均修复率74.7%，在所有基准测试中统计上优于随机选择和Arachne。效应量分析显示，无论所选权重的数量如何，RepTran的修复率都高于ArachneW。这些结果表明，RepTran对于提高AI赋能软件的可靠性是有效的。

Original abstract: To ensure the overall quality of AI-enabled software, not only traditional software components but also AI components need to be tested and repaired. Among AI components, Transformer models are increasingly integrated into software systems, which makes their misbehaviors critical. Although prior work in the software engineering community has proposed deep neural network (DNN) repair methods, most overlook Transformer-specific structures. We propose RepTran, a search-based repair method for Transformer models. It targets their feed-forward networks (FFNs), which play a central role in the architecture. RepTran identifies suspicious weights by combining two types of scores: a variance-based neuron score and an existing bidirectional score. It then iteratively optimizes these weights using differential evolution. Our evaluation includes 18 fault benchmarks constructed from CIFAR-100 and Tiny-ImageNet. We compare RepTran against three baselines: random weight selection, Arachne (a state-of-the-art DNN repair method), and ArachneW, which enables Arachne to control the number of selected weights. RepTran achieved an average repair rate of 74.7%, statistically outperforming random selection and Arachne across all benchmarks. Effect size analysis revealed that RepTran achieved higher repair rates than ArachneW regardless of the number of selected weights. These results suggest that RepTran is effective for enhancing the reliability of AI-enabled software.

</details>


### [7] [An Empirical Study for Android-to-OpenHarmony GUI Test Migration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11245v2)
*Yakun Zhang,Xinjia Chen,Yiyun Chen,Yuxia Zhang,Mingyi Zhou,Xiang Gao,Shaokun Zhang,Li Li,Yunming Ye*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次系统研究Android到OpenHarmony的GUI测试迁移，构建ATH Benchmark数据集，评估两种方法发现成功率低（15%-26%），分析原因为OpenHarmony特性，提出ITeM-HM方法将成功率提升至81%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 减少从Android到OpenHarmony应用测试的工程工作量，现有研究缺乏针对OpenHarmony的解决方案和系统评估。

Method: 构建ATH Benchmark数据集（36个商业应用+108个测试用例），选取并适配ReSPlay和ITeM两种方法，从测试性能、失败原因、系统特性影响三方面评估，基于分析提出ITeM-HM增强方法。

Result: ReSPlay成功率15%，ITeM成功率26%；ITeM-HM成功率81%，相对提升214%。

Conclusion: 现有迁移方法在OpenHarmony上效果差，通过融合系统特性可显著提升成功率。

中文摘要：为了减少将应用程序从Android迁移到OpenHarmony所需的大量工程工作，迁移现有的GUI测试用例已成为一个关键问题。然而，目前的研究既没有提出针对OpenHarmony的解决方案，也没有对迁移方法在该系统上进行系统评估，使得开发者在实践中缺乏经验指导。在本文中，我们首次对从Android到OpenHarmony的测试迁移进行了系统的实证研究。具体来说，我们首先构建了一个名为ATH Benchmark的数据集，包含36个商业应用（平均下载量超过90亿次）和108个手动设计的测试用例。其次，我们选择了两种最先进的测试迁移方法（即ReSPlay和ITeM），并调整这两种方法使其能够在OpenHarmony上运行。第三，我们利用上述基础设施从三个角度评估这两种方法：测试性能、失败的根本原因以及OpenHarmony特性的影响。我们的结果表明，在Android到OpenHarmony场景中，现有的测试迁移方法效果较差（ReSPlay成功率15%，ITeM成功率26%）。通过对失败案例的深入分析，我们发现测试性能主要受到OpenHarmony特定特性的阻碍，包括技术架构差异和独特的生态系统特征。利用这些发现，我们提出了一种基于ITeM的增强方法，称为ITeM-HM，它融合了特定的OpenHarmony系统特性。结果，ITeM-HM相对于原始ITeM实现了214%的成功率相对提升（从26%提升到81%）。

Original abstract: To reduce the substantial engineering effort required to test the corresponding applications from Android to OpenHarmony, migrating existing GUI test cases has become a critical problem. However, current research neither proposes solutions tailored for OpenHarmony nor provides a systematic evaluation of migration approaches on this system, leaving developers with limited empirical guidance in practice. In this paper, we present the first systematic empirical study of test migration from Android to OpenHarmony. Specifically, we first construct a dataset referred to as the ATH Benchmark, comprising 36 commercial applications with an average of over 9 billion downloads, along with 108 manually designed test cases. Second, we select two state-of-the-art test migration approaches (i.e., ReSPlay and ITeM) and adapt these two approaches to enable their execution on OpenHarmony. Third, we use the preceding infrastructure to evaluate these two approaches from three perspectives, including testing performance, root causes of failures, and the impact of OpenHarmony characteristics. Our results reveal that existing test migration approaches are less effective (15% success-rate on ReSPlay and 26% success-rate on ITeM) in Android-to-OpenHarmony scenarios. Through an in-depth analysis of failed cases, we identify that test performance is primarily hindered by OpenHarmony-specific characteristics, including technical architecture differences and unique ecosystem traits. Utilizing these findings, we propose an enhanced approach based on ITeM, referred as ITeM-HM, which incorporates specific OpenHarmony system features. As a result, ITeM-HM successfully achieves a 214% success-rate relative improvement over the original ITeM (from 26% to 81%).

</details>


### [8] [Hidden or Formal Architects: Understanding Who Makes Architectural Decisions in Practice](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11251v1)
*Klara Borowa,Dominik Nowak,Mikołaj Nowak*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 该研究发现架构决策通常由非正式架构师做出，正式架构师仅在大型公司和团队中被视为必要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别实践中谁做出架构决策以及何时需要正式架构师，因为并非所有公司都有正式架构师。

Method: 对来自不同公司的54名参与者进行问卷调查，并进行七次后续访谈。

Result: 架构决策通常由没有正式架构师头衔的个人做出；正式架构师主要在大型公司和大型团队中被认为必不可少。

Conclusion: 许多参与架构决策制定的实践者可能被先前关注正式架构师的研究所忽略。

中文摘要：软件架构的实证研究有时会关注那些拥有正式软件架构师头衔的个人。然而，并非所有公司都有担任此类角色的员工。尽管没有正式架构师，所有系统都有架构，并且必须有实践者做出架构决策。本研究旨在识别在实践中谁做出架构决策，以及在何种环境中正式架构师的存在被认为是必要的。本研究采用了一种方法，包括对来自不同公司的54名参与者进行问卷调查和七次后续访谈。研究结果表明，架构决策往往由没有正式架构师头衔的个人做出。正式架构师主要被认为在大型公司和大型团队中必不可少。本研究的结果显示，许多参与架构决策制定的实践者可能被先前的研究忽略了，特别是那些关注正式架构师的研究。

Original abstract: Empirical research on software architecture sometimes focuses on individuals holding the formal title of software architect. However, not all companies have individuals hired in such roles. Despite no formal architects, all systems have architectures, and there must be practitioners making the architectural decisions. This study aims to identify who, in practice, makes architectural decisions and in what environments the existence of a formal architect is perceived as necessary. This research employed a method consisting of a questionnaire with 54 participants from different companies and seven follow-up interviews. The findings indicate that architectural decisions are often made by individuals without a formal architect title. A formal architect is perceived as essential mainly in large companies and large teams. The results of this study show that many practitioners taking part in ADM may have been omitted by previous research, particularly if it focused on formal architects.

### [9] [Extending Decision Maps for Sustainable Safety and Security in Self-Adaptive Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11274v1)
*Marco Stadler,Wesley K. G. Assunção,Michael Vierhauser,Iris Groher,Michael Riegler,Johannes Sametinger*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 扩展Decision Maps符号以支持安全性和安保建模，并通过真实案例验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Decision Maps符号缺乏对安全性和安保问题的充分建模支持，限制了其在可持续性驱动的自适应系统中的应用。

Method: 引入额外建模维度处理安全事件，并采用细粒度分治方法从不同时间安保视角（安保模式）进行建模。

Result: 扩展后的符号在行业真实用例中更准确地捕获安全性和安保场景，并为自适应生命周期提供整体支持。

Conclusion: 该建模符号能有效提升对安全性和安保场景的建模能力，适用于可持续性驱动的自适应系统开发。

中文摘要：可持续性是指系统维持其功能并长期存在的能力。因此，可持续性是软件系统（包括自适应系统（SASs））高度期望的属性。自适应系统可以在运行时改变（适应）其行为，以在外部或内部影响下继续实现其目标。自适应系统的预期长期系统行为可以通过一种称为决策图（DMs）的可持续性驱动的视觉建模符号来表达。尽管决策图已被证明是有用的，但它们缺乏对安全性和安保问题的充分建模支持。我们通过扩展当前用于可持续性驱动的自适应系统建模的符号来解决这一限制，以更好地适应安全性和安保场景的独特特征。首先，我们引入了一个额外的建模维度来考虑安全事件。其次，我们采用一种细粒度的分治方法，从不同的时间安保视角（“安保模式”）进行建模，以解决安保问题。我们在行业合作伙伴提供的真实用例场景中采用扩展的决策图符号，以评估其对实践者的可行性和适用性。我们的结果表明，我们的建模符号有助于更准确地捕获安保和安全场景，并为自适应生命周期阶段提供整体支持。

Original abstract: Sustainability refers to a system's ability to maintain its functionality and endure over time. Hence, sustainability is a highly desirable property of software systems, including Self-Adaptive Systems (SASs). SASs can change (adapt) their behavior at runtime to continue achieving their objectives despite external or internal impacts. SASs' intended long-term system behavior can be expressed through a sustainability-driven visual modeling notation called Decision Maps (DMs). Although DMs have been proven helpful, they lack adequate modeling support for safety and security concerns. We address this limitation by extending the current notation for sustainability-driven modeling of SASs to better accommodate the unique characteristics of safety and security scenarios. First, we introduce an additional modeling dimension to account for safety incidents. Second, we adopt a fine-grained divide-and-conquer approach, modeling from distinct temporal security viewpoints ("security modes") to address security. We employ the extended DM notation in a real-world use case scenario provided by our industry partner to assess its feasibility and suitability for practitioners. Our results indicate that our modeling notation helps capture security and safety scenarios more accurately and provides holistic support for the self-adaptation life cycle phases.

### [10] [FlowArk: Boosting Agentic Data-flow Analysis for Android Apps via Context-Aware Knowledge Reuse](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11308v1)
*Yiming Zhang,Jiangrong Wu,Yuhong Nan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: FlowArk通过重用已完成分析的知识，减少了批处理数据流分析中的API成本，提高了效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在批处理数据流分析中，不同污点源的分析实例重复分析共享代码片段，造成不必要的API成本，限制了可扩展性。

Method: 提出FlowArk，将完成的分析历史提炼为可重用知识候选，打包成可匹配的知识条目，并注入到后续代理实例的上下文中。

Result: 在4,685个任务上，与标准OpenCode相比，API成本降低26.83%，在100美元预算下多完成36.66%的任务（1,060 vs. 776）。

Conclusion: FlowArk能有效降低批处理数据流分析的重新分析成本，同时保持分析质量。

中文摘要：数据流分析是安卓应用隐私和安全审计的基础。最近的编码代理可以通过搜索、阅读和推理仓库代码来协助非平凡的源到源数据流分析任务。然而，当这些任务作为批处理工作负载执行时，当前的代理分析设置会 incur 大量的重新分析成本。分配给不同污点源的代理实例可能会检查共享的代码片段，因为目标应用中的代码重用会导致不同数据流路径汇聚到共享的程序逻辑上。由于这些代理实例是上下文隔离的，批处理中可能会重复分析这些共享代码片段，不必要地消耗API预算并限制可扩展性。我们提出FlowArk，一个知识重用系统，通过使已完成分析的知识可用于后续代理实例，来减少批处理代理数据流分析中的重新分析成本。具体来说，FlowArk将完成的分析历史提炼为可重用的知识候选，将这些候选打包为可匹配的知识条目，并将匹配的条目注入到后续代理实例的上下文中。我们在OpenCode上实现了FlowArk，并在来自50个开源安卓应用的4,685个源到源数据流分析任务上进行了评估。与标准OpenCode相比，启用FlowArk的OpenCode保持了相当的分析质量，同时将端到端API成本降低了26.83%。此外，在100美元的预算下，FlowArk完成了36.66%更多的任务（1,060 vs. 776）。

Original abstract: Data-flow analysis is foundational to Android app privacy and security auditing. Recent coding agents can assist with non-trivial source-to-sink data-flow analysis tasks by searching, reading, and reasoning over repository code. However, when these tasks are executed as a batch workload, current agentic analysis setups incur substantial re-analysis cost. Agent instances assigned to different taint sources may inspect shared code fragments, because code reuse in the target app can cause different data-flow paths to converge on shared program logic. Since these agent instances are context-isolated, analysis of these shared code fragments can be repeated within a batch, unnecessarily consuming API budget and limiting scalability.
  We propose FlowArk, a knowledge-reuse system that reduces re-analysis cost in batch agentic data-flow analysis by making knowledge from completed analyses available to later agent instances. Specifically, FlowArk distills completed analysis histories into reusable knowledge candidates, packages these candidates into matchable knowledge entries, and injects matched entries into a later agent instance's context. We implement FlowArk on OpenCode and evaluate it on 4,685 source-to-sink data-flow analysis tasks from 50 open-source Android apps. Compared with standard OpenCode, FlowArk-enabled OpenCode maintains comparable analysis quality while reducing end-to-end API cost by 26.83%. In addition, under a USD 100 budget, FlowArk completes 36.66% more tasks (1,060 vs. 776).

</details>


### [11] [Fail-Aware and Explainable Test Oracle Prediction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11342v1)
*Yue Zhao,Binish Tanveer,Jelena Zdravkovic*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出FOCAL，一个基于代码LLM的判别式预言预测器，通过直接预测测试前缀通过/失败来替代断言生成，显著提升未见项目上的故障检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试断言生成方法即使语法正确也常无法有效发现错误，需要一种不依赖断言生成而是直接预测测试结果的方法。

Method: FOCAL利用标注的测试前缀-方法对训练，采用强调失败案例的损失函数，并基于语句级行为证据进行预测。

Result: 在故障检测基准和自动化测试生成工件上，FOCAL在训练分布内准确度高，在未见项目上故障检测性能显著优于SEER，且高亮语句通过行为解释验证。

Conclusion: 故障感知的判别式预言预测可补充现有测试方法，将测试前缀转化为带故障感知预言的执行测试，有望暴露更多语义失败。

中文摘要：尽管测试预言在故障检测中起着核心作用，但其有效构建仍具有挑战性。最近基于学习的方法通过自动生成测试断言来应对这一挑战，但即使语法正确，它们通常也无法有效揭示错误。本研究没有生成断言，而是探索了一种不同的方法：训练模型直接预测给定的测试前缀是否通过或失败。我们提出了FOCAL，一种基于代码LLM的判别式预言预测器。它从标注的测试前缀与被测方法对中学习，采用在训练中强调失败案例的损失函数，并将其预测基于语句级别的行为证据。与基线方法SEER相比，我们在未见项目上的失败案例性能显著提升，并提供了更丰富的解释。针对故障检测基准和自动化测试生成工件的初步评估表明，我们的方法在其训练分布内具有高准确性，并在先前判别式预言失效的未见项目上显著提高了故障检测能力。此外，高亮的语句得到了行为解释检查的支持。这些早期结果表明，故障感知的判别式预言预测可以补充现有方法，如模糊测试、基于搜索的测试和基于LLM的测试生成。这些技术大规模生成测试前缀，但通常缺乏面向故障的预言。未来工作中，FOCAL可以获取生成的测试前缀并附加故障感知的预测预言，从而将高容量输入生成转化为更有可能暴露语义失败的可执行测试。

Original abstract: Despite their central role in fault detection, test oracles remain challenging to construct effectively. Recent learning based methods address this challenge by automatically generating test assertions, yet even if syntactically correct, they are often ineffective in revealing bugs. Rather than generating assertions, this study explores a different approach by training a model to directly predict whether a given test prefix passes or fails. We present FOCAL, an emerging code LLM-based discriminative oracle predictor. It learns from labeled pairs of test prefixes and methods under test, employs losses that emphasize failing cases during training, and grounds its predictions in statement level behavioral evidence. Compared with the baseline method SEER, we substantially improve performance on failing cases for unseen projects and provide richer explanations. A preliminary evaluation on fault-detection benchmarks and automated test-generation artifacts shows that our approach is highly accurate within its training distribution and substantially improves failure detection on previously unseen projects where prior discriminative oracles collapse. Moreover, the highlighted statements are supported by behavioral explanation checks. These early results suggest that fail-aware discriminative oracle prediction can complement existing approaches such as fuzzing, search-based testing, and LLM-based test generation. These techniques produce test prefixes at scale but often lack fault oriented oracles. In future work, FOCAL could take generated test prefixes and attach fault-aware predicted oracles to them, turning high-volume input generation into executable tests that are more likely to expose semantic failures.

</details>


### [12] [Understanding the Impact of AI Code Assistants on Security API Usage: An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11348v1)
*Zahra Mousavi,Chadni Islam,M. Ali Babar,Alsharif Abuadbba,Kristen Moore*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过44名开发者的实验发现，GitHub Copilot提高了功能正确性但未显著改善安全API使用，开发者常忽视安全问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏从开发者角度探究AI助手对安全API使用的影响，需要实证证据来制定缓解策略。

Method: 对44名专业开发者进行对照实验，比较有/无GitHub Copilot辅助时完成安全API编程任务的表现。

Result: Copilot提升功能正确性并轻微减少不安全模式，但未显著提高安全API使用；开发者很少主动关注安全问题且常未发现实现仍不安全。

Conclusion: 提出增强开发者安全意识的建议，并指出未来研究方向以促进更安全的AI辅助软件开发。

中文摘要：AI代码助手正在改变软件开发，但其对软件安全的影响仍是一个主要关注点，特别是在安全API的背景下。这些API对于保护软件系统至关重要，但它们的复杂性常常导致使用不当和严重漏洞。因此，发展基于证据的理解，了解AI助手如何影响开发者对这些API的使用，对于制定有效的缓解策略至关重要。虽然少数用户研究已经考察了AI助手对软件漏洞的广泛影响，但从开发者中心的角度来看，安全API的使用仍未得到探索。本研究通过首次实证调查AI代码助手如何影响专业开发者对安全API的使用，填补了这一空白。我们进行了一项研究，有44名开发者在有和没有GitHub Copilot帮助的情况下完成安全API编程任务。我们的研究结果表明，虽然Copilot提高了功能正确性并略微减少了某些不安全模式，但它并未显著改善安全的API使用。我们还发现，开发者在与Copilot互动时很少提出安全问题，许多人没有意识到他们的最终实现仍然不安全。最后，我们提出了增强开发者安全意识的建议，并提出了未来研究的方向，以支持更安全的AI辅助软件开发。

Original abstract: AI code assistants are transforming software development, but their implications for software security remain a major concern, particularly in the context of security APIs. These APIs are critical for safeguarding software systems, yet their complexity often leads to incorrect use and serious vulnerabilities. Developing an evidence-based understanding of how AI assistants influence developers' use of these APIs is therefore essential for informing effective mitigation strategies. While a few user studies have examined the broader impact of AI assistants on software vulnerabilities, the use of security APIs remains unexplored from a developer-centered perspective. This study addresses this gap by presenting the first empirical investigation into how AI code assistants affect professional developers' use of security APIs. We conducted a study with 44 developers who completed security API programming tasks with and without GitHub Copilot assistance. Our findings show that, while Copilot improves functional correctness and marginally reduces certain insecure patterns, it does not significantly improve secure API usage. We also found that developers rarely raised security concerns when engaging with Copilot, and many did not recognize that their final implementations remained insecure. Finally, we offer recommendations for enhancing security awareness among developers and propose future research directions to support safer AI-assisted software development.

</details>


### [13] [Predicting Program Comprehension with Foundation Models of Human Cognition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11372v2)
*Yannick Lehmen,Marvin Wyrich,Anna-Maria Maurer,Norman Peitek,Sven Apel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Centaur，一个基于一般心理学实验数据训练的基础模型，在程序理解任务中比基础模型Llama 3.1更准确地预测人类响应，且更少依赖历史信息，表明心理学行为模式可迁移到软件工程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有程序理解预测方法要么精度低要么难以规模化，心理学研究显示通过大规模行为数据学习认知规律可捕捉人类行为，因此探索将其应用于软件工程。

Method: 评估Centaur（基于160项心理学实验训练）在9个程序理解研究上的表现，与Llama 3.1比较，并进行消融研究分析不同信息源贡献。

Result: Centaur比Llama 3.1更接近人类响应模式，对先前试验和响应的依赖更少，更多受益于任务相关信息。

Conclusion: 从一般心理学数据习得的行为模式可迁移到程序理解，为使用人类认知基础模型建模开发者行为提供支持。

中文摘要：软件工程依赖于开发者理解代码的能力，然而尽管经过数十年的研究，预测他们如何做到这一点仍然是一个开放的挑战。现有方法要么依赖限制准确性的简化代理指标，要么需要难以扩展和实际应用的非平凡测量及复杂实验设置。相比之下，心理学的最新研究提出了另一种视角：不是直接建模特定任务的现象，而是通过从大规模行为数据中学习的认知规律来捕捉人类行为。这一观点将复杂的人类行为视为底层认知过程的可观察结果，这些过程在任务和领域中一致地表现出来。在本文中，我们在程序理解的背景下探索了这一视角。我们评估了Centaur，一个在160项一般心理学实验上训练的基础模型，在9项先前发布的程序理解研究上的表现。我们评估其预测响应分布与人类响应数据的一致性，并将Centaur的性能与其基础模型Llama 3.1进行比较。为了更好地理解其性能来源，我们进行了消融研究，以隔离不同信息来源的贡献，例如代码工件、任务相关上下文以及先前的试验和参与者响应。简而言之，我们发现Centaur比其基础模型更接近人类响应模式，对先前试验和响应信息的依赖显著减少，并且从任务相关信息中获益更多。这些发现表明，从一般心理学数据中学到的行为模式可以迁移到复杂的软件工程任务（如程序理解）中。更广泛地说，它们指向了人类认知基础模型作为软件工程中建模开发者行为的基础。

Original abstract: Software engineering depends on the ability of developers to understand code, yet predicting how they do so remains an open challenge despite decades of research. Existing approaches rely either on simplified proxy measures that limit accuracy or on non-trivial measurements requiring elaborate experimental setups that are difficult to scale and apply in practice. In contrast, recent work in psychology suggests an alternative perspective: Instead of modeling task-specific phenomena directly, human behavior can be captured through cognitive regularities learned from large-scale behavioral data. This idea treats complex human behavior as the observable outcome of underlying cognitive processes that manifest consistently across tasks and domains. In this paper, we explore this perspective in the context of program comprehension. We evaluate Centaur, a foundation model trained on 160 general psychological experiments, on 9 previously published program-comprehension studies. We assess how well its predicted response distributions align with human response data and compare Centaur's performance to its base model, Llama 3.1. To better understand the source of its performance, we conduct ablation studies to isolate the contribution of different sources of information, such as the code artifacts, task-related context, and prior trials and participant responses. In a nutshell, we find that Centaur more closely aligns with human response patterns than its base model, is significantly less reliant on information from prior trials and responses, and benefits more from task-related information. These findings suggest that behavioral patterns learned from general psychological data can transfer to complex software engineering tasks such as program comprehension. More broadly, they point toward foundation models of human cognition as a basis for modeling developer behavior in software engineering.

### [14] [From GUI Tests to Conversational Interaction: A New Perspective on App-Specific Voice Assistants](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11387v1)
*Xue Qin,Sumesh Surendran Letha*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出利用LLM将GUI测试代码转化为应用特定的语音助手，以降低开发成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语音助手是系统级服务，与应用特定行为对齐不佳，导致开发者需手动重写应用逻辑，成本高。

Method: 利用LLM将GUI测试代码（行为保持、可执行规范）重新解释为对话交互的桥梁，转化为语音意图、能力描述和行动计划等VA工件。

Result: 在五个开源应用上的初步实验表明，GUI测试代码可重用，合成应用特定语音助手。

Conclusion: GUI测试代码可超越测试用途，为自动构建应用特定语音助手提供新途径，促进软件测试、交互设计与LLM自动化的交叉研究。

中文摘要：语音助手已广泛应用于移动平台，但大多数被设计为系统级服务，与应用特定的行为对齐不佳。因此，在应用层面启用语音交互需要开发者手动重新实现应用逻辑，导致高昂的开发与维护成本。我们提出了一种基于LLM的方法，通过重新利用GUI测试代码（这些代码编码了应用功能的行为保持、可执行规范）来自动开发应用特定的语音助手。在本文中，我们提出了一种视角，即大型语言模型将GUI测试重新解释为应用行为与对话交互之间的桥梁。通过将测试方法转化为应用特定的VA工件，如语音意图、能力描述和可执行行动计划，我们的方法将语音助手直接基于现有的应用逻辑而非外部规范。我们通过Android上的研究原型AppVA展示了这一愿景。我们在五个开源应用上的初步结果表明，GUI测试代码可以在测试之外重复利用，实现应用特定语音助手的合成，并突出了一个涉及软件测试、交互设计和LLM驱动的自动化的交叉研究领域。

Original abstract: Voice assistants are widely deployed on mobile platforms, yet most are designed as system-level services that remain poorly aligned with application-specific behavior. As a result, enabling voice interaction at the app level requires developers to manually reimplement application logic, leading to high development and maintenance costs.
  We propose an LLM-driven approach to automating the development of app-specific voice assistants by repurposing GUI test code, which encodes behavior-preserving, executable specifications of application functionality. In this paper, we present a perspective in which large language models reinterpret GUI tests as bridges between application behavior and conversational interaction. By transforming test methods into app-specific VA artifacts, such as voice intents, capability descriptions, and executable action plans, our approach grounds voice assistants directly in existing application logic rather than external specifications.
  We illustrate this vision through AppVA, a research prototype on Android. Our preliminary results across five open-source applications suggest that GUI test code can be reused beyond testing, enabling the synthesis of app-specific voice assistants and highlighting a broader research direction at the intersection of software testing, interaction design, and LLM-enabled automation.

### [15] [TerraRepair: A Tool-Grounded LLM Agent for Infrastructure-as-Code Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11390v1)
*Minase Mekete Mengistu,Juri Di Rocco,Phuong T. Nguyen,Davide Di Ruscio*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TerraRepair，一种工具接地的LLM代理，用于Terraform配置修复，在修复时检索依赖、查询提供者模式并重新扫描，缺失上下文时升级而非编造修复；实验表明修复率显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM修复方法可能产生幻觉或无效修复，且缺乏部署上下文；工具接地可以提升修复可靠性和真实性。

Method: 开发TerraRepair，集成依赖检索、提供者模式查询和扫描器重运行，并在缺少上下文时进行结构化升级。

Result: 在AWS基准上，Checkov验证修复率从26.6%升至78.4%，Trivy从44.8%升至72.4%，修复多数投票正确。

Conclusion: 工具接地显著提升LLM修复的扫描验证率，但部署上下文缺失仍是实现完全自主的主要障碍。

中文摘要：背景：基础设施即代码（IaC）扫描器可在部署前检测到Terraform及其他IaC语言中的云配置错误，但修复标记的配置仍需大量人工操作。近期基于大规模语言模型（LLM）的修复方法可以修复部分发现，但可能幻觉出不支持的构造或在不修复问题的情况下压制警告。目标：我们研究工具接地（tool grounding）能否改善基于LLM的Terraform修复，以及在缺乏所需部署特定上下文时，何时应升级问题。方法：我们提出TerraRepair，一个针对Terraform修复的工具接地LLM代理原型，具有结构化升级机制。TerraRepair从Terraform引用中检索依赖上下文，查询已安装的提供者模式，并在返回候选修复前重新运行扫描器。当所需上下文缺失时，TerraRepair会升级问题，而不是编造一个看似合理的修复。结果：我们使用两个IaC安全扫描器Checkov和Trivy，在AWS、Azure和GCP上对两个刻意存在漏洞的Terraform仓库进行了评估。在组合的AWS基准测试中，与受控的一次性基线相比，TerraRepair将经扫描器验证的修复率从26.6%提高到78.4%（Checkov），从44.8%提高到72.4%（Trivy）。其修复在多数投票协议下被标记为正确。结论：这些初步结果表明，在研究的基准测试中，工具接地可以大幅改善经扫描器验证的基于LLM的IaC修复，而缺失部署特定上下文仍是实现完全自主的主要知识边界。

Original abstract: Background: Infrastructure-as-Code (IaC) scanners detect cloud misconfigurations in Terraform and other IaC languages before deployment, but repairing the flagged configurations remains largely manual. Recent Large Language Model (LLM)-based repair approaches can repair some findings, but may hallucinate unsupported constructs or suppress warnings without fixing the issue. Aims: We study whether tool grounding can improve LLM-based Terraform repair, and when a finding should be escalated because the required deploymnet-specific context is not availble. Method: We present TerraRepair, a prototype of a tool-grounded LLM agent for Terraform repair with structured escalation. TerraRepair retrieves dependency context from Terraform references, consults the installed provider schema, and re-runs the scanner before returning a candidate repair. Then teh required context is absent, TerraRepair escalates instead of fabricating a plausible fix. Results: We evaluate our tool on two vulnerable-by-design Terraform repositories using two IaC security scanners, Checkov and Trivy, across AWS, Azure, and GCP. On the combined AWS benchmark, TerraRepair improves scanner-verified fix rates from 26.6% to 78.4% on Checkov and from 44.8% to 72.4% on Trivy, compared with a controlled one-shot baseline. It repairs are labelled as correct under a majority-vote protocol. Conclusions: These emerging results show that tool grounding can substantially improve scanner-verified LLM-based IaC repair on the studied benchmarks, while missing deployment-specific context remains the main knowledge boundary for full autonomy.

</details>


### [16] [Knowledge-Guided Synthetic Bug Feedback for LLM-Based Unit Test Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11573v1)
*Ziheng Wang,Maike Li,Chen Zhi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出将历史真实缺陷机制转化为可执行反馈目标，指导LLM生成能检测真实缺陷的单元测试，在Defects4J上优于多种基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可执行的LLM生成测试不一定能发现真实缺陷，需要利用历史真实缺陷机制来引导测试生成。

Method: 构建真实缺陷记录的结构和语义表示，检索适用于焦点方法的机制，实例化为合成缺陷，用于迭代测试增强。

Result: 在Defects4J方法级缺陷检测任务上，机制引导的合成缺陷反馈优于执行、覆盖、变异、知识和搜索基线。

Conclusion: 将真实缺陷机制组织为可检索和可执行的反馈目标，能有效引导生成测试触发缺陷输入和行为预言机。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）为单元测试生成开辟了新的机会，但可执行的测试并不一定能够发现真正的缺陷。本文研究如何将历史上的真实缺陷机制转化为可执行的反馈目标，用于基于LLM的单元测试生成。所提出的框架构建了真实缺陷记录的结构和语义表示，检索适用于焦点方法的机制，并将其实例化为合成缺陷，以指导迭代测试增强。我们在Defects4J的方法级真实缺陷检测任务上评估了该方法，并表明机制引导的合成缺陷反馈在真实缺陷检测上优于基于执行、覆盖、变异、知识和搜索的基线。结果表明，将真实缺陷机制组织为可检索和可执行的反馈目标是引导生成的测试朝向触发缺陷的输入和行为预言机的有效方式。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have opened new opportunities for unit test generation, but executable tests do not necessarily reveal real defects. This paper studies how historical real-bug mechanisms can be transformed into executable feedback targets for LLM-based unit test generation. The proposed framework constructs structural and semantic representations of real-bug records, retrieves mechanisms applicable to a focal method, and instantiates them as synthetic bugs that guide iterative test enhancement. We evaluate the approach on method-level real-bug detection tasks from Defects4J and show that mechanism-guided synthetic-bug feedback improves real-bug detection over execution-, coverage-, mutation-, knowledge-, and search-based baselines. The results suggest that organizing real-bug mechanisms as retrievable and executable feedback targets is an effective way to guide generated tests toward bug-triggering inputs and behavioral oracles.

### [17] [ThinkLog: Leveraging Reasoning for Log Statement Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11615v1)
*Kazuki Kusama,Honglin Shu,Masanari Kondo,Tao Xiao,Yasutaka Kamei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ThinkLog通过将推理融入提示中，显著提升了LLM在日志语句生成任务上的准确性，同时降低了推理成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端日志语句生成方法精度有限，需要更准确的方法来减轻开发人员负担。

Method: 提出ThinkLog方法，将推理作为少样本示例注入提示，引导LLM进行日志插入、严重级别分配和消息生成的决策。

Result: 在9,619个Java方法上，ThinkLog达到20.55%的准确率，比最佳现有方法提高15.4%，且推理成本降低约50%。

Conclusion: 利用推理是提高端到端日志语句生成准确性的一种有效且经济高效的方式。

中文摘要：运行时日志是支持软件维护的重要信息来源。为了获得有用的日志，开发人员需要花费大量精力确定适当的日志位置、分配正确的严重级别以及编写简洁且信息丰富的消息。因此，端到端的自动化日志语句生成可以帮助减轻这一负担，先前的工作已经为此任务提出了许多方法。然而，现有方法仍显示出有限的准确性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了ThinkLog，一种基于LLM的端到端日志语句生成方法。ThinkLog的核心思想是融入推理，帮助LLM在日志插入、严重级别分配和消息生成方面做出决策，从而提高日志语句生成的准确性。ThinkLog将推理作为少样本示例注入提示中，并引导LLM生成适当的日志语句。在从公共GitHub仓库提取的9,619个Java方法上评估，ThinkLog实现了20.55%的日志语句生成准确率，相比最佳现有方法提高了15.4%。此外，这些改进是在推理成本（美元）约为最佳现有方法50%的情况下实现的。这些结果表明，利用推理是提高端到端日志语句生成准确性的一种有效且经济高效的方式。

Original abstract: Runtime logs are an important source of information that supports software maintenance. To obtain useful logs, developers spend significant effort identifying appropriate log locations, assigning correct severity levels, and writing concise yet informative messages. Therefore, end-to-end automated log statement generation can help reduce this burden, and prior work has proposed many methods for this task. However, existing methods still exhibit limited accuracy. To address this problem, we propose ThinkLog, an LLM-based end-to-end log statement generation method. The core idea of ThinkLog is to incorporate reasoning that helps LLMs make decisions about log insertion, severity level assignment, and message generation, thereby improving log statement generation accuracy. ThinkLog injects reasoning into prompts as few-shot examples and guides LLMs to generate appropriate log statements. Evaluated on 9,619 Java methods extracted from public GitHub repositories, ThinkLog achieves 20.55% log statement generation accuracy, representing a 15.4% improvement over the best existing method. Moreover, these improvements were achieved at approximately 50% of the inference cost (USD) compared to the best existing method. These results show that leveraging reasoning is an effective and cost-efficient way to improve the accuracy of end-to-end log statement generation.

### [18] [Which Optimizer, At What Budget? A Tournament of Optimizers for Search-Based SE](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11705v1)
*Kishan Kumar Ganguly,Tim Menzies*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过聚类和锦标赛比较20个优化器，发现没有绝对胜者，最佳优化器随标签预算变化，且可通过查表预测替代昂贵的锦标赛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 帮助从业者在配置系统时更好地选择优化器，解决现有指导的误导性和大量优化器选择的困难。

Method: 基于数据六个假设对20个优化器聚类，在106个软件工程优化任务上以四个标签预算进行锦标赛，并开发基于两个任务属性和标签预算的查表方法。

Result: 没有优化器能完全胜出；最佳优化器随预算迁移；查表方法在约75%的保留任务上优于或持平于事后最优。

Conclusion: 为每个领域运行锦标赛不切实际，但查表方法有效；已开源支持开放科学。

中文摘要：配置和调优现代软件是不可避免的、昂贵的且容易出错的：单个系统可能暴露数百个相互作用的选项，而评估一个设置可能意味着完整的构建或测试运行。标准的应对方法是自动优化，但可用的优化器数量庞大且不断增长。同时，一些选择优化器的指导具有误导性：例如，NSGA-II被广泛推荐，但其他算法仅需其1/20的评估次数就能达到相同结果。为了帮助从业者更好地选择工具来配置其系统，我们基于数据的六个假设对20个优化器进行了聚类。接下来，我们在106个软件工程优化任务上，在四个标记预算下（耗时超过14,000 CPU小时）对这些优化器进行了一场锦标赛。我们发现没有优化器能完全胜出。最佳优化器随预算而变化（从标记稀缺时的几何主动学习器到标记充足时的差分进化），因此在一个预算下被“加冕”的获胜者在另一个预算下可能在我们多达一半的任务上是错误的。由于CPU成本问题，为每个新领域运行这样的锦标赛是不切实际的。幸运的是，我们发现这14,000小时可以通过对两个易于获取的任务属性（加上标记预算）进行查表来替代。该表的预测在大约75%的保留任务上优于或持平于事后最优选择。为了支持开放科学，我们的锦标赛和复现包已开源供SBSE研究者和从业者使用，地址为https://github.com/KKGanguly/OptimizerTournament。

Original abstract: Configuring and tuning modern software is unavoidable, expensive, and error-prone: a single system can expose hundreds of interacting options, and scoring one setting can mean a full build or test run. The standard response is automated optimization, but the number of available optimizers is large and growing. And some of the guidance for selecting among them is misleading: NSGA-II, for example, is widely recommended, yet other algorithms reach the same results using only 1/20th as many evaluations.
  To help practitioners make better choices about tools to configure their systems, we cluster 20 optimizers, based on six assumptions about the data. Next, we run a tournament across those optimizers, using 106 SE optimization tasks at four labeling budgets (taking 14,000+ CPU hours). We find that no optimizer wins outright. The best one migrates with the budget (from a geometric active learner when labels are scarce to differential evolution when labels are plentiful) so a winner "crowned" at one budget is wrong at another on up to half our tasks.
  Running such a tournament for every new domain is impractical due to its CPU cost. Fortunately, we find that those 14,000 hours can be replaced by a table lookup over two cheap-to-obtain task attributes (plus the labeling budget). Predictions from this table tie or beat a hindsight oracle on $\approx 75%$ of held-out tasks.
  To support open science, our tournament and replication package are open-sourced for SBSE researchers and practitioners at https://github.com/KKGanguly/OptimizerTournament.

</details>


### [19] [Evaluating RE Practices for Explainability: Synthesizing Insights from Daimler Truck into an Explainable RE Framework Proposal](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11771v1)
*Umm-e- Habiba,Lucas Mauser,Jonas Fritzsch,Justus Bogner,Stefan Wagner*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过行业案例研究，揭示了现有需求工程实践在支持解释性需求方面存在概念模糊、可测试性差、验证碎片化等挑战，并提出了开发经验驱动的RE框架的愿景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管解释性对AI系统至关重要，但现有RE实践如何支持解释性需求的实证理解不足，特别是在工业环境中。

Method: 在戴姆勒卡车公司进行多阶段定性研究，涉及8名从业者，采用有声思维协议和主持组讨论，覆盖需求引出、规范和验证步骤。

Result: 发现所有步骤存在反复出现的挑战：引出阶段概念模糊、规范阶段可测试性和表达性有限、验证阶段因模糊标准和监管不确定性而碎片化。

Conclusion: 当前RE实践系统性支持解释性需求不足，需要开发经验基础的RE框架，并提供了步骤具体和跨领域挑战的实证见解。

中文摘要：解释性已成为基于AI的系统的一个关键需求，特别是在安全关键和受监管领域。尽管先前的研究提出了支持解释性的框架、模式和以用户为中心的方法，但对于现有需求工程（RE）实践如何在RE生命周期中支持解释性需求，尤其是在工业背景下，实证理解仍然有限。本文报告了一项正在进行的行业研究的初步发现，该研究调查了如何使用既定的RE技术来引出、规范和验证解释性需求。我们在戴姆勒卡车公司与八名从业者进行了一项多阶段定性研究，采用有声思维协议和主持的组讨论，涵盖了需求引出、规范和验证步骤。我们的初步分析揭示了所有步骤中反复出现的挑战，包括引出阶段的概念模糊性、规范阶段的可测试性和表达性有限，以及由于模糊标准和监管不确定性导致的碎片化验证。这些发现表明，当前的RE实践在系统性地解决解释性需求方面提供的支持有限。本文提供了针对具体步骤和跨领域挑战的实证见解，并概述了一个研究愿景，即开发一个经验基础的RE框架，用于可解释的基于AI的系统。

Original abstract: Explainability has emerged as a critical requirement for AI-based systems, particularly in safety-critical and regulated domains. Although prior research has proposed frameworks, patterns, and user-centered approaches to support explainability, there is limited empirical understanding of how existing Requirements Engineering (RE) practices support explainability requirements across the RE lifecycle, especially in an industrial context. This paper reports early findings from an ongoing industry-based study investigating how explainability requirements are elicited, specified, and validated using established RE techniques. We conducted a multi-phase qualitative study with eight practitioners at Daimler Truck, employing think-aloud protocols and moderated group discussions across requirements elicitation, specification, and validation steps. Our preliminary analysis reveals recurring challenges across all steps, including conceptual ambiguity during elicitation, limited testability and expressiveness during specification, and fragmented validation due to vague criteria and regulatory uncertainty. These findings indicate that current RE practices provide limited support to systematically address explainability requirements. The paper contributes empirical insights into step-specific and cross-cutting challenges and outlines a research vision toward developing an empirically grounded RE framework for explainable AI-based systems.

### [20] [Predicting Acceptance and Review Effort in Human and Agent Pull Requests](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12057v1)
*Kartik Ghanshyambhai Pansuriya,Ehsan Ghorbani,Deepak Singh,Eman Abdullah AlOmar*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究在PR提交时预测其接受与否及审查工作量，发现接受预测可行（F1>0.95），但审查工作量预测较难，建议作为咨询工具使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI代理和人类开发者提交更多PR，维护者需要快速识别哪些PR可能被接受或需要大量审查，以优化资源分配。

Method: 使用AIDev数据集，构建泄漏感知的预测管道，提取提交时的特征（文本、元数据、上下文等），评估多种经典机器学习模型（逻辑回归、随机森林等）。

Result: 接受预测的F1分数超过0.95（树模型），文本清晰度和元数据是主要预测因素；审查工作量预测（评论数、合并时间）效果一般。

Conclusion: 早期PR模型可辅助分类和审查优先级排序，但应作为咨询工具而非自动决策者，因为审查过程受人为因素影响较大。

中文摘要：拉取请求（PR）是现代软件仓库中审查和集成代码更改的核心机制。随着AI编码代理开始与人类开发者一起提交更多代码更改，维护者面临一个新挑战：决定哪些PR可能被接受，哪些可能需要大量的审查工作。本文研究了在PR打开时，即在审查者讨论、CI反馈或合并决定可用之前，是否能够估计这些结果。利用AIDev数据集，我们构建了一个泄漏感知的预测管道，用于人类和代理编写的PR。特征集限于提交时的信息，包括PR文本特征、元数据、仓库上下文、时间信号和轻量级差异统计。我们评估了经典机器学习模型，包括逻辑回归、随机森林、梯度提升、极端随机树和MLP，涵盖混合、仅人类、仅代理和平衡贡献者视图。我们的结果表明，从早期信号预测接受是可行的：基于树的模型F1分数超过0.95，文本清晰度和元数据是最具影响力的预测因素。审查工作量的预测则更为困难。评论数量和时间到合并仅能由提交时特征适度解释，表明审查者可用性、项目工作流和团队特定的审查实践起主要作用。这些发现表明，早期PR模型可以支持分类和审查者优先级排序，但应作为咨询工具而非自动决策者使用。

Original abstract: Pull requests (PRs) are a central mechanism for reviewing and integrating code changes in modern software repositories. As AI coding agents begin to submit more code changes alongside human developers, maintainers face a new challenge: deciding which PRs are likely to be accepted and which ones may require substantial review effort. This paper studies whether such outcomes can be estimated at the time a PR is opened, before reviewer discussion, CI feedback, or merge decisions are available. Using the AIDev dataset, we construct a leakage-aware prediction pipeline for human- and agent-authored PRs. The feature set is limited to submission-time information, including PR text characteristics, metadata, repository context, temporal signals, and lightweight diff statistics. We evaluate classical machine-learning models, including Logistic Regression, Random Forests, Gradient Boosting, Extra Trees, and MLPs, across pooled, human-only, agent-only, and balanced contributor views. Our results show that acceptance prediction is feasible from early signals: tree-based models achieve F1 scores above 0.95, with textual clarity and metadata among the most influential predictors. Review-effort prediction is more difficult. Comment counts and time-to-merge are only modestly explained by submission-time features, suggesting that reviewer availability, project workflow, and team-specific review practices play a major role. These findings indicate that early PR models can support triage and reviewer prioritization, but should be used as advisory tools rather than automated decision-makers.

</details>


### [21] [AutoTrace: From Patches to Triggers via Agentic Interprocedural Exploration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12058v1)
*Arastoo Zibaeirad,Marco Vieira,Thomas Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AutoTrace是一个通过LLM智能体逐层探索代码属性图来定位漏洞触发点的流水线，在InterPVD上达到75.0% VulnHit和80.8% FuncHit，并构建了SinkTrace-Bench数据集以暴露因果推理差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以处理跨过程触发点，因为触发语句常位于补丁函数之外多层，静态规则和模式匹配语言模型无法有效处理。

Method: 提出AutoTrace智能体流水线，通过LLM智能体逐层探索代码属性图，结合确定性可接受性门确保每个触发点都有显式证据支持，避免无根据的模型判断。

Result: 在InterPVD基准上达到75.0% VulnHit和80.8% FuncHit，超越先前最先进技术。构建的SinkTrace-Bench数据集有1,542个平衡样本，前沿LLM难以区分匹配对。

Conclusion: AutoTrace有效提升了跨过程漏洞触发定位性能，SinkTrace-Bench暴露了当前模型在因果推理上的显著差距，未来可基于此进一步研究。

中文摘要：给定一个修复漏洞的提交，触发定位询问的是哪条具体语句将易受攻击的程序状态转变为具体的危险操作。这个问题比二分类漏洞检测更难，因为答案需要跨过程、因果推理：在相当大比例的真实世界CVE中，触发语句位于补丁函数之外的几个调用层之外，超出了静态规则集和模式匹配语言模型的范围。我们提出了AutoTrace，一个智能体流水线，通过逐层探索代码属性图来定位漏洞触发点，由LLM智能体决定下一步查看哪里，并由确定性可接受性门决定在报告触发点之前需要什么证据。智能体从不自行接受触发点；每个报告的触发点都有从图中提取的明确证据支持，因此该流水线涵盖了过程和跨过程漏洞，而不依赖无根据的模型判断。在完整的InterPVD基准测试上，AutoTrace达到了75.0%的VulnHit和80.8%的FuncHit，超过了同一语料库上的先前最先进技术。基于相同的机制，我们构建了SinkTrace-Bench，这是一个数据集，将每个漏洞暴露为从攻击者控制的输入通过传播到危险操作的源到汇（S2S）因果链，来自匹配的易受攻击和补丁程序状态。它包含1,542个验证器确认、完美平衡的易受攻击/安全样本，我们对照专家注释审计其标签保真度。在此基准测试上对前沿LLM进行测试，我们发现即使是最强的模型也难以分离匹配对，这暴露了触发定位所针对的因果推理差距。工件可在https://github.com/Erroristotle/AutoTrace获取。

Original abstract: Given a vulnerability-fixing commit, trigger localization asks which specific statement turns the vulnerable program state into a concrete unsafe operation. This question is harder than binary vulnerability detection because the answer demands interprocedural, causal reasoning: in a substantial fraction of real-world CVEs the triggering statement lies several call layers outside the patched function, beyond the reach of static rule sets and pattern-matching language models alike. We present AutoTrace, an agentic pipeline that localizes vulnerability triggers by exploring a code property graph layer by layer, with LLM agents deciding where to look next and deterministic admissibility gates deciding what evidence is required before a trigger can be reported. Agents never accept a trigger on their own authority; every reported trigger is backed by explicit evidence drawn from the graph, so the pipeline covers both intra- and interprocedural vulnerabilities without relying on ungrounded model judgment. On the full InterPVD benchmark, AutoTrace reaches 75.0% VulnHit and 80.8% FuncHit, surpassing the prior state of the art on the same corpus. Building on the same machinery, we construct SinkTrace-Bench, a dataset that exposes each vulnerability as a source-to-sink (S2S) causal chain from attacker-controlled input through propagation to the dangerous operation, drawn from matched vulnerable and patched program states. It comprises 1,542 verifier-confirmed, perfectly balanced vulnerable/safe samples whose label fidelity we audit against expert annotations. Benchmarking frontier LLMs on it, we find that even the strongest struggle to separate the matched pairs, exposing the causal-reasoning gap that trigger localization targets. Artifact available at https://github.com/Erroristotle/AutoTrace.

</details>


### [22] [Beyond Test Presence: Assessing the Quality and Robustness of Agent-Generated Tests in Open-Source Projects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12068v1)
*Preet Jhanglani,Zeel Kaushal Desai,Vidhi Kansara,Eman Abdullah AlOmar*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AI代理在生成测试时边界覆盖率优于人类，但断言强度略低且易失性更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅关注测试通过率，忽略了测试质量，可能导致隐性技术债务，因此需要评估AI生成测试的内在质量。

Method: 使用AST静态分析框架，从AIDev数据集中比较24,941个人工和179,732个代理生成的测试工件，评估断言强度、边界覆盖率和易失性潜力。

Result: AI代理在边界覆盖率上显著优于人类（多样性得分0.62 vs 0.32，空安全测试13.40% vs 8.3%），但断言强度略低（88.1% vs 85.37%），且易失性风险更高（候选率0.41 vs 0.30）。

Conclusion: AI代理擅长边界测试但缺乏环境意识，导致生成不稳定测试，需改进其稳定性。

中文摘要：将人工智能驱动的编码代理集成到持续集成/持续交付（CI/CD）流水线中，从根本改变了软件验证的方式。虽然这些代理成功自动化了测试生成，但当前的评估基准（如SWE-bench）主要关注通过率，而非生成测试的内在质量。这引发了“隐性技术债务”的可能性，即测试套件通过执行但未提供全面的覆盖率或语义价值。我们通过大规模实证比较填补了这一方法论空白，对204,673个测试工件进行了分析，其中包括24,941个人工编写文件和179,732个代理生成文件，这些文件来自AIDev数据集。利用Python原生ast模块的抽象语法树（AST）解析，我们实现了一个“白盒”静态分析框架，以评估三个质量维度：断言强度（RQ1）、边界情况覆盖率（RQ2）和易失性潜力（RQ3）。我们的结果呈现了传统假设的细微反转。AI代理在边界情况覆盖率方面优于人类，其边界检查的多样性几乎是人类的两倍（多样性得分：0.62对0.32），并且空安全性测试的频率更高（13.40%对8.3%），尽管人类开发者在断言强度上略有优势（88.1%强断言对代理的85.37%）。但这种彻底性是有代价的：由于主要依赖文件I/O和非确定性逻辑，代理生成的测试表现出更高的易失性风险（候选率：0.41对0.30）。这些发现表明，虽然AI代理擅长严格的边界测试，但它们缺乏编写稳定、密闭测试所需的“环境意识”。

Original abstract: The integration of AI-powered coding agents into Continuous Integration/Continuous Delivery (CI/CD) pipelines has fundamentally altered how software verification is conducted. While these agents successfully automate the test generation, current evaluation benchmarks (e.g., SWE-bench) largely focus on pass-rates rather than the intrinsic quality of the generated tests. This raises the possibility of "stealth technical debt", in which test suites pass execution but do not offer comprehensive coverage or semantic value. We address this methodological gap through a large-scale, empirical comparison of 204,673 test artifacts which comprises of 24,941 human-authored files and 179,732 agent-generated files; sourced from the AIDev dataset. Using the Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) parsing with Python's naive ast module, we implemented a "white-box" static analysis framework to evaluate three quality dimensions: Assertion Strength (RQ1), Edge-Case Coverage (RQ2), and Flakiness Potential (RQ3). Our results present a nuanced inversion of traditional assumptions. AI agents performed better than humans in Edge-Case Coverage, with almost twice the variety of boundary checks (Variety Score: 0.62 vs 0.32) and a higher frequency of null-safety testing (13.40% vs. 8.3%), even though human developers had a slight advantage in Assertion Strength (88.1% strong assertions vs. 85.37% for agents). But this thoroughness comes at a price: due mostly to their reliance on file I/O and non-deterministic logic, agent-generated tests exhibited a higher risk of flakiness (Candidate Rate: 0.41 vs. 0.30). These findings suggest that while AI agents excel at rigorous boundary testing, they lack the "environmental awareness" needed to write stable, hermetic tests.

</details>


### [23] [Fault Injection in OpenAPI Specifications for Evaluating Black-Box Testing Effectiveness](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12101v1)
*Hamza Bin Mazhar,Yuqing Wang,Mika V. Mäntylä*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出六类OpenAPI规范错误分类，通过注入错误评估对黑盒测试的影响，发现规范错误导致测试效果退化且仅依赖覆盖率会低估影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作假设OpenAPI规范正确，但实际中规范常存在错误，需要系统研究规范错误对黑盒测试的影响。

Method: 基于文献提出六类OpenAPI规范错误分类，注入五个严重级别的错误，在两个微服务基准测试上使用三个测试工具评估，通过代码覆盖率、规范覆盖率、请求/响应质量和行为多样性测量影响。

Result: 规范错误导致测试工具和系统上退化模式各异；方法语义错误影响广泛，响应代码修改影响弱；模式约束放宽导致隐藏退化，不影响覆盖率但影响请求/响应质量。

Conclusion: 规范质量直接影响黑盒API测试有效性，仅依赖覆盖率评估会低估影响，应补充请求/响应质量和行为多样性。

中文摘要：OpenAPI规范是微服务系统（MSS）中黑盒测试工具的主要输入，然而先前的研究表明这些规范通常不完整、不一致或不正确。尽管如此，大多数基于OpenAPI的黑盒测试研究都假设规范正确并评估工具性能。我们通过引入一个基于文献的六类OpenAPI规范错误分类来填补这一空白。我们在五个严重级别注入错误，并在两个微服务基准测试TrainTicket和SocialNetwork上使用三个测试工具EvoMaster、RESTler和Schemathesis评估生成的变异规范。我们使用代码覆盖率、规范覆盖率、请求/响应质量和行为多样性来衡量这些错误的影响。我们的结果表明，规范错误在不同测试工具和系统中引起强烈且异质的退化模式。方法语义中的错误导致所有指标的广泛退化，而其他错误（如响应代码修改）仍然较弱。模式约束的放宽导致隐藏的退化，对代码和规范覆盖率没有影响，但对请求/响应质量影响很大。这些发现表明，规范质量直接影响黑盒API测试的有效性。此外，仅基于代码和规范覆盖率的评估可能会低估规范错误对MSS黑盒测试的影响，应该辅以请求/响应质量和行为多样性。

Original abstract: OpenAPI specifications are the primary input for black-box testing tools in microservice systems (MSS), yet prior work shows these specifications are often incomplete, inconsistent, or incorrect. Despite this, most studies on OpenAPI-based black-box testing assume correct specifications and evaluate tool performance. We address this gap by introducing a literature-grounded taxonomy of six OpenAPI specification fault classes. We inject faults at five severity levels, and evaluate the resulting mutated specifications on two microservice benchmarks, TrainTicket and SocialNetwork, using three testing tools: EvoMaster, RESTler, and Schemathesis. We measure the impact of these faults using code coverage, specification coverage, request/response quality, and behavioral diversity. Our results show that specification faults cause strong and heterogeneous degradation patterns across testing tools and systems. Faults in method semantics cause broad degradation across all metrics, while others, such as modifications to response codes, remain weak. Relaxations of schema constraints cause hidden degradation, with no impact on code and specification coverage but a large impact on request/response quality. These findings demonstrate that specification quality directly shapes black-box API testing effectiveness. Also, code and specification coverage-only evaluations can understate the impact of specification faults on black-box testing in MSS and should be complemented by request/response quality and behavioral diversity.

</details>


### [24] [TraceSynth: Generating Production-Quality Kernel Traces with Constraint-Guided Diffusion Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12104v1)
*Yuvraj Sehgal,Sneh Patel,Mahsa Panahandeh,Naser Ezzati-Jivan,Francois Tetreault*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: TraceSynth是一个基于扩散的合成内核轨迹生成框架，通过多通道序列建模和约束引导修复，有效增强有限真实数据，在计算密集型工作负载下达到接近真实的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 收集生产环境内核执行轨迹成本高昂（运行时开销、存储、隐私），需要生成合成数据来增强有限真实数据。

Method: 提出TraceSynth，将轨迹建模为多通道序列（事件类型、时间戳、CPU亲和性、线程标识符、进程元数据），使用Transformer去噪扩散过程，并加入约束引导修复以强制执行系统不变量。

Result: 在六个基准测试上，上下文长度是主导质量因素，L=4096相比L=256相对改进+104%，约束引导修复提升质量最多4.3%，2通道轻量模型保留97-99%性能且成本减半。对于scimark2，合成增强F1-Macro达87.2%，仅比真实数据低2.6个百分点。

Conclusion: TraceSynth支持成本有效的合成轨迹增强，可用于生产可观测性管道，并能识别何时合成数据可替代真实数据。

中文摘要：用于系统诊断的机器学习模型依赖内核执行轨迹来捕获细粒度的系统行为，但在工业系统中收集生产轨迹由于运行时开销、存储需求和隐私约束而成本高昂。我们提出了TraceSynth，一个基于扩散的框架，用于生成合成内核轨迹，以增强有限的实际数据，用于下游机器学习任务。TraceSynth将轨迹建模为多通道序列（事件类型、时间戳、CPU亲和性、线程标识符和进程元数据），使用基于Transformer的去噪扩散过程，并通过约束引导修复来强制执行系统不变量。在六个基准测试中，结果显示强工作负载依赖性。对于确定性、计算密集型工作负载（scimark2），在上下文长度L=4096时，合成增强实现了87.2%的F1-Macro，仅比仅使用真实数据的基线低2.6个百分点。上下文长度是主导质量因素，L=4096相比L=256相对改进+104%，而约束引导修复将合成数据质量提高了最多4.3%。消融研究表明，轻量级2通道模型保留了完整6通道模型97-99%的性能，计算成本大约减半。TraceSynth支持在生产可观测性管道中成本有效地增强内核执行轨迹，并帮助确定何时合成数据可以替代有限的真实轨迹。

Original abstract: Machine learning models for system diagnostics rely on kernel execution traces to capture fine-grained system behavior, but collecting production traces in industrial systems is costly due to runtime overhead, storage demands, and privacy constraints. We present TraceSynth, a diffusion-based framework for generating synthetic kernel traces that augment limited real data for downstream ML tasks. TraceSynth models traces as multi-channel sequences (event types, timestamps, CPU affinity, thread identifiers, and process metadata) using a Transformer-based denoising diffusion process with constraint-guided repair to enforce system invariants. Across six benchmarks, results show strong workload dependence. For deterministic, compute-heavy workloads (scimark2), synthetic augmentation achieves 87.2% F1-Macro at context length L=4096, only 2.6 percentage points below real-only baselines. Context length is the dominant quality factor, with L=4096 yielding a +104% relative improvement over L=256, while constraint-guided repair improves synthetic data quality by up to 4.3%. Ablation studies show that lightweight 2-channel models retain 97-99% of the performance of full 6-channel models at roughly half the computational cost. TraceSynth supports cost-effective augmentation of kernel execution traces in production observability pipelines and helps identify when synthetic data can substitute for limited real traces.

</details>


### [25] [Self-Improving AI Coding Agents Through Accumulated Behavioral Rules: A Closed-Loop Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13091v1)
*Aditya Aggarwal,Nahid Farhady Ghalaty*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出闭环框架，将代码评审反馈转化为持久规则，消除错误复发，实现跨会话学习，无需更新模型权重。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM编码智能体因缺乏保留人类评审反馈的机制，重复相同错误，需持续人工介入。

Method: 构建累积规则集（版本控制指令文件），结合自我评审清单和自动验证，使每次评审反馈持久化。

Result: 在35+服务平台上规则从5增至18条，0%复发率，评审转向设计层面，跨接口有效。

Conclusion: 该框架通过规则积累实现编码智能体的行为一致性，无需权重更新，有效利用人类经验。

中文摘要：基于LLM的编码助手在不同会话中重复相同类型的错误，因为它们缺乏从人类评审反馈中保留修正的机制。我们提出一个闭环框架，其中每个被接受的评审意见都被编码为持久的行为规则，逐步扩展智能体能够自我检测的错误类型集合。该框架结合了版本控制指令文件中的累积规则集、代码提交前执行的自我评审清单以及确保规则集完整性随增长而增长的自动验证。在部署于一个35+服务微服务平台时，规则集从5条行为规则增长到18条，15+语言特定标准，以及一个15项的自我评审清单，全部源自真实的评审反馈。我们展示了来自11个记录工作会话的实证结果，涵盖代码生成、PR评审、事件调查和跨服务重构。我们观察到累积的规则将评审工作从低层正确性转向设计层面验证，实现了对已规则化错误类型的0%复发率，并且能够跨异构智能体接口转移。我们将我们的方法与经验性LLM学习（Reflexion、ExpeL、Voyager）和自动代码评审（CodeReviewer、SWE-bench智能体）的相关工作进行比较，表明我们的框架在不更新权重的情况下实现了持久跨会话学习，运行在生产代码库而非合成基准上，并解决了一个现有基准未测量的正交维度（随时间的行为一致性）。结果是一个编码智能体，它在每个评审周期中改进，通过其人类合作者积累工程智慧而不改变任何模型权重。

Original abstract: LLM-based coding agents repeat the same classes of mistakes across sessions because they lack a mechanism to retain corrections from human review feedback. We present a closed-loop framework in which every accepted review comment is codified as a persistent behavioral rule, progressively expanding the set of error classes the agent can self-detect. The framework combines an accumulating rule set in a version-controlled instruction file, a self-review checklist executed before code submission, and automated validation that ensures rule set integrity as it grows. In deployment across a 35+ service microservices platform, the rule set grew from 5 to 18 behavioral rules, 15+ language-specific standards, and a 15-item self-review checklist, all derived from real review feedback. We present empirical results from 11 recorded working sessions spanning code generation, PR review, incident investigation, and cross service refactoring. We observe that accumulated rules shift review effort from low-level correctness toward design-level validation, achieve a measured 0% recurrence rate for ruled-against error classes, and transfer across heterogeneous agent interfaces. We compare our approach against related work in experiential LLM learning (Reflexion, ExpeL, Voyager) and automated code review (CodeReviewer, SWE-bench agents), showing that our framework achieves persistent cross-session learning without weight updates, operates on production codebases rather than synthetic benchmarks, and addresses an orthogonal dimension (behavioral consistency over time) that existing benchmarks do not measure. The result is a coding agent that improves with every review cycle, accumulating the engineering wisdom of its human collaborators without changing a single model weight.

</details>


### [26] [TestMiner: Software Testing Analysis for GitHub Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12223v1)
*Andre Hora,José Miguel Rojas,Romain Robbes*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TestMiner工具，用于探索GitHub仓库的测试实践，并在课程中验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同项目测试实践差异大，难以理解项目如何测试，需要工具提供概览。

Method: 开发TestMiner工具，提供测试统计、位置、跨版本指标和依赖分析，并在本科课程中应用。

Result: 50名学生使用后积极反馈，能批判性探索测试组织、演化、夹具、模拟和边缘案例等实践。

Conclusion: TestMiner有效帮助探索和理解真实世界项目的测试实践。

中文摘要：软件系统具有独特的测试特征。一些项目可能强调单元测试，而另一些可能侧重于端到端测试。测试组织在不同生态系统中可能有所不同：在Python和Java等语言中，测试通常放置在专用文件夹中，而Go和Rust项目通常将测试与源代码放在一起。这些区别使得理解一个项目如何进行测试变得更加困难。在本文中，我们提出了TestMiner，一个用于探索GitHub仓库中软件测试的工具。TestMiner提供了项目测试实践的概览，包括测试统计、测试位置、跨版本的测试指标以及与测试相关的依赖关系。我们在一个本科生软件测试课程中使用了TestMiner，50名学生探索了真实世界GitHub仓库的测试实践。总体而言，学生对TestMiner表达了积极的反馈。他们能够批判性地探索各种测试实践，包括测试组织、测试演化、测试夹具、模拟和边缘案例测试。TestMiner可在以下网址获取：https://andrehora.github.io/testminer。视频：https://youtu.be/w1sBgLTq-7Y。

Original abstract: Software systems have unique testing characteristics. Some projects can emphasize unit tests, while others may focus on end-to-end testing. Test organization may vary across ecosystems: in languages like Python and Java, tests are typically placed in dedicated folders, whereas Go and Rust projects commonly co-locate tests with source code. These distinctions make it harder to understand how a project approaches testing. In this paper, we present TestMiner, a tool for exploring software testing in GitHub repositories. TestMiner provides an overview of a project's testing practices, including test statistics, test location, test metrics across releases, and dependencies related to testing. We used TestMiner in an undergraduate Software Testing course, where 50 students explored the testing practices of real-world GitHub repositories. Overall, students expressed positive feedback regarding TestMiner. They were able to critically explore a variety of testing practices, including test organization, test evolution, test fixtures, mocking, and edge-case testing. TestMiner is available at: https://andrehora.github.io/testminer. Screencast: https://youtu.be/w1sBgLTq-7Y.

</details>

### [27] [SVR-R1: Bootstrapping Multi-modal Reasoning with Self-verification in Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10966v1)
*Mingyuan Wu,Jingcheng Yang,Shengyi Qian,Xudong Wang,Jize Jiang,Qifan Wang,Aashu Singh,Khoi Pham,Fei Liu,Zhaolun Su,Zhuokai Zhao,Klara Nahrstedt,Jianyu Wang,Hanchao Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自我验证的多轮RL框架，可迁移至agent自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出SVR-R1，一个多轮强化学习框架，通过模型自我验证信号提升多模态推理，无需外部监督，在视觉-语言推理基准上显著提高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型在推理时缺乏有效的自我精炼机制，且强化学习训练中验证信号通常来自外部，我们希望利用模型自身的验证作为学习信号，减少对外部监督的依赖。

Method: 采用GRPO和异步多轮滚动框架，每个查询模型先提出答案并给出二元自我判决（Yes/No），'No'触发重思考，'Yes'或达到上限后输出并计算基于结果的奖励，整个过程无需外部监督或辅助评论者。

Result: 在视觉-语言推理基准上，SVR-R1相比强标准GRPO基线大幅提高准确率；训练动态显示验证回合减少而测试准确率上升，表明验证与生成之间的差距缩小。

Conclusion: SVR-R1有效结合了推理时自我精炼和RL训练，为提升多模态推理能力提供了简单有效的方案，有望推动VLM研究。

中文摘要：我们提出了自我验证推理器（Self-Verified Reasoner, SVR-R1），这是一个多轮强化学习框架，将模型自身的验证转化为多模态推理的学习信号。对于每个查询，模型使用相同的权重提出一个答案，并发出一个二元自我判决（是/否）。'否'触发第二次机会重新思考；'是'或达到回合上限则最终输出以计算基于结果的奖励。SVR-R1采用GRPO和异步多轮滚动框架实现，不需要外部监督或辅助评论者。我们在视觉-语言推理基准上评估SVR-R1，并显示其在强标准GRPO基线上大幅提高了准确性。训练动态显示对验证的依赖减少——更少的验证回合，但更高的测试准确率——表明随着策略内化自我修正并通过我们的框架选择最自信的答案，验证与生成之间的差距缩小。SVR-R1连接了VLMs中较少探索的推理时自我精炼和RL训练的交集，为引导多模态推理提供了一个简单而有效的配方。我们将开源SVR-R1以促进VLMs的未来研究。

Original abstract: We introduce Self-Verified Reasoner (SVR-R1), a multi-turn RL framework that turns a model's own verification into a learning signal for multimodal reasoning. For each query, the model proposes an answer using the same weights, and issues a binary self-verdict (Yes/No). A 'No' triggers a second-chance rethink; a 'Yes,' or a turn cap, finalizes the output for computing the outcome-based reward. SVR-R1 is implemented with GRPO and an asynchronous multi-turn rollout framework and needs no external supervision or auxiliary critics. We evaluate SVR-R1 on vision-language reasoning benchmarks and show that it improves accuracy by a large margin over strong standard GRPO baselines. Training dynamics show decreasing reliance on verification-fewer verification turns, yet higher test accuracy-indicating that the gap between verification and generation narrows as the policy internalizes self-correction and chooses the most confident answer via our framework. SVR-R1 bridges the less explored intersection of inference-time self-refinement and RL training for VLMs, offering a simple yet effective recipe for bootstrapping multimodal reasoning. We will open-source \textbf{SVR-R1} to facilitate future research in VLMs.

</details>


### [28] [QwenPaw-Data: Bridging Facts, Methodology, and Execution for Autonomous Enterprise Data Analytics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11019v2)
*Tianjing Zeng,Yuntao Hong,Zhongjun Ding,Dandan Liu,Yinan Mei,Yunxiang Su,Yiming Wang,Xiaojian Zhang,Jingyu Zhu,Junhao Zhu,Zhuowen Liang,Jiazhen Peng,Lianggui Weng,Zhihao Ding,Kerui Yi,Qifeng Wang,Rong Zhu,Bolin Ding,Liyu Mou,Jingren Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 企业数据分析agent系统，架构包含语义、方法、执行与进化，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: QwenPaw-Data是一个专为企业数据分析设计的智能体数据系统，通过三个子系统整合语义、方法论、执行和演化，在公共基准和工业BI负载上提升了数据访问能力和分析质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业数据分析环境开放、模糊且持续演化，现有通用智能体架构无法满足其需求，需要将语义、方法论、执行和演化作为一等关注点来设计数据智能体架构。

Method: 提出QwenPaw-Data架构，包含三个协作子系统：DataBridge（通过互连图提供语义基础）、Skill-Hub（将专家方法论编码为可重用技能）、Host（物化为可控运行时执行），并通过持续反馈形成自演化资产飞轮。

Result: 在公共基准和真实工业BI工作负载上，QwenPaw-Data提升了可验证的数据访问能力和更高层次的分析质量。

Conclusion: QwenPaw-Data为构建可靠、可追踪且持续改进的企业数据智能体提供了实用基础。

中文摘要：企业数据分析正成为自主智能体的一个独特前沿。与通用交互和软件工程相比，它在一个开放、模糊且持续演化的环境中运行。这些特性要求一种数据智能体架构，将语义、方法论、执行和演化视为系统的一等关注点。为此，我们引入了QwenPaw-Data，一个专为企业智能数据分析设计的智能体数据系统。QwenPaw-Data将来自数据仓库、仪表盘、文档、交互日志和历史任务的异构资产整合为可重用、可治理和可演化的分析资产，然后将自然语言请求转化为端到端的分析工作流，涵盖数据理解、检索、分析、报告生成和决策支持。其架构将问题分解为三个协作子系统：DataBridge通过互连的元数据、知识和追踪图提供可信的语义基础；Skill-Hub将专家分析方法论编码为可重用和可验证的技能；Host将这些证据和方法资产物化为可控的、以工件为中心的运行时执行。跨这些子系统，语义、方法、追踪和反馈持续沉积回系统，形成自演化的资产飞轮。在公共基准和真实世界工业BI工作负载上的实验表明，QwenPaw-Data提升了可验证的数据访问能力和更高级的分析质量，为可靠、可追踪且持续改进的企业数据智能体提供了实用基础。

Original abstract: Enterprise data analysis is emerging as a distinct frontier for autonomous agents. Compared with general-purpose interaction and software engineering, it operates in an open, ambiguous, and continuously evolving environment. These characteristics call for a data-agent architecture that treats semantics, methodology, execution, and evolution as first-class system concerns. To this end, we introduce QwenPaw-Data, an agentic data system designed for enterprise intelligent data analysis. QwenPaw-Data consolidates heterogeneous assets from warehouses, dashboards, documents, interaction logs, and historical tasks into reusable, governable, and evolvable analysis assets, then turns natural-language requests into end-to-end analytical workflows spanning data understanding, retrieval, analysis, report generation, and decision support. Its architecture decomposes the problem into three collaborative subsystems: DataBridge provides trustworthy semantic grounding through interconnected metadata, knowledge, and trace graphs; Skill-Hub codifies expert analytical methodology into reusable and verifiable skills; and Host materializes these evidence and method assets into controllable, artifact-centric runtime execution. Across these subsystems, semantics, methods, traces, and feedback are continuously deposited back into the system, forming a self-evolving asset flywheel. Experiments on public benchmarks and real-world industrial BI workloads show that QwenPaw-Data improves both verifiable data access capability and higher-level analytical quality, offering a practical foundation for reliable, traceable, and continuously improving enterprise data agents.

</details>


### [29] [AdvNav: Behavior-Guided Black-Box Adversarial Attacks on Vision-Language Navigation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11063v1)
*Chenyang Li,Kaige Li,Zeyu Jiang,Changhao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 黑盒对抗攻击框架，针对agent的视觉语言导航，对agent安全有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出AdvNav，一种行为引导的黑盒对抗攻击框架，通过双粒度行为反馈和混合优化策略，在仅利用可观测输入输出的情况下有效干扰VLN导航，取得高攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有白盒攻击方法不现实且计算昂贵，黑盒方法难以处理多步时序任务，需要一种无梯度攻击方法利用可观测信息破坏感知-行动循环。

Method: 基于双粒度行为反馈（轨迹级性能得分、动作级奖励得分、偏离指标）引导混合优化策略（自适应更新扰动强度+遗传演化噪声空间结构），在黑盒设置下迭代搜索最优对抗噪声。

Result: 在R2R数据集上对HAMT和MapGPT攻击，ASR达49.70/65.96/87.30%，证明有效性和通用性。

Conclusion: AdvNav揭示了VLN模型的感知漏洞，为设计弹性模型提供见解，且方法具有一般性。

中文摘要：尽管具身人工智能取得了进展，视觉与语言导航系统仍然容易受到对抗性视觉干扰的影响。大多数现有方法依赖于对目标模型梯度的白盒访问，这对于现实世界中部署的系统来说往往不切实际，并且由于优化需要递归反向传播而计算量大，限制了它们的适用性。虽然以往的黑盒方法主要针对单步、即时决策任务，但它们难以处理任务复杂性和时间依赖性。这突显了对一种无梯度攻击方法的需求，该方法仅利用可观测的输入和输出就能有效破坏多步顺序感知-行动循环。因此，我们提出了AdvNav，一种行为引导的黑盒对抗攻击框架，在导航过程中干扰智能体的第一人称视图。为了在黑盒设置下的无梯度搜索中构建信息丰富的替代目标以进行有效优化引导，我们设计了一种双粒度基于行为的反馈，聚合了表示整体导航退化的轨迹级性能得分、考虑潜在决策风险的动作级奖励得分以及一个偏离指标，所有这些都从智能体的自我输出行为中提取。该反馈引导一种混合优化策略，通过自适应更新启发式地调整扰动强度，并遗传地演化噪声空间结构，以迭代地发现最具破坏性的噪声配置。在R2R数据集上对基于Transformer的HAMT和基于LLM的MapGPT（两种主干网络）进行评估，AdvNav实现了49.70/65.96/87.30%的攻击成功率。结果证明了AdvNav的有效性和通用性，揭示了关键的感知漏洞，并为未来弹性VLN模型的设计提供了见解。

Original abstract: Despite progress in Embodied AI, Vision-and-Language Navigation systems remain vulnerable to adversarial visual disturbances. Most existing methods rely on white-box access to target model gradients, which is often unrealistic for real-world deployed systems and computationally exhaustive due to recursive backpropagation for optimization, limiting their applicability. While previous black-box methods predominantly target single-step, instantaneous decision tasks, they struggle to handle the task complexities and temporal dependencies. This highlights the need for a gradient-free attack method that can effectively disrupt the multistep sequential perception-action loop using only observable inputs and outputs. Therefore, we propose AdvNav, a behavior-guided black-box adversarial attack framework that disturbs an agent's first-person views during navigation. To construct an informative surrogate objective for effective optimization guidance in gradient-free search under the black-box setting, we design a dual-granularity behavior-based feedback, aggregating a trajectory-level performance score representing overall navigation degradation, an action-level reward score considering the potential decision risk, and a deviation indicator, all of which are extracted from the agent's self-output behaviors. This feedback guides a hybrid optimization strategy that heuristically tunes perturbation strength via adaptive updates and evolves noise spatial structure genetically, to iteratively discover the most disruptive noise configuration. Evaluated against Transformer-based HAMT and LLM-based MapGPT with two types of backbones on R2R dataset, AdvNav achieves 49.70/65.96/87.30% Attack Success Rate. The result demonstrates the effectiveness and generality of AdvNav, reveals critical perception vulnerabilities and offers insights for the design of future resilient VLN models.
