### [30] [Are LLMs Ready for Scientific Discovery? A Capability-Oriented Benchmark for AI Scientists](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11079v1)
*Chuhan Shi,Xiaoquan Ren,Sicheng Song,Haobo Li,Rui Sheng,Yushi Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AI科学家能力基准，评估LLM六种分析能力，对agent评测有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出SDABench基准，围绕六种科学分析能力评估LLMs，发现模型在描述性分析上表现好，但在假设选择、潜在过程建模和机制推理上表现差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准忽略科学分析支持不同类型的科学主张，需要更细粒度的评估来检验LLMs的能力。

Method: 构建SDABench，包含527个真实和6000个合成数据实例，跨五个领域和六种能力，采用多项选择和开放式格式，并通过五阶段错误分析框架定位失败环节。

Result: 15个LLMs中，描述性分析表现良好，但在假设选择、潜在过程建模和机制推理任务上性能急剧下降；更先进的模型能更好识别范围变量，但仍难选择适当程序和建模变量关系。

Conclusion: SDABench揭示了LLMs在科学数据分析中关键能力的不足，并提供了系统诊断框架，有助于指导模型改进。

中文摘要：现有的科学数据分析基准主要评估LLMs的代码执行或工作流完成能力，忽略了科学分析旨在支持不同类型的科学主张：假设探索、统计推断、机制解释，每种都有不同的假设和有效性标准。我们引入了SDABench，这是一个围绕六种能力（描述性、探索性、推断性、预测性、因果性和机制性）在五个领域（生物学、化学、环境、地理、物理学）重新组织评估的基准。SDABench包括527个真实数据实例（SDA-Real）和6000个合成实例（SDA-Synth），每个实例都有多项选择和开放式两种格式，通过自动化管道构建。评估了15个代表性LLMs，我们发现模型在处理描述性分析时表现良好，但在需要假设选择、潜在过程建模或机制推理的任务上表现急剧下降。SDABench进一步提供了一个五阶段错误分析框架，用于定位LLMs失败的地方：更先进的模型更可靠地识别相关范围和变量，但仍然难以选择合适的分析程序、建模变量关系并得出有效结论。

Original abstract: Existing benchmarks for scientific data analysis evaluate LLMs primarily on code execution or workflow completion, overlooking that scientific analysis serves to support distinct types of scientific claims: hypothesis exploration, statistical inference, mechanistic explanation, each with different assumptions and validity criteria. We introduce SDABench, a benchmark that reorganizes evaluation around six capabilities (descriptive, exploratory, inferential, predictive, causal, and mechanistic) across five domains (Biology, Chemistry, Environment, Geography, Physics). SDABench comprises 527 real-data instances (SDA-Real) and 6000 synthetic instances (SDA-Synth), each in both multiple-choice and open-ended formats, constructed through an automated pipeline. Evaluating 15 representative LLMs, we find that models handle descriptive analysis well but degrade sharply on tasks requiring assumption selection, latent-process modeling, or mechanistic reasoning. SDABench further provides a five-stage error analysis framework that locates where LLMs fail: more advanced models more reliably identify the relevant scope and variables, but still struggle to select appropriate analytical procedures, model variable relationships, and draw valid conclusions.

### [31] [NVAITC AI Scientist: A Governed End-to-End Research System -- A Hypertension GWAS Case Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11084v1)
*Eddie Huang,Ken Liao,Iven Fu,Yang-Hsien Lin,Chao-Shun Zhan,Andy Liao,Virginia Chen,Johnson Sun,Pika Wang,Richard Huang,Jiun-Cheng Jiang,Ting-Yuan Liu,Hsing-Fang Lu,Ray Y. Lee,Chi-Chou Liao,Simon See,Fuu-Jen Tsai*

Selection reason: 提出受治理的端到端agent研究系统，可迁移至自动代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出一个受治理的端到端代理式研究系统NAIS，在真实GWAS和药物肝毒性预测中验证其有效性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI科学工作流缺乏治理机制，无法在生物医学机构中安全使用受保护数据，需要受治理的系统实现研究规划、数据访问、可重复性和人类监督。

Method: NAIS集成提案审查、执行规划、受治理计算路由、可重复工作流编排、证据生成和科学家在环监督；在GWAS中自动化队列提取、GWAS执行、质量控制及出版物输出，并允许人机交互迭代修正。

Result: 在286,422个体的GWAS中，NAIS复现已知高血压位点（FGF5等），最强信号-\log_{10}(p)≈70；在药物肝毒性预测中多模态图神经网络AUC达0.842。

Conclusion: 受治理的代理式研究系统能支持可扩展的AI辅助生物医学发现，输出质量与专家主导工作流相当。

中文摘要：代理式研究系统正在成为一种新范式，用于协调超越孤立模型推理、代码生成或统计分析的科学工作流程。然而，在机构生物医学环境中部署需要受治理的机制，用于研究规划、数据访问、工作流编排、证据跟踪、可重复性和人类监督。我们提出了NVAITC AI科学家（NAIS），一个受治理的端到端代理式研究系统，旨在支持通用领域科学工作流，同时将受保护数据保持在机构隐私边界内。NAIS集成了提案审查、执行规划、受治理的计算路由、可重复的工作流编排、证据生成以及科学家在环监督。我们在一个真实世界的高血压全基因组关联研究（GWAS）中验证了NAIS，使用了来自286,422个个体的医院关联基因型和电子健康记录（EHR）数据，并遵循仅聚合数据政策。该代理规划了队列提取，协调了GWAS执行，生成了质量控制摘要，并草拟了面向发表的输出。人机审查识别了表型差异，并使得高血压定义能够迭代改进。在协调后，代理编排的GWAS再现了已确立的高血压位点，包括FGF5、ATP2B1、CNNM2、FTO和GRB14，其中FGF5信号最强，达到-\log_{10}(p) \sim 70。作为次要演示，NAIS还支持了药物性肝损伤预测工作流，达到了多模态图神经网络AUC为0.842。这些结果表明，受治理的代理式研究系统可以支持可扩展的AI辅助生物医学发现，同时产生可与专家主导工作流相媲美的输出。

Original abstract: Agentic research systems are emerging as a new paradigm for coordinating scientific workflows beyond isolated model inference, code generation, or statistical analysis. However, deployment in institutional biomedical environments requires governed mechanisms for research planning, data access, workflow orchestration, evidence tracking, reproducibility, and human oversight. We present NVAITC AI Scientist (NAIS), a governed end-to-end agentic research system designed to support domain-general scientific workflows while keeping protected data within institutional privacy boundaries. NAIS integrates proposal review, execution planning, governed computational routing, reproducible workflow orchestration, evidence generation, and scientist-in-the-loop oversight. We validate NAIS in a real-world hypertension genome-wide association study (GWAS) using hospital-linked genotype and electronic health record (EHR) data from 286,422 individuals under an aggregate-only data policy. The agent planned cohort extraction, orchestrated GWAS execution, generated quality-control summaries, and drafted publication-oriented outputs. Human-AI review identified phenotype discrepancies and enabled iterative refinement of the hypertension definition. After reconciliation, the agent-orchestrated GWAS reproduced established hypertension loci, including FGF5, ATP2B1, CNNM2, FTO, and GRB14, with the strongest signal at FGF5 reaching $-\log_{10}(p) \sim 70$. As a secondary demonstration, NAIS also supported a drug-induced liver injury prediction workflow, achieving a multimodal graph neural network AUC of 0.842. These results demonstrate that governed agentic research systems can support scalable AI-assisted biomedical discovery while producing outputs comparable to expert-led workflows.

### [32] [OS-Pruner: Pruning Chains-of-Thought of Reasoning Models via Optimal Stopping](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11089v1)
*Mohammed Ehab,Aymane El Gadarri,Vivek F. Farias,Adam Jozefiak,Ciamac C. Moallemi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出CoT剪枝的最优停止框架，可启发agent推理效率优化。

TL;DR: 提出OS-Pruner，一种将思维链剪枝视为最优停止问题的轻量级框架，实现了20-60%的生成长度减少而几乎不牺牲准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLMs在CoT推理中产生的冗余步骤（计算过度思考）问题，现有方法依赖静态预算、启发式过滤或重训练，缺乏动态和高效的剪枝。

Method: 将CoT剪枝形式化为最优停止问题，通过优化显式效用（权衡准确性和长度）学习何时终止推理，动态评估充分终止点。

Result: 在多种推理基准和基础模型上，生成长度减少20-60%，准确性损失最小。

Conclusion: OS-Pruner是一种轻量级、有效的框架，提供细粒度控制，能在不显著降低准确性的情况下大幅削减推理成本。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）通过思维链（CoT）提示在复杂推理任务中取得了显著成功。然而，这些模型经常表现出'计算过度思考'，生成冗余的推理步骤，这增加了延迟和成本，而不提高准确性。最近的研究表明，CoT轨迹可以被显著剪枝，但现有方法通常依赖于强制静态思考预算、启发式过滤、通过分类进行的次优提前退出或昂贵的重新训练。在本文中，我们介绍了OS-Pruner，一个轻量级的插件框架，它将思维链剪枝形式化为一个最优停止问题。给定一个推理前缀，OS-Pruner通过优化一个在最终答案准确性和生成长度之间权衡的显式效用，来学习进一步的推理是否值得其token成本。我们的新颖公式使模型能够动态评估推理链的充分终止点。OS-Pruner设计为在训练和推理过程中都是轻量级的，并为用户提供对推理努力与准确性权衡的细粒度控制。在多种推理基准和基础模型上，OS-Pruner实现了20-60%的生成长度减少，且准确性损失最小。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable success in complex reasoning tasks through Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting. However, these models often exhibit "computational overthinking," generating redundant reasoning steps that increase latency and cost without improving accuracy. Recent studies suggest that CoT trajectories can be significantly pruned, yet existing methods often rely on forcing a static thinking budget, heuristic filtering, sub-optimal early exit via classification, or expensive re-training. In this paper, we introduce OS-Pruner, a lightweight plug-in framework that formulates chain-of-thought pruning as an optimal stopping problem. Given a reasoning prefix, OS-Pruner learns whether further reasoning is worth its token cost by optimizing an explicit utility that trades off final-answer accuracy against generated length. Our novel formulation enables the model to dynamically assess the sufficient point of termination for a reasoning chain. OS-Pruner is designed to be lightweight during both training and inference, and to provide users with fine-grained control over the reasoning-effort vs. accuracy trade-off. On diverse reasoning benchmarks and base models, OS-Pruner achieves 20-60\% reduction in generation length with minimal accuracy sacrifice.

*Kumar Rahul,Shovan Chowdhury*

中文摘要：贝叶斯信念网络（BBN）是在不确定性下进行决策的强大工具。然而，构建其结构和估计参数是困难的。目前，研究人员必须在依赖专家判断或使用大型数据集来学习网络的结构和参数之间做出选择。我们提出了一种新的方法，利用大型语言模型来弥合专家意见和数据驱动学习之间的差距。该方法使用一组人工智能代理基于特定角色和上下文来估计概率。然后，我们应用修剪均值规则来去除这些响应中的噪声。我们开发了一个六步BBN框架，并以建模客户在替代医疗系统中咨询医生的意图为例进行说明。该模型揭示了，虽然自我效能似乎是一个主要因素，但其实际因果影响很小。相反，主观规范在建模客户意图方面有更强的效果。最有效的策略是同时提高信心和社区规范。

Original abstract: Bayesian Belief Networks (BBNs) are powerful tools for decision-making under uncertainty. However, building their structures and estimating parameters are difficult. Currently, researchers must choose between relying on expert judgement or using large datasets to learn the structure and parameters of the network. We propose a new methodology using Large Language Models to bridge the gap between expert opinion and data-driven learning. This approach uses a panel of AI agents to estimate probabilities based on specific personas and context. We then apply a trimmed-mean rule to remove noise from these responses. We develop a six step BBN framework and illustrate it to model customer intention to consult a doctor in an alternative healthcare system. The model reveals that while self efficacy appears to be a major factor, its actual causal impact is small. In contrast, subjective norms have a much stronger effect in modelling customers' intention. The most effective strategy is to improve both confidence and community norms simultaneously.

### [34] [A Formal Hierarchical Architecture for Agentic Orchestration with Stack-Based Execution and Lazy Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11138v1)
*Prashant Devadiga,Abhishek,Adithya Mishra,Alok Singh,Amisha Sinha,Asit Desai,Gaurang Dahad,Harshit Bhushan,Mandati Pramod Reddy,Prakhar Gupta,Rupesh Patil,Siddhi Behere*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 通过控制基准测试，分层路由在工具目录增大、多步工作流压力下优于扁平路由，并且减少了每次LLM调用的模式令牌暴露。

Conclusion: 该架构通过局部化内存和栈帧隔离，提供了企业级部署所需的隔离保证，并有效扩展了LLM智能体的工具管理能力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体能力的快速扩展暴露了一个关键的架构瓶颈：当智能体可以访问一个扁平、整体的工具注册表时，模型必须同时评估数百或数千个选项。这导致了决策空间爆炸、上下文窗口饱和以及路由精度下降。为了解决这些限制，本文提出了一种分层、基于技能的智能体编排架构。能力被组织成一棵有根树，其中内部节点做出路由决策，叶节点执行确定性任务。运行时强制执行由后进先出（LIFO）栈控制的单步执行循环，赋予智能体一种类似下推自动机的记忆形式，从而使其能够跟踪嵌套的执行上下文并从任何深度确定性恢复。能力发现遵循清单驱动的惰性加载协议：仅加载活动节点的直接子节点，因此内存和提示成本随探索路径而非全局注册表扩展。通过用本地化的栈帧取代全局内存，该架构防止一个执行分支的输出泄漏到另一个分支，为在受监管的企业环境中部署建立了所需的隔离保证。我们还讨论了UPI Help，一个AI驱动的数字支付支持产品，作为激励性的生产部署背景。我们提供了编排状态的数学形式化、执行循环的详细算法分析，以及在不断增加的工具目录、多步骤工作流压力和每次LLM调用的可见模式令牌暴露下，比较扁平路由和分层路由的控制基准测试。

Original abstract: The rapid expansion of capabilities in Large Language Model (LLM) agents has exposed a critical architectural bottleneck: when agents are given access to a flat, monolithic registry of tools, the model must evaluate hundreds or thousands of options simultaneously. This leads to decision-space explosion, context window saturation, and degraded routing accuracy. To address these limitations, this paper presents a hierarchical, skill-based architecture for agentic orchestration. Capabilities are organized as a rooted tree where internal nodes make routing decisions and leaf nodes execute deterministic tasks. The runtime enforces a single-step execution loop governed by a Last-In-First-Out (LIFO) stack, giving the agent a form of memory akin to a Pushdown Automaton, therefore enabling it to track nested execution contexts and resume deterministically from any depth. Capability discovery follows a manifest-driven, lazy-loading protocol: only the immediate children of the active node are loaded, so memory and prompt costs scale with the explored path rather than the global registry. By replacing global memory with localized stack frames, the architecture prevents outputs from one execution branch from leaking into another, establishing the isolation guarantees required for deployment in regulated enterprise environments. We also discuss UPI Help, an AI-powered digital payments support product, as a motivating production deployment context. We provide a mathematical formalization of the orchestration state, detailed algorithmic analysis of the execution loop, and controlled benchmarks comparing flat and hierarchical routing under increasing tool catalogs, multi-step workflow pressure, and visible schema-token exposure per LLM call.

</details>


### [35] [NextFund: A Unified Performance Tracking Platform for Agentic Portfolio Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11141v1)
*Changlun Li,Peixian Ma,Qiqi Duan,Zhenyu Lin,Peineng Wu*

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) based agents are beginning to participate in portfolio construction and market analysis, where decisions must be justified under evolving information and risk constraints. Current assessment practice, however, remains poorly aligned with this setting: many studies rely on static examinations or report only terminal portfolio returns, while the intermediate evidence, analyst judgments, and execution steps that produced those returns stay largely invisible. We introduce NextFund, an evaluation platform that makes financial-agent behavior observable under live market conditions. The platform couples time-consistent market access, coordinated multi-agent analysis, and persistent logging of the full decision path from observation to trade. Through an interactive Trading Arena, users can compare models across markets, inspect equity curves, and drill from leaderboard outcomes down to individual justifications. We present NextFund on Hong Kong, U.S., and China A-share equities, illustrating how inspectable decision histories enable fairer benchmarking and more actionable diagnosis. ### [36] [The Hidden Footprint: Making Storage a First-Class Metric for LLM Agent Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11149v2)
*Chenglin Yu,Hongquan Gui,Ying Yu,Hongxia Yang,Tao Zeng,Ming Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent存储开销基准，可迁移至agent资源效率评估。

TL;DR: AgentFootprint是一个评估LLM agent运行后存储足迹的基准测试，揭示了不同配置下存储差异巨大，并提出内容寻址存储可显著减少存储占用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试忽略agent运行时产生的持久数据，而存储足迹影响成本和资源管理。

Method: 开发序列化感知的度量套件，通过固定轨迹控制分离逻辑卷和持久化层放大，测量多个指标。

Result: 相同准确率下存储差异达15.7倍，内容寻址存储减少4.8-32.7倍保留量。

Conclusion: 持久存储应作为与准确性和可重构性并列的报告指标。

中文摘要：LLM agent基准测试衡量任务完成度、可靠性和推理成本，但不衡量agent运行后留在磁盘上的持久数据，包括日志、上下文快照、检查点和调试跟踪。我们引入AgentFootprint，一个跨框架的agent运行后存储足迹基准测试。其序列化感知的度量套件测量总保留量、通道组成、重复、增长、可压缩性和对话历史可重构性。它解决了一个测量陷阱：朴素的字节级测量低估了重复量一个数量级，因为数据库分页和JSON转义掩盖了重复内容。固定轨迹控制将agent生成的逻辑卷与持久化层放大分离开来：通过七个持久化框架重放相同的轨迹，产生了6.7倍的差异。在相同的模型、工具和任务下，具有100%准确率的配置在保留字节上相差15.7倍，尽管它们的默认设置支持不同的恢复和审计能力。三种全历史配置在重复观察压力任务上呈现超线性增长。来自108个实例标准化SWE-bench Verified提交的导出轨迹在每个实例上跨越三个数量级，与解决率没有可检测的相关性。内容寻址存储将保留量减少了4.8倍至32.7倍，同时保持了每个可重构性得分。这些结果将持久存储确立为与准确性和可重构性一起报告的资源度量。

Original abstract: LLM agent benchmarks measure task completion, reliability, and inference cost, but not the persistent data an agent run leaves on disk, including logs, context snapshots, checkpoints, and debug traces. We introduce AgentFootprint, a cross-framework benchmark of post-run agent storage footprint. Its serialization-aware metric suite measures total retention, channel composition, duplication, growth, compressibility, and conversation-history reconstructability. It addresses a measurement trap: naive byte-level measurement understates duplication by an order of magnitude because database paging and JSON escaping obscure repeated content. A fixed-trace control separates agent-generated logical volume from persistence-layer amplification: replaying the same trajectory through seven persisting frameworks yields a 6.7x spread. Under identical models, tools, and tasks, configurations with 100% accuracy differ by 15.7x in retained bytes, although their defaults support different recovery and audit capabilities. Three full-history configurations grow superlinearly on a repeated-observation stress task. Exported trajectories from 108 instance-normalized SWE-bench Verified submissions span three orders of magnitude per instance, with no detectable correlation with resolve rate. A content-addressed store reduces retention by 4.8x-32.7x while preserving every reconstructability score. These results establish persistent storage as a resource metric to report jointly with accuracy and reconstructability.

### [37] [STAMP: Provenance-Guided Credit Assignment for Deep Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11172v1)
*Ke Xu,Han Xu,Xinran Chen,Yuqian Wang,Zhixuan Li,Xiaojian Liu,Changwo Wu,Jianqiang Xia,Yuchen Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于来源的信用分配，可迁移至agent强化学习与奖励设计。

TL;DR: 针对强化学习中的奖励-信用不匹配问题，提出STAMP方法，通过首次暴露归因和符号保持优势调制提升步骤信用，在多个基准上取得显著改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法对暴露支持文档的动作缺乏针对性信用，导致奖励-信用不匹配，限制了深度搜索智能体的性能。

Method: 提出STAMP，包括参考验证器判断引用支持性、首次暴露归因追踪来源，并通过符号保持优势调制将步骤信用注入训练。

Result: 在BrowseComp、BrowseComp-ZH和xbench-DS上，STAMP分别提升GRPO基线+2.0/+5.5/+3.0分，且与多种奖励函数兼容。

Conclusion: 基于来源的信用信号和符号保持优势调制各自有效，证明了归因和调制对性能提升的必要性。

中文摘要：面向深度搜索智能体的强化学习主要关注轨迹级评分——结果正确性、引文感知奖励和证据覆盖。然而，暴露支持文档的动作并未获得针对性的信用，我们将这一差距称为奖励-信用不匹配。我们提出STAMP，其中基于参考的验证器判断每个引用文档是否支持训练时证据图中的实体或关系，并且首次暴露归因将每个受支持的引用追溯到首次暴露它的动作。通过符号保持优势调制注入这种步骤信用，该方法在不改变轨迹级奖励或每组内轨迹相对排名的情况下，跨步骤重新分配优势。在BrowseComp、BrowseComp-ZH和xbench-DS上，在匹配的SFT初始化、训练数据和搜索工具下，STAMP将GRPO基线提升了+2.0/+5.5/+3.0分，并且与仅结果和引文准则基础奖励组合使用。组件消融实验证实，基于来源的信用信号和符号保持优势调制各自对提升有所贡献。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning for deep-search agents has largely focused on trajectory-level scoring -- outcome correctness, citation-aware rewards, and evidence coverage. Yet the actions that expose supporting documents receive no targeted credit, a gap we call the reward-credit mismatch. We propose STAMP, in which a reference-based verifier judges whether each cited document supports an entity or relation in a training-time evidence graph, and first-exposure attribution traces each supported citation back to the action that first surfaced it. This step credit is injected through sign-preserving advantage modulation, which redistributes advantage across steps without changing the trajectory-level reward or the relative ranking of trajectories within each group. On BrowseComp, BrowseComp-ZH, and xbench-DS, STAMP improves the GRPO baseline by +2.0/+5.5/+3.0 points under matched SFT initialization, training data, and search tools, and composes with both outcome-only and citation-rubric base rewards. Component ablations confirm that the provenance-based credit signal and the sign-preserving advantage modulation each contribute to the gains.

Original abstract: The growing ability of large language models and vision language models to jointly interpret and reason over images and text is reshaping medical agents, moving them from task specific predictors toward autonomous systems that perceive, reason, plan, remember, and act in clinical environments. This work departs from the capability first perspective of existing literature and instead begins from clinical deployment, asking what tasks, contamination resistant benchmarks, and interactive training environments are required before medical agents can be trusted in practice. Medical agents are formalized as sequential decision making systems under partial observability, together with a three level autonomy taxonomy spanning assisted, cooperative, and fully autonomous operation. The field is organized along a unified scaling spine consisting of framework scaling, capability scaling, and environment scaling. Within this framework, clinical environment scaling, the integration of tools, data, and clinical gyms, is identified as the most actionable yet underexplored direction for agents operating in PACS, EHR, and FHIR ecosystems. Clinical self evolution, where agents improve through interaction with their environments rather than parameter scaling alone, is further positioned as a key research frontier, drawing insights from self improving agents, agent gyms, and test time compute scaling. Applications across radiology, pathology, ophthalmology, and hospital workflows are examined together with deployment challenges including hallucination, cascading failures, and fairness. By consolidating more than 300 references, with particular emphasis on advances from 2025 to 2026, this work provides a roadmap toward trustworthy, self improving medical imaging systems for real clinical practice.

### [39] [SCALECUA: Scaling Computer Use Agents with Verifiable Task Synthesis and Efficient Online RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11185v1)
*Bowen Lv,Xiao Liu,Yanyu Ren,Hanyu Lai,Bohao Jing,Hanchen Zhang,Yanxiao Zhao,Shuntian Yao,Jie Tang,Yuxiao Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出计算机使用agent的缩放框架，直接相关coding agent与自动代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出ScaleCUA框架，通过可验证任务合成和高效训练，扩展计算机使用智能体的在线强化学习，在OSWorld和ScienceBoard上达到新SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可验证数据稀缺和在线强化学习效率低下是扩展CUA能力的主要瓶颈。

Method: 设计VeriGen生成可验证任务，采用Frontier Sampling提高样本效率，以及Visual Context Segmentation加速训练。

Result: OSWorld上68.7%，ScienceBoard上54.0%，达到开源CUA新SOTA。

Conclusion: ScaleCUA有效提升了CUA性能，代码、模型和数据集已开源。

中文摘要：计算机使用智能体（CUA）正在成为一种强大的接口，通过视觉感知和GUI执行来自动化复杂的数字工作流程。具有可验证奖励的在线强化学习（RLVR）已成为扩展其能力的关键方向。然而，这一范式受到可验证数据稀缺和在线强化学习效率低下的瓶颈。为了打破这些障碍，我们引入了ScaleCUA，一个统一的框架，通过可验证任务合成和高效训练来扩展CUAs的在线强化学习。在数据层面，我们设计了VeriGen，一个端到端的框架，通过迭代的docker交互和多智能体反馈循环生成可验证的强化学习任务。通过共享的docker交互探针扩展到100多个并发代理工作器，该流程产生了超过24K个可验证任务和近3K个高质量强化学习任务。为了最大化样本效率，我们提出了Frontier Sampling，它跟踪每个任务的能力并将探索分配给当前学习前沿。在训练方面，我们进一步设计了Visual Context Segmentation，这是一个对最近视觉上下文的滑动窗口，平衡了探索和训练引擎的压力，与逐步分解相比，实现了2.83倍的训练加速。综上所述，ScaleCUA在OSWorld上达到68.7%，在ScienceBoard上达到54.0%，在开源计算机使用智能体中建立了新的最先进水平。代码、模型和数据集可在https://github.com/THUDM/SCALE-CUA获取。

Original abstract: Computer use agents (CUAs) are emerging as a powerful interface for automating complex digital workflows through visual perception and GUI execution. Online reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a key direction for scaling their capabilities. However, this paradigm is bottlenecked by verifiable data scarcity and online RL inefficiency. To break these barriers, we introduce ScaleCUA, a unified framework that scales online RL for CUAs via verifiable task synthesis and efficient training. At the data level, we design VeriGen, an end-to-end framework for generating verifiable RL tasks through iterative docker interactions and a multi-agent feedback loop. Scaled to 100+ concurrent agent workers via a shared docker interaction probe, this pipeline produces 24K+ verifiable tasks and nearly 3K high-quality RL tasks. To maximize sample efficiency, we propose Frontier Sampling, which tracks per-task capability and allocates rollouts to the current learning frontier. On the training side, we further design Visual Context Segmentation, a sliding window over recent visual context that balances rollout and training-engine pressure, yielding a 2.83x training speedup over step-wise decomposition. Together, ScaleCUA achieves 68.7% on OSWorld and 54.0% on ScienceBoard, establishing new state-of-the-art performance among open-source computer use agents. Code, models, and datasets are available at https://github.com/THUDM/SCALE-CUA.

### [40] [What We Talk About When We Talk About LLM Planning: Evidence for Two Distinct Planning Abilities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11197v1)
*Sukai Huang,Chenyuan Zhang,Fucai Ke,Zhixi Cai,Naim Rastgoo,Gholamreza Haffari,Hamid Rezatofighi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 区分两种规划能力，对LLM agent规划评测有直接迁移价值。

TL;DR: LLMs在规划任务中的表现差异源于两种独立的能力维度：操作推理和结构枚举，其中操作推理随模型规模和推理时间提升，而结构枚举则不然。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论证仅归因于任务难度不完整，提出LLM规划表现差异可能反映多种潜在规划能力而非单一能力谱系。

Method: 使用ACPBench-Hard数据集，评估多个LLM家族在不同测试时推理预算下的表现，并应用多维项目反应理论模型分析潜在能力结构。

Result: 发现两个主要维度：操作推理（受模型规模和推理时间正向影响）和结构枚举（对规模和时间不敏感）。

Conclusion: 提倡能力层面评估，关注哪些规划能力在什么条件下改进，而非仅关注整体性能提升。

中文摘要：当LLM在规划任务中表现出不均匀的表现时，这些差距通常归因于任务难度。我们认为这种解释是不完整的，因为任务层面的变化可能反映了不同的潜在规划能力，而不是沿着单一能力谱系的差异。我们在ACPBench-Hard上研究这个问题，通过评估多个LLM家族在不同测试时推理预算下的表现，并应用多维项目反应理论模型来揭示LLM规划背后的潜在能力结构。分析揭示了影响规划表现的两个主要维度：操作推理，即评估局部动作适用性和即时状态转换的能力，以及结构枚举，即推理目标可达性和地标结构的能力。操作推理在模型规模扩大和推理轨迹延长时得到改善，而结构枚举相对不敏感。我们的发现激发了LLM规划的能力层面评估，将关注点从模型是否整体改进转移到哪些规划能力在什么条件下以及为什么得到改进。

Original abstract: When LLMs exhibit uneven performance across planning tasks, these gaps are often attributed to task difficulty. We argue that this explanation is incomplete, as task-level variation may reflect distinct latent planning competencies rather than differences along a single ability spectrum. We study this question on ACPBench-Hard by evaluating multiple LLM families under varying test-time reasoning budgets and applying a multidimensional item response theory model to uncover the latent competency structure underlying LLM planning. The analysis reveals two principal dimensions that shape planning performance: operational reasoning, the ability to evaluate local action applicability and immediate state transitions, and structural enumeration, the ability to reason about goal reachability and landmark structure. Operational reasoning improving under model scaling and longer reasoning traces, while structural enumeration remains comparatively insensitive. Our findings motivate competency-level evaluation of LLM planning, shifting the focus from whether models improve overall to which planning competencies improve, under what conditions, and why.

</details>


### [41] [Heterogeneous Agent Cohorts for Safe Open-Ended Exploration with Runtime Constraint Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11226v1)
*Tengjiao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 异质agent队列用于安全探索，包含MCTS约束补丁，通用多agent协作机制。

TL;DR: 通过分离角色（破坏者、验证者、经纪人）并使用MCTS生成约束补丁（伤疤），该方法在保证安全的同时提高了创造性，并显著降低了代币消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLM代理在安全与创造力之间的困境：静态指令限制创造力，自由则导致安全违规。

Method: 分离角色：破坏者生成非传统提案，验证者执行运行时检查，经纪人引入类比；通过MCTS将失败编译成约束补丁（伤疤），并缓存继承；使用信用通信分配得分（CAS）限制带宽。

Result: 在空间语义沙盒中实现远程目标，无安全违规；伤疤减少15.1%代币消耗，CAS减少55.9%总代币成本。

Conclusion: 该方法有效平衡了安全与创造力，且显著降低了运行成本。

中文摘要：当今的LLM代理陷入了一个尴尬的困境。如果用静态安全指令限制它们，它们很少会突破显而易见的边界；但如果赋予它们使用工具和多代理辩论的自由，安全违规就会迅速出现。我们没有强迫单一模型同时兼顾创造性和谨慎性，而是将关注点分离到专门的角色中。一个“破坏者”生成非传统的提案，一个“验证者”在工具网关处强制执行严格的运行时检查，一个“经纪人”引入遥远但相关的类比。失败不会被丢弃——通过MCTS，它们被编译成紧凑的、签名的约束补丁，我们称之为“伤疤”。这些补丁被本地缓存并被未来的同组继承，将重复的失败转化为可重复使用的低成本运行时约束。在一个空间语义沙盒中（N=20次运行，p<0.01），我们的同组能够到达辩论失败的远程目标，验证者阻止了所有已执行的违规，并且由于避免了冗余的验证者检查，伤疤将代币消耗减少了15.1%。此外，基于信用的通信分配得分（CAS）限制了输出带宽，在资源约束下将总代币成本降低了55.9%。

Original abstract: LLM agents today are caught in an awkward bind. Lock them down with static safety instructions and they rarely venture beyond the obvious; give them free reign with tools and multi-agent debate, and safety violations quickly follow. Rather than forcing a single model to juggle both creativity and caution, we separate the concerns across specialized roles. A Disrupter generates unconventional proposals, a Validator enforces hard runtime checks at the tool gateway, and a Broker pulls in distant but relevant analogies. Failures are not discarded -- they are compiled, via MCTS, into compact, signed constraint patches we call Scars. These patches are cached locally and inherited by future cohorts, turning repeated failures into reusable, low-cost runtime constraints. In a spatial-semantic sandbox (N=20 runs, p<0.01), our cohort reaches remote targets where debate fails, the Validator prevents all executed breaches, and Scars reduce token consumption by 15.1% by avoiding redundant validator checks. Furthermore, credit-based Communication Allocation Scores (CAS) restrict outbound bandwidth, reducing overall token costs by 55.9% under resource constraints.

### [42] [Bringing Back Rule Induction to Fluid Intelligence Research? An Initial Validation of the ARC-AGI Benchmark in Humans](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11263v3)
*Jasmin Thelen,Oliver Wilhelm*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: ARC-AGI基准人类验证，可提供agent评估参考，但非直接方法。

TL;DR: 本研究首次检验了ARC-AGI基准在人类样本中的心理测量学特性，发现其具有良好的测量属性并与流体智力高度相关，支持其作为人类流体智力测量的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两种竞争观点分别强调工作记忆容量和规则归纳能力对流体智力的约束，而ARC-AGI侧重规则归纳但缺乏人类心理测量检验，因此本研究旨在评估其作为人类流体智力测量的有效性。

Method: 对100名参与者进行ARC-AGI项目测试，分析其心理测量特性并通过图形推理测试（测量图形流体智力）和图形原创性测试建立法则网络。

Conclusion: ARC-AGI可作为人类流体智力的有效测量，建议将AI基准系统嵌入人类认知能力法则网络以促进评估和跨学科合作。

中文摘要：关于流体智力（gf）测量的两种相互竞争的观点认为，表现主要受工作记忆容量或归纳新关系的能力所限制。第一种观点在当前测量中占主导地位，这体现在使用有限的一组重复规则，而第二种观点体现在许多定义中，但很少出现在测量中。ARC-AGI基准主要要求规则归纳，并被提议作为人类和人工系统的流体智力测量。然而，其心理测量学特性尚未在人类样本中检验。因此，我们在第一项研究中调查了ARC-AGI的心理测量学特性和法则网络，参与者为100人。ARC-AGI项目的汇编显示出良好的心理测量学特性，并且与通过图形推理测试测量的图形流体智力有显著相关（ρ = .63）。与图形原创性的关联较弱。这些发现为ARC-AGI作为人类流体智力测量的有效性提供了初步支持。未来研究应包括更多规则归纳任务以及额外的多变量协变量。本研究不同寻常之处在于研究最初为机器设计的任务在人类中的表现。我们建议将人工智能基准系统地嵌入到人类认知能力的法则网络中，以实现更系统的评估和跨学科合作。

Original abstract: Two competing perspectives on fluid intelligence (gf) measures propose that performance is primarily constrained either by working memory capacity or by the ability to induce novel relations. The first perspective is currently dominant in measurement, as evident from the use of a limited set of recurring rules, whereas the second perspective is reflected in many definitions but rarely present in measurement. The ARC-AGI benchmark predominantly requires rule induction and was proposed as a measure of gf for both humans and artificial systems. However, its psychometric properties have not yet been examined in human samples. We therefore investigated the psychometric characteristics and nomological network of ARC-AGI in a first study with 100 participants. A compilation of ARC-AGI items showed good psychometric properties and correlated substantially with figural fluid intelligence as measured by a figural reasoning test ($ρ$ = .63). Associations with figural originality were weak. These findings provide initial support for the validity of ARC-AGI as a measure of human fluid intelligence. Future research should include more rule induction tasks as well as additional multivariate covariates. This study is unusual by studying a task in humans that was initially designed for machines. We suggest systematically embedding AI benchmarks into the nomological network of human cognitive abilities to enable more systematic evaluation and interdisciplinary cooperation.

### [43] [Valid $\ne$ Necessary: Diagnosing Latent Inefficiency in Chain-of-Thought](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11266v1)
*Daeyeop Lee,Hwanjo Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 诊断CoT低效提出CAID度量，对agent推理优化有启发。

TL;DR: 本文揭示了CoT推理中低效步骤的评估盲点，提出CAID度量及PACE压缩策略，在三个基准上减少31-53%的token消耗且不损失准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理步骤评估器无法惩罚有效但低效的步骤，导致过度推理和计算开销。

Method: 提出基于信息论的上下文感知信息密度（CAID）度量，用于识别低效步骤，并应用于事后压缩策略PACE。

Result: 在GSM8K、StrategyQA和ARC-Challenge上，PACE将token消耗减少31-53%，同时保持准确性，优于随机移除和PRM基线。

Conclusion: CAID能有效从推理链中去除信息泡沫而不损害演绎有效性，实现高压缩率下的准确率保持。

中文摘要：链式思维（CoT）提示显著提升了大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但它常常由于过度推理而产生大量计算成本：生成冗余、冗长或不相关的步骤。虽然现有的推理步骤评估器能有效检测逻辑谬误和事实错误，但我们的分析揭示了一个关键盲点：它们未能惩罚那些有效但低效、增加token使用却不贡献于解决方案的推理步骤。为了系统诊断这一局限，我们引入了RIV-GSM8K，一个注入了五种不同类型低效（包括循环推理和过度分解）的诊断基准。诊断实验表明，最先进的评估器难以区分这些低效与必要推理。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了CAID（上下文感知信息密度），一种基于信息论的无训练指标，用于识别低效用步骤。为了验证该指标的实际效用，我们将其应用于PACE，一种事后压缩策略。额外的对照实验表明，PACE的收益并非由简单剪枝解释：与随机移除步骤和基于PRM的压缩基线相比，它在显著更高的压缩率下保持了准确性。在GSM8K、StrategyQA和ARC-Challenge上的实证结果表明，PACE在保持准确性的同时将token消耗减少了31-53%，证实了CAID成功地从推理链中提炼出信息泡沫而不损害演绎有效性。

Original abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), yet it often incurs substantial computational costs due to over-reasoning: the generation of redundant, verbose, or irrelevant steps. While existing reasoning step evaluators effectively detect logical fallacies and factual errors, our analysis reveals a critical blind spot: they fail to penalize valid but inefficient reasoning steps that inflate token usage without contributing to the solution. To systematically diagnose this limitation, we introduce RIV-GSM8K, a diagnostic benchmark injected with five distinct types of inefficiencies, including circular reasoning and excessive decomposition. Diagnostic experiments reveal that state-of-the-art evaluators struggle to distinguish these inefficiencies from necessary reasoning. To address this gap, we propose CAID (Context-Aware Information Density), a training-free metric grounded in information theory that identifies low-utility steps. To validate the metric's practical utility, we apply it within PACE, a post-hoc compression strategy. Additional control experiments show that the gains of PACE are not explained by trivial pruning: compared with random step removal and PRM-based compression baselines, it preserves accuracy at substantially higher compression rates. Empirical results on GSM8K, StrategyQA, and ARC-Challenge demonstrate that PACE reduces token consumption by 31-53% while maintaining accuracy, confirming that CAID successfully distills informational froth from reasoning chains without compromising deductive validity.

### [44] [Efficient Test-Time Optimization for Multi-Agent Proof Autoformalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11307v1)
*Tian-Shuo Liu,Shiyuan Zhang,Zijie Geng,Haoyu Liu,Runjie Xu,Pengyuan Wang,Lei Yuan,Yang Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent证明自动形式化，Decomposer-Formalizer-Prover架构，直接相关long-horizon agent。

TL;DR: ToMap是一个多智能体框架，通过瓶颈分析聚焦于分解器的测试时优化，在证明自动形式化任务上实现了19.0%的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有证明自动形式化方法要么依赖昂贵的模型训练，要么在推理时进行过度且无指导的修复，缺乏高效的测试时优化策略。

Method: 提出ToMap框架，采用分解器-形式化器-证明器流水线，通过瓶颈分析确定分解器为关键瓶颈，并利用受GEPA启发的循环和帕累托前沿指导分解进化，将测试时计算集中于此。

Result: 在ProofFlowBench上，ToMap在语法正确性和语义忠实性上比之前最佳方法提高19.0%，且测试时成本更低。

Conclusion: ToMap通过高效的测试时计算分配和分解进化，显著提升了证明自动形式化的性能，证明了聚焦瓶颈优化的有效性。

中文摘要：完全自动形式化将自然语言中的广泛数学证明与形式验证的推理联系起来，为提升可验证数学推理的上限提供了途径。与语句级形式化不同，证明自动形式化是一个长期挑战，需要在多个证明步骤中协调声明、上下文和依赖关系，但直到最近才成为集中研究的对象。当前的方法要么依赖昂贵的模型训练，要么在推理时进行过度、无指导的修复。为此，我们引入了ToMap，一个多智能体框架，将证明自动形式化结构化为分解器-形式化器-证明器流水线，并配备由形式验证和证明质量的语义评分指导的高效测试时优化。ToMap不是将测试时计算分配给所有智能体，而是进行瓶颈分析，确定分解器是关键瓶颈：其原子性、自包含的证明单元的质量直接决定了下游智能体能否成功形式化并证明每一步。因此，ToMap将形式化器和证明器视为下游执行器，并高效地将测试时计算集中在分解器的优化上。这一优化遵循受GEPA启发的循环，在候选分解上进化提示，并利用形式验证进度和语义证明评分来定义帕累托前沿，指导下一次分解更新。在ProofFlowBench上的实验表明，当通过语法正确性和语义忠实性进行评估时，ToMap比之前的最佳方法提高了19.0%，同时测试时成本更低。规模分析显示，大多数收益出现在几次分解进化迭代内，指导着测试时预算的选择。

Original abstract: Full-proof autoformalization bridges extensive mathematical proofs in natural language with formally validated reasoning, offering a pathway to elevate the ceiling of verifiable mathematical reasoning. Unlike statement-level formalization, proof autoformalization is a long-horizon challenge requiring coordination of claims, contexts, and dependencies across many proof steps, yet has only recently come under focused study. Current approaches either rely on costly model training or apply excessive, unguided repair at inference time. To this end, we introduce ToMap, a multi-agent framework that structures proof autoformalization as a Decomposer-Formalizer-Prover pipeline with efficient test-time optimization guided by formal verification and semantic rubrics for proof quality. Rather than distributing test-time compute across all agents, we perform bottleneck analysis and identify the Decomposer as the critical bottleneck: the quality of its atomic, self-contained proof units directly determines whether downstream agents can successfully formalize and prove each step. ToMap therefore treats the Formalizer and Prover as downstream executors and efficiently focuses test-time compute on Decomposer refinement. This refinement follows a loop inspired by GEPA, evolving prompts over candidate decompositions and using formal verification progress together with semantic proof rubrics to define a Pareto frontier that guides the next decomposition update. Experiments on ProofFlowBench show that ToMap improves over the best previous method by 19.0% when evaluated by both syntactic correctness and semantic faithfulness, while requiring lower test-time cost. Scaling analysis shows that most gains emerge within a few iterations of decomposition evolution, guiding test-time budget selection.

### [45] [Calibrated e-CUSUM Decoding for Quantized Reasoning Models: Why Token Log-Probability Is the Wrong Observable for Decoding Monitors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11317v1)
*El Hassane Ettifouri,Ayoub Belfatmi,Mahaman Sanoussi Yahaya Alassan,Walid Dahhane*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 量化模型解码监控，提出校准检测器，对agent可靠性有启发。

TL;DR: 针对低比特量化导致小型推理模型思维链退化的问题，提出一种无需训练的解码控制器，通过融合词元不确定性与逐字重复的报警评分和e-过程启发的序列检测器，有效识别失败轨迹，并在GSM8K上验证了其效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低比特量化虽降低部署成本，但会损害小型模型的思维链质量，且自然候选指标（中心化词元对数概率增量）在监测退化时无效，因此需要更好的解码器监控方法。

Method: 提出一种无需训练的解码控制器，包含(i)退化感知报警评分（融合词元不确定性与显式逐字重复）和(ii)基于e-过程启发的序列检测器（使用CUSUM下限统计量作为经验变化检测器）。

Result: 在GSM8K上使用DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B的FP16和INT4版本，校准将误报率从93-95%降至选择性检测（φ≈0.3，精确率≈0.6），INT4准确率从63%升至69%（p=0.18），代价为28%词元预算；非终止是主要失败模式。

Conclusion: 主要贡献是方法论上的：揭示了中心化词元对数概率不适用于解码器监控的原因，并提供了一个经过校准、审慎评估的替代方案。

中文摘要：低比特量化使得小型推理模型部署成本低廉，但可能降低其思维链质量。这激发了解码器端监控器的需求，在生成变得不可靠时进行干预。我们表明，一个自然的候选指标——中心化词元对数概率增量log p(w_t)+H_t——在此用途上是错误的可观测变量。根据模型自身的采样规律，它本质上是一个均值为零的鞅，因此衡量的是采样的自一致性而非轨迹的健康状况，并且在置信重复期间几乎保持沉默，此时log p(w_t)和熵都接近于零。我们引入了一种无需训练的解码控制器，它结合了(i)一个退化感知报警评分，融合了词元不确定性与显式逐字重复；(ii)一个校准的基于e-过程启发的序列检测器。原始乘积过程在条件均值零假设下满足Ville有效性，而部署的基于CUSUM下限的统计量被当作经验变化检测器，因为评分具有历史依赖性和自相关性。在GSM8K上，使用DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B的FP16和INT4版本，校准将一个对93-95%的生成都触发报警的监控器转变为对失败轨迹的选择性检测器（φ≈0.3，精确率≈0.6，基础发生率0.38）。在此试点中，控制器减少了测量的逐字退化信号，并带来了INT4准确率从63%到69%的正面但统计上不显著的提升（配对McNemar检验p=0.18，n=100），代价是28%的词元预算。我们还发现，非终止而非循环是GSM8K上的主要失败模式。主要贡献是方法论的：解释了为什么中心化词元对数概率不足以用于解码器监控，以及一个经过校准、审慎评估的替代方案。

Original abstract: Low-bit quantization makes small reasoning models inexpensive to deploy but can degrade their chains of thought. This motivates decoder-side monitors that intervene when generation becomes unreliable. We show that a natural candidate, the centered token log-probability increment $\log p(w_t)+H_t$, is the wrong observable for this purpose. Under the model's own sampling law it is a mean-zero martingale by construction, so it measures sampling self-consistency rather than trajectory health and is nearly silent during confident repetition, where both $\log p(w_t)$ and entropy are close to zero. We introduce a training-free decoding controller that combines (i) a degeneration-aware alarm score fusing token uncertainty with explicit verbatim repetition and (ii) a calibrated e-process-inspired sequential detector. The raw product process is Ville-valid under a conditional-mean null, while the deployed CUSUM-floored statistic is treated as an empirical change detector because the score is history-dependent and autocorrelated. On GSM8K with DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B in FP16 and INT4, calibration turns a monitor that fires on 93--95% of generations into a selective detector of failing traces ($φ\approx 0.3$, precision $\approx 0.6$ against a 0.38 base rate). In this pilot, the controller reduces measured verbatim-degeneration signals and yields a positive but statistically inconclusive INT4 accuracy change from 63% to 69% (paired McNemar $p=0.18$, $n=100$), at a 28% token-budget cost. We also find that non-termination, rather than looping, is the dominant failure mode on GSM8K. The main contribution is methodological: an explanation of why centered token log-probability is inadequate for decoder monitoring and a calibrated, cautiously evaluated replacement.

</details>


### [46] [Verifier-Guided Twelve-Tone Composition: A Generate-Verify-Repair Harness for Symbolic Music Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11334v2)
*Congren Dai,Danni Zhao,Enyang Liu,Michael Ching Yam,Zhancheng Guo,Siyi Gu,Wentao Yang,Bo Dai,Xiaobing Li,Maosong Sun*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型生成的十二音谱表面合法但易退化，需要提高其局部一致性。

Result: 约束检查交付率从13.3%提升到48.1%，碰撞检查通过率从33.5%提升到58.3%，退化率保持0.05，专家偏好框架结果。

中文摘要：大型语言模型可以生成表面上合法的十二音谱，但这些谱往往退化为退化织体。我们引入了一种神经符号框架，该框架将语言模型生成器包装在生成-验证-修复-追踪循环中，并辅以符号验证。整个流水线提升了事件局部一致性，但不声称整体作品合法性。在40个受控任务和四个配对模型上，经约束检查的交付率从原始生成的13.3%上升到使用框架后的48.1%；剩余的51.9%运行中框架选择弃权。较窄的碰撞和序列化一致性检查的通过率从33.5%上升到58.3%，而退化率保持在0.05附近，包括在对抗性提示下。五位专家进行的盲审评估还表明，在遵循性、感知合法性、连贯性和整体质量方面，专家总体上更偏好框架生成的候选结果而非原始生成结果。

Original abstract: Large language models can produce superficially legal twelve-tone scores that collapse into degenerate textures. We introduce a neuro-symbolic harness that wraps a language-model proposer in a generate-verify-repair-trace loop with symbolic verification. The complete pipeline improves event-local consistency without claiming whole-piece legality. Across 40 controlled tasks and four paired models, constraint-checked delivery rises from 13.3% under raw generation to 48.1% with the harness; it abstains on the remaining 51.9% of runs. The pass rate of a narrower collision and serialisation-consistency check rises from 33.5% to 58.3%, while degeneracy remains near 0.05, including under adversarial prompting. A blinded evaluation by five experts also shows a descriptive aggregate preference for harness candidates over raw generation in adherence, perceived legality, coherence, and overall quality.

### [47] [AutoVSR: Automatic Visual-to-Symbolic Reasoning for Symbolic Expression Generation from Circuit Schematic](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11338v1)
*Zhe Xiao,Longfei Li,Xu He,Haoying Wu,Zixing Zhang,Mingyu Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: VLM+符号求解器规划agent，方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出AutoVSR框架，结合视觉语言模型和符号求解器，从电路图像生成符号表达式，显著提升准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从电路原理图直接推导符号表达式需要准确的视觉到符号构建和多步符号推导，现有方法准确率低，缺乏可靠框架。

Method: AutoVSR通过组件规则检索和验证反馈构建可执行中间表示，并使用规划代理符号求解器进行多步推导。

Result: 在符号表达式生成任务上，准确率比端到端VLM提升30.01-59.45%，比专门方法提升41.96-51.84%，推理成本和计算效率超越闭源VLM。

中文摘要：符号表达式可以有效地表征和预测电路行为，但从电路原理图中直接推导它们是具有挑战性的。这个过程需要从图像中准确地进行电路结构的视觉到符号的构建，以及正确的多步符号推导，这两者都对正确性有严格的要求。本文提出了AutoVSR，一个使用视觉语言模型（VLM）自动从视觉到符号生成电路表达式的框架。通过将电路图重构为可执行的中间表示（Executable IR）并利用符号求解器进行推理，AutoVSR显著提高了符号表达式生成的准确性。AutoVSR引入了两个关键创新：一种由组件规则检索和基于验证的反馈引导的IR构建方法，以及一个作为规划代理实现的符号求解器，配备符号工具库以实现可靠的多步推导。与端到端的VLM方法和专门方法相比，AutoVSR在主符号表达式生成任务上的准确率分别提高了30.01-59.45%和41.96-51.84%。此外，AutoVSR在推理成本和计算效率上超越了闭源的最先进VLM。代码可在https://github.com/LongfeiLi1/AutoVSR获取。

Original abstract: Symbolic expressions can effectively characterize and predict circuit behavior, but deriving them directly from circuit schematics is challenging. This process requires accurate visual-to-symbolic construction of circuit structure from images and correct multi-step symbolic derivation, both of which impose strict correctness requirements. This work proposes AutoVSR, an automated framework for visual-to-symbolic generation of circuit expressions using Vision Language Models (VLMs). By reconstructing circuit diagrams into an executable intermediate representation (Executable IR) and leveraging a symbolic solver for reasoning, AutoVSR significantly improves the accuracy of symbolic expression generation. AutoVSR introduces two key innovations: an IR construction method guided by component rule retrieval and verification-based feedback, and a symbolic solver implemented as a planning agent equipped with a symbolic tool library for reliable multi-step derivation. Compared with end-to-end VLM approaches and specialized methods on the main symbolic expression generation task, AutoVSR achieves accuracy improvements of 30.01--59.45% and 41.96--51.84%, respectively. Moreover, AutoVSR surpasses closed-source state-of-the-art VLMs in inference cost and computational efficiency. Code is available at https://github.com/LongfeiLi1/AutoVSR.

### [48] [Compile, Then Page: Executable SOP Programs and a Capability-Gated Runtime for Procedural LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11346v2)
*Chenglin Yu,Li Yin,Ying Yu,Qingxin Fan,RunyangRay Zhong,Hongxia Yang,Ming Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 编译SOP为agent程序，运行时状态管理，对长程agent有启发。

TL;DR: 通过将SOP编译为伪代码并结合程序引导栈机器，强模型在遵循流程方面显著提升，而弱模型则受到损害，建议先编译并根据模型纪律启用分页。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业代理需要遵循复杂的安全关键标准操作程序（SOP），但现有LLM在长时序条件任务中表现不佳，需要更结构化的执行框架。

Method: 将SOP约束编译为可执行伪代码，使用程序引导（PG）栈机器管理活动帧分页，并由LLM执行语义执行；通过SOPBench实验比较不同表示和运行时策略。

Result: 编译文本在弱表示下增益高达16.0分；强模型在PG运行时下表现优异（58:19和75:31不一致对），弱模型受损；全程序光标消融恢复大部分强模型拒绝增益；Bank任务上三臂得分从70.4升至86.4再至92.8，拒绝正确性100%。

Conclusion: 实用建议：应优先编译SOP，并仅在模型通过纪律检查后才启用活动帧分页，以提升强模型性能并避免弱模型受损。

中文摘要：企业代理必须遵循长期、条件性、安全关键的标准操作程序（SOP）。我们将机器可读的SOP约束编译为可执行的伪代码，并使用程序引导（PG）的栈机器运行，该机器对活动帧进行分页，同时大语言模型（LLM）执行语义执行。一项横跨六个模型的三臂SOPBench研究将表示与运行时分离：编译文本从未显著损害性能，且在官方散文表现不佳的情况下增益高达16.0分。运行时指导是能力门控的。两个强模型独立显示出正向的七领域PG对比（58:19和75:31的不一致对），而弱模型则受到损害。全程序光标消融（活动帧优先，完整程序保留）恢复了强模型拒绝增益的大部分；选择性可见性带来了较小的改进。配对探针和审计测量将此差异追踪到自发状态纪律而非重建能力。在Bank上，三个主要臂从70.4升至86.4再升至92.8，拒绝正确性达到100%。实用指南：先编译；仅通过模型级纪律检查后启用活动帧分页。

Original abstract: Enterprise agents must follow long-horizon, conditional, safety-critical standard operating procedures (SOPs). We compile machine-readable SOP constraints into executable pseudo-code and run them with a program-guided (PG) stack machine that pages the active frame while an LLM performs semantic execution. A three-arm SOPBench study across six models separates representation from runtime: compiled text never significantly hurts and gains up to 16.0 points where official prose underperforms. Runtime guidance is capability-gated. Two strong models independently show positive seven-domain PG contrasts (58:19 and 75:31 discordant pairs), whereas weak models are harmed. A full-program cursor ablation (active frame first, complete program retained) recovers much of the strong-model refusal gain; selective visibility adds a smaller improvement. Paired probe and audit measurements track this divide to spontaneous state discipline rather than reconstruction ability. On Bank the three primary arms rise from 70.4 to 86.4 to 92.8, with 100% refusal correctness. Practical guidance: compile first; enable active-frame paging only after a model-level discipline check.

Original abstract: Failure diagnosis in modern software systems requires iterative evidence acquisition and hypothesis reasoning guided by operational experience. Existing LLM-based methods improve diagnosis through agentic reasoning or knowledge augmentation, but they often lack a mechanism to coordinate the evolving diagnostic state with operational experience during iterative diagnosis. We propose OpsMem, a dual-memory framework that maintains a short-term memory for the current diagnostic state and a long-term memory for reusable operational experience. OpsMem uses cross-memory resonance to activate state-relevant long-term memory, conditions multi-agent diagnosis on the short-term and activated long-term memories, and consolidates reusable experience from solved incidents back into long-term memory. Experiments on a real-world Huawei microservice failure diagnosis dataset show that OpsMem outperforms representative agentic-reasoning and knowledge-augmented baselines, improving Match and Relevant by up to 46.88% and 18.39% over the strongest baseline, respectively.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs) have enabled increasingly capable digital agents for computer use. However, real-world tasks are often long-horizon and involve evolving contexts containing accumulated observations, intermediate edits, failed attempts, and partially completed executions. Existing agents typically operate over raw interaction history, making task progress difficult to interpret, verify, and recover, which ultimately limits reliable long-horizon execution. In this paper, we argue that addressing this challenge requires explicitly structuring both the agent's state and workflow around a unified causal representation of task progress. We present \textbf{StructAgent}, a state-centered framework that introduces a unified state for maintaining compact, verifiable task progress and a structured workflow that regulates progress through verifier-backed state transitions. Building on this design, StructAgent further enables explicit progress checkpointing, evidence-driven task completion, targeted failure recovery, and tool-supported execution, while ensuring that all progress updates remain grounded in verification. Extensive experiments demonstrate that StructAgent consistently improves a wide range of LLM and VLM backbones on long-horizon computer-use tasks. On OSWorld-Verified, it improves Qwen3.5-9B from 27.0\% to 46.9\% success rate and Qwen3.5-27B from 31.6\% to 62.2\%, while achieving a new open-source state of the art of 78.9\% with MiniMax-M3. ### [51] [Omni-Decision: A Progressive Evidence-State Agent System for Omni-Modal QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11433v1)
*Ming Ma,Yi Zhu,Yiran Zhong,Feida Zhu,Weigao Sun,Junhan Shi,Lingrui Mei,Tianming Yang,Steven Hoi*

TL;DR: Omni-Decision通过维护结构化证据状态，实现了无需训练的、可解释的全模态证据寻找问答，显著提升了性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统难以跟踪证据状态，导致证据缺失和冗余。

Method: 提出训练自由的证据状态系统，维护并更新结构化证据状态。

Result: OmniGAIA上45.6%，WorldSense上58.3%，分别提升27.3和30.2个百分点。

Conclusion: 显式证据状态控制有效支持多步全模态证据寻找。

中文摘要：全模态证据寻找问答要求智能体回答其证据稀疏分布在视频、音频、图像、网页和计算结果中的问题。现有的智能体多模态系统通常将证据留在暂存器、工具轨迹或自由格式的历史记录中，这使得难以跟踪哪些证据已被确认，哪些仍然缺失，以及何时证据足以回答问题。我们提出Omni-Decision，一个无需训练的证据状态系统，它将全模态问答转化为查询范围的证据封闭过程。对于每个查询，Omni-Decision维护一个结构化的证据状态，包含已确认的证据、未解决的冲突、事实和计算依赖关系以及未满足的证据需求。共享的状态视图条件化规划、证据获取、验证、修复和最终化。来自媒体、网页、计算和验证模块的异构观察通过确定性状态更新进行归一化、判断和提交。这种设计实现了有针对性的证据获取，保留了稀疏的跨模态线索，并提供了可检查的修复和停止控制。Omni-Decision在OmniGAIA上达到45.6%的准确率，在WorldSense上达到58.3%，分别比基线提高了27.3和30.2个百分点。无状态消融实验和轨迹审计进一步支持了显式证据状态控制在多步骤全模态证据寻找中的作用。

Original abstract: Omni-modal evidence-seeking QA requires agents to answer questions whose evidence is sparsely distributed across videos, audio, images, web pages, and computation results. Existing agentic multimodal systems often leave evidence in scratchpads, tool trajectories, or free-form histories, making it difficult to track what has been grounded, what remains missing, and when the evidence is sufficient to answer. We propose Omni-Decision, a training-free evidence-state system that turns omni-modal QA into a query-scoped evidence-closure process. For each query, Omni-Decision maintains a structured evidence state containing confirmed evidence, unresolved conflicts, fact and computation dependencies, and open evidence needs. A shared state view conditions planning, evidence acquisition, validation, repair, and finalization. Heterogeneous observations from media, web, computation, and verification modules are normalized, judged, and committed through deterministic state updates. This design enables targeted evidence acquisition, preserves sparse cross-modal cues, and provides inspectable control over repair and stopping. Omni-Decision achieves 45.6% accuracy on OmniGAIA and 58.3% on WorldSense, improving over the baselines by +27.3 and +30.2 percentage points, respectively. No-state ablations and trajectory audits further support the role of explicit evidence-state control in multi-step omni-modal evidence seeking.

*Tsz Hei Fan,Choi Wing Fung,Yuxuan Wan,Shuqing Li,Michael R. Lyu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM生成多场景游戏世界，包含规划、验证等agent流程，虽非代码优化但可提供复杂任务分解启发。

TL;DR: MAGIC是一个四阶段流水线系统，将自然语言提示转化为可运行的多场景游戏项目，解决了跨场景一致性、场景内可导航性和转换评估问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多场景游戏创作费力，现有单场景生成方法无法直接产生连贯的多场景世界，存在跨场景一致性、可导航性和转换评估三个未解决障碍。

Method: MAGIC包含四个阶段：规划共享的转换感知中间表示、通过洪水填充验证强制执行传送门可达性、生成场景和转换脚本、组合成项目；并引入专注于转换的评估代理在游戏中运行每个转换。

Result: 在100个多场景案例上，MAGIC生成每个案例的可执行项目，端到端转换识别达到0.99精确率、0.95召回率和0.96 F1；逐阶段比基线和Holodeck恢复更多地面真值传送门且布局更可导航。

Conclusion: MAGIC有效解决了多场景导航创作中的关键问题，成功生成了可运行的多场景游戏项目，并提供了代码开源。

中文摘要：多场景导航（在一个有边界空间中完成目标，然后穿过传送门进入下一个空间）是当代3D游戏的一个标志性特征，但创作它非常费力：每个传送门必须在两侧有一致的端点，每个内部空间在布置后必须保持可导航性，并且最终的连通性必须在多个文件中保持一致。最近的大型语言模型（LLM）和多模态LLM（MLLM）场景生成器使得单个内部空间的合成成本显著降低，但它们一次只生成一个场景，并且通过简单的重复无法生成一个连接的多场景世界。我们确定了单场景方法未解决的三个障碍：跨场景一致性、场景内可导航性以及评估转换是否实际有效。我们提出了MAGIC，一个提示到项目的系统，解决了这三个问题。MAGIC是一个四阶段流水线，将单个自然语言提示转化为可运行的多场景游戏项目：它规划一个共享的、感知转换的中间表示，指定每个场景同时通过洪水填充验证器强制执行传送门可达性，生成场景及其转换脚本，并将它们组合成一个项目。由于现有的单场景保真度指标从不执行转换，我们进一步引入了一个专注于转换的评估代理，它在游戏中运行每个转换。在一个包含100个多场景案例的新基准上，MAGIC为每个案例生成了一个可执行的项目，并在端到端转换识别上达到0.99精确率、0.95召回率和0.96 F1；逐阶段地，它比LLM基线和Holodeck恢复了更多的地面真值传送门，并产生了明显更可导航的布局。我们的代码可在https://github.com/sereneee1201/MAGIC/获取。

Original abstract: Multi-scene navigation (clearing an objective in one bounded space and then crossing a portal into the next) is a defining feature of contemporary 3D games, but authoring it is laborious: every portal must have consistent endpoints on both sides, each interior must remain navigable once it is furnished, and the resulting connectivity must be kept consistent across many files. Recent large language model (LLM) and multimodal LLM (MLLM) scene generators have made single-interior synthesis dramatically cheaper, yet they produce one scene at a time and cannot, by naive repetition, yield a connected multi-scene world. We identify three obstacles that single-scene methods leave unsolved: cross-scene consistency, in-scene navigability, and the evaluation of whether a transition actually works. We present MAGIC, a prompt-to-project system that addresses all three. MAGIC is a four-stage pipeline that turns a single natural-language prompt into a runnable multi-scene game project: it plans a shared transition-aware intermediate representation, specifies each scene while enforcing portal reachability with a flood-fill validator, generates the scenes together with their transition scripts, and combines them into one project. Because existing single-scene fidelity metrics never execute a transition, we further introduce a transition-focused evaluation agent that runs each transition in play. On a new benchmark of 100 multi-scene cases, MAGIC produces an executable project for every case and reaches 0.99 precision, 0.95 recall, and 0.96 F1 on end-to-end transition identification; stage by stage, it recovers more ground-truth portals and yields markedly more navigable layouts than an LLM baseline and Holodeck. Our code is available at https://github.com/sereneee1201/MAGIC/.

</details>


### [53] [Interaction Scaling: Grounding the Third Axis of Test-Time Compute](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11598v1)
*Bojie Li,Noah Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出交互缩放作为测试时计算，强调外部反馈接地，直接提升编程任务性能，对coding agent设计极具启发。

TL;DR: 交互式扩展（模型与外部工具交互）比内部推理或采样更有效，但前提是反馈和度量都基于真实世界的观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时计算扩展方法（推理和采样）受限于内部知识，无法引入新信息，而交互可以通过外部观测突破性能天花板。

Method: 提出交互框架：模型生成产物，外部仪器观察实际行为并反馈，模型据此修订；强调反馈和度量必须基于真实观测（grounding）。

Result: 在编码任务上，交互策略持续改进，提议者-评审者框架达到100%通过率；在视觉任务上，基于真实布局的度量消除了40-74%缺陷，而基于VLM的度量无效。

Conclusion: 交互缩放是有效的第三轴，但与推理和采样不同，其成功依赖于反馈和度量的基础性（grounding）。

中文摘要：有两种标准方法可以在测试时投入更多计算：让模型思考更久，或者采样更多尝试并保留一个。两者都有一个隐藏的限制：它们是内部的。每一个额外的token都来自相同的冻结权重和相同的提示，因此两者都无法告诉模型任何它还不知道的信息。我们研究了第三种方法，即交互：模型提出一个产物，外部仪器观察其实际行为，然后模型进行修订。每一次循环都引入了一个真实的观察，因此交互突破了其他两种方法所遇到的天花板。我们认为，一个单一的变量支配着这第三个轴，即基础性（grounding），并且它必须在循环的两侧都成立。驱动修订的反馈必须来自一个实际观察缺陷的仪器，评分结果的度量也必须如此。在固定token预算的困难编码任务上，仅推理和最佳N采样都出现平台期（后者即使有一个oracle来选择最佳样本），而每一种交互策略都在持续改进；我们的提议者-评审者框架达到了完美的100%通过率，没有运行间方差，并且这种增益在三个模型家族中保持一致。在渲染的视觉产物上，通常的评审者（一个视觉语言模型，或VLM，读取屏幕截图）将14个明显有缺陷的图形中的15个评为“完美”，因为屏幕截图在评审者看到之前就隐藏了缺陷。相反，一个测量真实布局的工具显示，循环消除了四种模态中40-74%的缺陷；而同样的VLM作为评审者，会使幻灯片布局变得更差，而测量工具则会修复它们。交互缩放是真实的，并且不同于推理和采样，但只有当反馈和度量都有基础性时才可见。

Original abstract: There are two standard ways to spend more compute at test time: let a model reason longer, or sample more attempts and keep one. Both share a hidden limit: they are internal. Every extra token comes from the same frozen weights and the same prompt, so neither can tell the model anything it does not already know. We study a third way, interaction: the model proposes an artifact, an external instrument observes how it actually behaves, and the model revises. Each cycle imports a real observation, so interaction breaks through the ceiling the other two hit.
  We argue that a single variable governs this third axis, grounding, and that it must hold on both sides of the loop. The feedback that drives revision must come from an instrument that actually observes the flaw, and so must the metric that scores the result. On hard coding tasks at a fixed token budget, reasoning-only and best-of-N sampling both plateau (the latter even when an oracle picks the best sample), while every interaction strategy keeps improving; our proposer-reviewer harness reaches a perfect 100% pass rate with no run-to-run variance, and the gain holds across three model families. On rendered visual artifacts, the usual judge (a vision-language model, or VLM, reading a screenshot) rates 14 of 15 visibly broken figures "perfect," because the screenshot hides the flaws before the judge can see them. A tool that measures the real layout instead shows the loop removing 40-74% of defects across four modalities; and that same VLM, used as the reviewer, makes slide layouts worse where the measuring tool repairs them. Interaction scaling is real and distinct from reasoning and sampling, but only visible when both the feedback and the metric are grounded.

</details>


### [54] [Think Through a Bottleneck: Hourglass Reasoning for Rigorous Induction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11696v1)
*Huan Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Hourglass推理方法，通过严格隔离推理阶段提升归纳推理，属于agent推理规划方法，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出沙漏推理，通过强制隔离推理阶段并只传递压缩符号状态，显著提升LLM在小样本归纳推理中的表现，在多个基准上超越迭代精炼基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我精炼方法在增强LLM小样本归纳推理时效果有限，因为明确陈述规则本身作用不大；关键在于推理阶段间的信息流动方式。

Method: Hourglass推理：冻结LLM作为元构造器，构建符号编码器-解码器，包括归纳、演绎、实现和精炼四个阶段，仅允许压缩的符号状态(φ,T)跨越阶段边界，实现严格上下文隔离。

Result: 在ARC-AGI-2上准确率提升14个百分点；ChipBench上Verilog合成准确率从31%提升至58%；BBEH-Linguini上逆转显式语言化对性能的负面影响。

Conclusion: 推理阶段间的结构隔离和初始归纳质量是关键，而非提示措辞或符号形式；信息流动方式驱动归纳推理。

中文摘要：自我精炼通常无法增强大型语言模型在小样本归纳推理中的能力。仅仅提示模型明确陈述其推断的规则本身作用不大。真正重要的是在推理阶段之间进行结构强制隔离，使得信息只能以压缩的符号状态在阶段之间传递。

我们引入了**沙漏推理**，它在推理阶段之间强制执行严格的上下文隔离。冻结的LLM充当元构造器，为每个任务构建一个符号编码器-解码器：一个归纳模块将支持示例压缩为模式$φ$（编码器）和一个临时支架$z$；一个演绎模块从这些中推导出规则$T$（解码器）并丢弃$z$；一个实现者将$(φ, T)$编译成工件；一个错误驱动的精炼者修订$(φ, T)$并从头重新生成工件。只有$(φ, T)$跨越阶段边界，因此所有精炼都锚定在规则上。

我们在三个基准上评估沙漏推理，涵盖视觉抽象、硬件综合和文本规则归纳，使用GPT-5.5和Gemini 3.1 Pro。在ARC-AGI-2上，它将最佳5次准确率比迭代精炼基线提高了多达14个百分点。在ChipBench上，它使GPT-5.5的Verilog综合准确率几乎翻倍，从31%提高到58%。BBEH-Linguini基于国际语言学奥林匹克竞赛的谜题，在这种设置下，先前工作表明显式语言表达可能损害性能。沙漏推理缓解了这种趋势，在Gemini 3.1 Pro上，它完全逆转了这种影响。

消融实验证实，这些收益来自于阶段间的隔离和初始归纳的质量，而非提示措辞或所使用的特定符号形式。驱动冻结LLM归纳推理的是信息在推理过程中的流动方式，而不是用于表达信息的语言。

Original abstract: Self-refinement often fails to strengthen few-shot inductive reasoning in large language models. Prompting a model to explicitly state its inferred rule does little on its own. What actually matters is a structurally enforced isolation between reasoning stages, so that information can only pass between them as a compressed symbolic state.
  We introduce \textbf{Hourglass reasoning}, which enforces strict context isolation between reasoning stages. The frozen LLM acts as a meta-constructor, building for each task a symbolic encoder--decoder: an Induction module compresses the support examples into a schema $φ$ (encoder) and a transient scaffold $z$; a Deduction module derives rule $T$ (decoder) from these and discards $z$; an Implementer compiles $(φ, T)$ into artifacts; an error-driven Refiner revises $(φ, T)$ and regenerates artifacts from scratch. Only $(φ, T)$ crosses stage boundaries, so all refinement stays anchored to the rule.
  We evaluate Hourglass across three benchmarks spanning visual abstraction, hardware synthesis, and textual rule induction, using GPT-5.5 and Gemini 3.1 Pro. On ARC-AGI-2, it raises best-of-5 accuracy by up to 14 points over an iterative-refinement baseline. On ChipBench, it nearly doubles Verilog synthesis accuracy with GPT-5.5, from 31\% to 58\%. BBEH-Linguini draws on puzzles from the International Linguistics Olympiad, a setting where prior work has shown that explicit verbalization can hurt performance. Hourglass mitigates this tendency, and on Gemini 3.1 Pro, it reverses the effect entirely.
  Ablations confirm that these gains come from the isolation between stages and the quality of the initial induction, not from prompt wording or the particular symbolic form used. It is how information flows through the reasoning process, rather than the language used to express it, that drives inductive reasoning in frozen LLMs.

</details>


### [55] [Designing Agent-Ready Websites for AI Web Agents: A Framework for Machine Readability, Actionability, and Decision Reliability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12056v1)
*Said Elnaffar,Farzad Rashidi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent-ready网站框架，增强AI web agent的可靠性与效率，可迁移至coding agent设计。

TL;DR: 提出“代理就绪网站”设计框架，通过实验证明增强结构清晰性、行动提示等可大幅提升AI浏览代理的成功率和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SEO和GEO指标无法评估网站对AI代理的友好性，需要新框架支持人机共同交互。

Method: 构建三个维度（可解释性、可执行性、决策可靠性）的框架，通过对照实验（5任务、3代理、300次运行）比较基线网站与代理就绪网站。

Result: 代理就绪网站严格成功率89.3% vs 49.3%，部分结果从43降到3，平均步骤从9.31降到6.49。

Conclusion: 增强结构清晰性、行动提示、证据信号和时间有效性可显著提升AI浏览代理的可靠性和效率。

中文摘要：在线购物正日益转向一种模式，即AI代理独立为用户搜索产品、比较选项、评估约束并执行部分购买过程。网站设计现在必须同时支持人类和代理中介的交互。本文介绍了“代理就绪网站”，这是一个设计框架，旨在增强电子商务平台对AI代理的可读性、可解释性、可验证性和可操作性。现有的网页设计、搜索引擎优化（SEO）和生成式引擎优化（GEO）指标并不能完全评估网站对代理中介交互的能力。所提出的框架围绕三个维度构建：代理可解释性、代理可执行性和代理决策可靠性，并辅以机器可读性、语义清晰性、代理可操作性和上下文决策可靠性信号等特征。该框架通过一项对照实验进行评估，比较了面向人类基线和代理就绪版本的相同网站原型，两者具有相同的目录、定价、库存和购物流程。评估涉及五项任务、三种浏览器代理模型（GPT-4.1、Gemini-2.5 Flash和Grok-4 Fast）以及300次运行，测量了PASS、PARTIAL、FAIL结果、严格和功能成功率、错误模式、步骤数和令牌消耗。代理就绪网站在150次运行中实现了134次PASS，而基线为74次（严格成功率分别为89.3%和49.3%），在产品详情提取、比较和多约束选择方面提升最大。它还部分结果从43次减少到3次，平均步骤数从9.31降至6.49。这些结果提供了初步证据，表明增强的结构清晰性、行动提示、证据信号和时间有效性指标可以显著提高AI浏览器代理的可靠性和效率。

Original abstract: Online shopping is increasingly shifting toward a model in which AI agents independently search for products, compare options, evaluate constraints, and carry out parts of the purchasing process for users. Website design must now support both human and agent-mediated interaction. This paper introduces the agent-ready website, a design framework for enhancing the readability, interpretability, verifiability, and actionability of e-commerce platforms for AI agents. Existing web design, SEO, and generative engine optimization (GEO) metrics do not fully assess a website's capacity for agent-mediated interaction. The proposed framework is structured around three dimensions agent interpretability, agent executability, and agent decision reliability supported by features such as machine readability, semantic clarity, agent actionability, and contextual decision-reliability signals. The framework is evaluated through a controlled experiment comparing a human-oriented baseline and an agent-ready version of an identical website prototype, with identical catalogs, pricing, stock, and shopping workflows. The evaluation involved five tasks, three browser-agent models (GPT-4.1, Gemini-2.5 Flash, and Grok-4 Fast), and 300 runs, measuring PASS,PARTIAL,FAIL outcomes, strict and functional success rates, error patterns, step counts, and token consumption. The agent-ready website achieved 134 PASS runs out of 150 versus 74 out of 150 for the baseline (strict success rates of 89.3% vs. 49.3%), with the largest gains in product detail extraction, comparison, and multi-constraint selection. It also reduced PARTIAL outcomes from 43 to 3 and lowered the average step count from 9.31 to 6.49. These results provide preliminary evidence that enhanced structural clarity, action cues, evidence signals, and temporal validity indicators can substantially improve the reliability and efficiency of AI browser agents.

### [56] [Graph Feedback Controls Consensus and Clique Formation in Open-Weight Language-Model Populations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12077v1)
*Samer Saab,Chaouki Abdallah*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent语言模型群体的共识形成，涉及图反馈与协作，对多agent系统设计有启发。

TL;DR: 研究开源权重LM群体中的惯例形成，发现保留历史有助于达成共识，而阈值相似性路由导致碎片化，桥接搜索可修复碎片化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体语言模型系统中运行时交互图常被忽视，但其对惯例形成的影响至关重要。

Method: 使用命名博弈协议，通过受限首token分数测量状态分布，构建相似性图，并分离标签一致性与状态共识。

Result: 阈值相似性路由导致碎片化，桥接搜索在内存可用时修复碎片化；保留历史促进共识，Qwen2.5-32B在所有保留历史设置中达成共识。

Conclusion: 保留历史对于达成共识至关重要，而路由策略的选择显著影响系统收敛性，图能量特征可作为有效诊断工具。

中文摘要：多智能体语言模型系统越来越多地路由局部交互，但运行时交互图通常被视为实现细节。我们通过命名博弈协议研究了参数规模1.1B-32B的开源权重LM群体中的惯例形成。基于token化安全标签的受限首token分数，我们可以测量提示条件分数状态分布，构建状态相似性图，并将采样标签一致性从潜在状态空间共识中分离出来。在受控干预中，主要开源权重修复网格中，保留的伙伴标签证据是必要但不充分的：同质性阈值相似性路由消除了跨盆地暴露并加剧了碎片化，而桥接搜索路由在内存可用时通常能修复碎片化。在一个三种种子混合四模型网格中，阈值相似性在189个设置-种子运行中未产生最终行为或状态共识，而状态组件和标签不一致桥接在14/18次保留内存运行中恢复了最终行为共识。在同质模型群体中，保留历史通常将碎片化动态转向共识；最明显的案例是Qwen2.5-32B，在所有18次保留历史充分混合设置中达到稳定行为和最终状态共识，而阈值相似性在189个设置中未达到任何一种共识。在状态阈值、种群大小和词汇量上的鲁棒性保持了定性排序，早期窗口图能量特征提供了有用的网格内诊断。

Original abstract: Multi-agent language-model systems increasingly route local interactions, yet the runtime interaction graph is often treated as an implementation detail. We study convention formation in open-weight LM populations spanning 1.1B-32B parameters with a naming-game protocol. Restricted first-token scores over tokenizer-safe labels let us measure prompt-conditioned score-state distributions, construct state-similarity graphs, and separate sampled-label agreement from latent state-space consensus. Across controlled interventions, in the main open-weight repair grids, retained partner-label evidence is necessary but not sufficient: homophilous threshold-similarity routing deletes cross-basin exposure and amplifies fragmentation, while bridge-seeking routing often repairs fragmentation when memory is available. In a three-seed mixed four-model grid, threshold-similarity produces no final behavioral or state consensus in 189 setting-seed runs, whereas state-component and label-disagreement bridges recover final behavioral consensus in 14/18 retained-memory runs. Across homogeneous model populations, retained history generally shifts fragmented dynamics toward consensus; the clearest case is Qwen2.5-32B, which reaches stable behavioral and final state consensus in all 18 retained-history well-mixed settings, while threshold-similarity reaches neither form of consensus in 189 settings. Robustness over state thresholds, population size, and vocabulary size preserves the qualitative ordering, and early-window graph-energy features provide useful within-grid diagnostics.

</details>


### [57] [Operationalising Multi-Dimensional Evaluation for Conversational Agents: A Scalable, Governed Pipeline with Selective Re-evaluation and Model Benchmarking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12085v1)
*Niranjan Kumar M,Balaji Nagarajan,Karthik Nair,Faysal Satter,Nithin Surendran*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 对话agent的多维评估流水线，LLM-as-judge方法可迁移至coding agent评估。

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为GenAI Evaluation的配置驱动管道，用于大规模评估零售对话系统，通过LLM评分处理50,000条/天的日志，实现了宏F1 0.93和89%的翻译准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法（如词汇重叠指标）无法充分评估对话系统的意图对齐、事实性等维度，而LLM作为评判员在生产环境中面临治理、可重复性等挑战，需要一种可扩展且受治理的评估框架。

Method: 构建了一个配置驱动的评估管道，包含日志规范化、分片、异步执行和模式约束的LLM评分；支持选择性重新评估，并通过模式锁定、版本化配置和记录级出处实现可审计性。

Result: 每天处理约50,000条记录，总计评估超过200万次交互；在12,980条人工标注数据上，宏F1达到0.93，翻译准确率为89%。

Conclusion: GenAI Evaluation提供了一种有效、可扩展且受治理的大规模对话评估方案，在零售场景下取得了高准确率和良好的可审计性。

中文摘要：评估零售对话智能体需要超越词汇重叠指标的方法，以评估意图对齐、事实性、帮助性、清晰度、语气和整体响应质量。尽管LLM-as-a-judge方法提供了可扩展的替代方案以替代人工评估，但生产部署引入了治理、可重复性、成本、模式一致性、可追溯性和可靠性方面的挑战。我们提出GenAI Evaluation，一个受治理的、配置驱动的管道，用于大规模评估零售对话系统。它通过规范化、分片、异步执行和模式约束的LLM评分来处理生产聊天机器人日志。该框架评估帮助性、真实性、清晰度、语气一致性以及翻译特定维度。选择性重新评估仅处理不完整、格式错误或模式无效的记录，而模式锁定、版本化配置、验证日志和记录级出处支持可审计性。该框架每天处理约50,000条记录，并已评估超过两百万次交互。验证使用了来自四名训练注释者的12,980条分层随机人工标记记录。分类覆盖了14个意图、156个子意图、18个主要领域和129个子领域。该管道实现了0.93的宏F1得分和89%的翻译人类可接受性准确率。

Original abstract: Evaluating retail conversational agents requires methods beyond lexical-overlap metrics to assess intent alignment, factuality, helpfulness, clarity, tone, and overall response quality. Although LLM-as-a-judge methods provide scalable alternatives to human evaluation, production deployment introduces challenges in governance, reproducibility, cost, schema consistency, traceability, and reliability. We present GenAI Evaluation, a governed, configuration-driven pipeline for large-scale evaluation of retail conversational systems. It processes production chatbot logs through normalization, sharding, asynchronous execution, and schema-constrained LLM scoring. The framework evaluates helpfulness, truthfulness, clarity, tone alignment, and translation-specific dimensions. Selective re-evaluation processes only incomplete, malformed, or schema-invalid records, while schema locking, versioned configurations, validation logs, and record-level provenance support auditability. The framework processes approximately 50,000 records daily and has evaluated more than two million interactions. Validation used 12,980 stratified-random human-labeled records from four trained annotators. Classification covered 14 intents, 156 sub-intents, 18 major domains, and 129 sub-domains. The pipeline achieved a macro F1 score of 0.93 and 89% human-acceptability accuracy for translation.

### [58] [Good Benchmarks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12217v1)
*Ivan Bercovich*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 讨论良好benchmark设计原则，可迁移至agent评测

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 给出了好任务的明确定义和特征描述，为实际应用提供指导。

Conclusion: 好的任务应聚焦于真实问题、使用专业语言、以结果验证任务有效性。

中文摘要：好的任务是正确、可解决、可验证、明确指定，并且因有趣的原因而困难。最好的任务描述了一个有经验的从业者会认识到的真实问题，使用从业者会使用的语言，并附有验证结果而非方法的测试。

Original abstract: Good tasks are correct, solvable, verifiable, well-specified, and hard for interesting reasons. The best tasks describe a real problem an experienced practitioner would recognize, in language a practitioner would use, with tests that verify the outcome rather than the approach.

### [59] [Complexity Theory of Randomised Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11811v1)
*Pingshi Yu,Chengsong Tan,Nicolas Wu,Alastair Donaldson*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文为软件测试中的随机生成器建立复杂性理论基础，刻画了可生成语言与高效生成的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机测试的理论基础薄弱，缺乏对“可生成性”的正式定义，限制了其在边界测试中的应用。

Method: 将生成器建模为图灵换能器，利用计算复杂性理论（时间、空间有界）分析生成器的能力，并定义证书方案刻画高效生成。

Result: 理论上可生成语言等价于递归可枚举语言；高效生成与高效决策的复杂性不同（P中语言可能无高效生成器）；多项式时间生成器等价于证书方案；某些逻辑谓词（合取、否定）无法组合出高效生成器，但NL类可行。

Conclusion: 建立了生成器的复杂性分类，揭示了高效生成的基本限制，为测试生成器的设计和理论分析提供了基础。

中文摘要：随机测试是一种广泛使用的软件验证方法，但其理论基础仍然薄弱。特别是，关于一组输入“可生成”的基本含义在文献和常识中都没有得到解答。我们首次提出了软件测试中随机生成器的复杂性理论基础。我们将生成器建模为消耗随机位并产生字符串编码输出的图灵换能器，并表明理论上可生成的语言恰好与递归可枚举语言重合。这对可判定性边界上的测试（如编译器测试）有直接影响。对于高效生成，我们表明多项式时间可生成的语言位于NP内，某些NP完全语言拥有高效的生成器，并且——在标准密码学假设下——存在P中的语言没有高效的生成器：高效生成和高效决策的复杂性并不相同。我们表明空间有界复杂度是产生相关样本的生成器的自然框架，涵盖了诸如覆盖率引导的模糊测试和符号执行等方法。除了分类之外，我们刻画了高效可生成性：一个语言有多项式时间生成器当且仅当它在一个验证器上拥有证书方案——因此，用于测试SAT求解器的生成器背后的常识技术——见证植入，从某种意义上说是实现高效生成的唯一途径。在基于属性的测试库设计方面，我们证明在标准假设下，没有库能够从涉及合取或否定的逻辑谓词组合地派生高效生成器。然而，受限的类如NL（等价于线性Datalog谓词）将允许这样的编译。

Original abstract: Randomised testing is a widely-used approach to software validation, yet its theoretical foundations remain thin. In particular, the fundamental question of what it means for a set of inputs to be \emph{generable} has gone unanswered in both the literature and folklore. We present the first complexity-theoretic foundations for random generators in software testing. We model generators as Turing transducers that consume random bits and produce string-encoded outputs, and show that the theoretically generable languages coincide exactly with the recursively enumerable languages. This has direct implications for testing at the boundaries of decidability, such as compiler testing. For \emph{efficient} generation, we show that the polynomial-time generable languages lie within \textit{NP}, that certain \textit{NP}-complete languages admit efficient generators, and that -- under standard cryptographic assumptions -- there are languages in \textit{P} for which no efficient generator exists: the complexity of efficienct generation and of efficient decision are not the same. We show space-bounded complexity is the natural framework for generators producing \emph{correlated} samples, capturing methodologies such as coverage-guided fuzzing and symbolic execution. Beyond classification, we characterise efficient generability: a language has a polynomial-time generator iff it admits a \emph{certificate scheme} over a verifier -- so witness planting, the folklore technique behind generators to test SAT solvers, is in a sense the only route to efficient generation. On the design of property-based testing libraries, we prove no library can compositionally derive efficient generators from logical predicates involving conjunction or negation, under standard assumptions. However, restricted classes like \textit{NL} (equivalently, linear Datalog predicates) would admit such a compilation.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [60] [PRISM Edit: One Vector for All Temporal Answers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11327v2)
*Chen Huang,Qi Zheng,Ruiqin Zheng,Long Zeng,Yuantong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 模型编辑方法，可服务于agent知识更新，但非直接agent架构。

TL;DR: 提出PRISM Edit方法，通过利用LLM内部的两阶段时间感知计算机制，在不修改架构的情况下实现时间事实的编辑，显著提升时间一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有定位-编辑范式在时间事实变化时无法区分新旧答案的适用性，需要一种支持时间上下文感知的编辑方法。

Method: 基于因果追踪发现LLM的两阶段处理（早期MLP层得时间无关表示，后期层用时间上下文调制），优化单个多义表示并通过模型固有调制路径实现时间正确预测。

Result: 在TimeConflict和CounterFact基准上，PRISM Edit在时间一致性（TC）上提升23.3，当前相对时间分数（CRS）提升33.7，速度加快2倍以上。

Conclusion: PRISM Edit有效解决了时间事实编辑问题，无需架构修改，性能显著优于基线。

中文摘要：模型编辑使大型语言模型（LLM）无需重新训练即可保持更新，但时间事实暴露了当前定位-编辑范式的一个局限性：更新并不总是替换。当事实发生变化时，新答案应当成为当前答案，而旧答案在历史时间上下文中可能仍然正确。基于这一见解，我们使用因果追踪表明，LLM已经通过两阶段内部计算支持这种区分：早期的MLP层检索与时间无关的主体表示，后期的层用时间上下文对其进行调制，以产生时间正确的答案。受此发现启发，我们引入了PRISM Edit，它在时间上下文中优化单个多义表示，并利用模型固有的调制路径将其路由到时间上正确的预测，无需任何架构修改。我们在TimeConflict（我们引入的新的时间编辑基准）和时间增强的CounterFact上进行评估。PRISM Edit在平均时间一致性（TC）上比最佳基线提高+23.3，在当前相对时间分数（CRS）上提高+33.7，同时速度提高2倍以上。代码和数据公开在https://github.com/AnonymousStudy972/PRISM-Edit。

Original abstract: Model editing keeps large language models (LLMs) up to date without retraining, but temporal facts expose a limitation of the prevailing locate-and-edit paradigm: an update is not always a replacement. When a fact changes, the new answer should become current while the old answer may remain correct in historical time contexts. Building on this insight, we use causal tracing to show that LLMs already support this distinction via a two-stage internal computation: early MLP layers retrieve a time-agnostic subject representation, and later layers modulate it with temporal context to yield the time-correct answer. Motivated by this finding, we introduce PRISM Edit, which optimizes a single polysemous representation across temporal contexts and leverages the model's inherent modulation pathway to route it to temporally correct predictions, without any architectural modification. We evaluate on TimeConflict, a new temporal editing benchmark we introduce, and on temporally augmented CounterFact. PRISM Edit improves over the best baseline by +23.3 Temporal Consistency (TC) and +33.7 Current Relative-time Score (CRS) on average while being more than 2x faster. Code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/AnonymousStudy972/PRISM-Edit.

</details>


### [61] [BackgroundMellow: A Multi-Modal Cohesive Framework for Narrative-Driven Rich Cinematic Soundscape Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11364v1)
*Ajitesh Jamulkar,Aritra Hazra*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多agent master-specialist架构，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出BackgroundMellow框架，通过主-专家代理架构和NLP参数预测，实现长文本叙事的沉浸式同步电影级音频生成，实验验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TTA方法在长文本叙事中缺乏叙事连贯性、时间对齐和电影情感深度。

Method: 采用主-专家代理架构分解文本为精确音频线索，利用Tango2扩散模型和电影BGM检索器生成音景，并通过NLP模块预测音频参数进行自动化混音。

Result: 通过最近邻检索评估，所提框架在时序同步、覆盖率和频谱丰富度上表现有效。

Conclusion: BackgroundMellow能够为长文本叙事生成沉浸式、同步且电影化的音频。

中文摘要：生成沉浸式、同步且电影化的长文本叙事音频仍然是多模态AI中的一个重大挑战。虽然当前的文本到音频（TTA）框架成功合成了孤立的声音效果，但它们在叙事连贯性、时间对齐和电影情感深度方面存在困难。我们提出了BackgroundMellow，一个将故事到音频生成视为精确编排和信号处理问题的框架。该框架通过无真实标签的主-专家代理架构实现，该架构将文本分解为精确的多层音频线索，用合适的专家模型生成每类声音，并叠加声音景观以创建统一且对齐的音频片段。我们的pipeline构建在Tango2潜在扩散模型之上用于环境声音合成，同时结合了一个从专业原声带中挖掘的新型电影化BGM检索器。为了自动化混音过程，我们使用了一个基于NLP的模块，该模块根据叙事时间线预测精确的音频参数，如开始时间、持续时间和相对响度。我们进一步通过实验评估了所提框架的有效性，利用最近邻检索针对一个由YouTube电影预告片组成的精选数据集，衡量了时间同步、覆盖率和频谱丰富度。

Original abstract: Generating immersive, synchronized and cinematic audio for long-form textual narratives remains a significant challenge in multi-modal AI. While current Text-to-Audio (TTA) frameworks successfully synthesize isolated sound effects, they struggle with narrative cohesion, temporal alignment, and cinematic emotional depth. We present BackgroundMellow, a framework that treats story-to-audio generation as a precise orchestration and signal processing problem. This framework is enabled without ground-truth through a master-specialist agent architecture that decomposes text into precise and multi-layered audio cues, generates each category of sounds with suitable specialist model, and superimposes the soundscapes to create a unified and aligned audio segment. Our pipeline is built over Tango2 latent diffusion model for environmental synthesis alongside a novel Cinematic BGM Retriever mined from professional soundtracks. To automate the sound mixing process, we use an NLP based module that predicts precise audio parameters, like start time, duration, and relative loudness, based on the narrative timeline. We further empirically evaluate and show the efficacy of the proposed framework leveraging nearest-neighbor retrieval against a curated dataset of YouTube cinematic trailers to measure temporal synchronization, coverage, and spectral richness.
