### [88] [Flout at Your Own Risk: LLMs Struggle with Pragmatic Cooperativity Under Epistemic Asymmetry](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11053v1)
*Hannah VanderHoeven,Abhijnan Nath,Nikhil Krishnaswamy*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究LLM在多智能体协作中的语用能力，对agent协作设计有启发。

TL;DR: LLMs在部分信息下的多主体协作任务中展现了一定的语用推理能力，但仍面临不完整信息交流的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于LLMs在协作和智能体管道中的广泛使用，需要探究它们在不完全信息条件下的语用推理能力。

Method: 形式化了协作性认知不对称概念，并实验评估了多种LLMs作为说话者和听者时的合作能力，采用了提示和后训练策略。

Result: LLMs表现出一定的语用能力，可通过提示和后训练提升，但在不完整信息下仍存在挑战，且某些失败与未识别的格赖斯准则违背相关。

Conclusion: LLMs在协作语用交流中仍有局限，未来工作需改进其在信息不对称下的表现。

中文摘要：富有成效的合作依赖于合作性交流，包括将上下文线索纳入推理。大语言模型在协作和智能体管道中的日益使用引发了一个问题，即它们在多大程度上展现出这些语用能力，尤其是在它们可能无法获取与协作者相同信息的场景中。在本文中，我们在部分信息条件下，对多主体协作任务中大语言模型的语用推理能力进行了一项新颖的研究。我们形式化了协作性认知不对称的概念，该概念将客观任务成功与格赖斯的合作原则明确联系起来，并实证评估了各种大语言模型作为说话者和听者时的合作能力，包括提示和后训练策略。我们的结果表明，虽然大语言模型在协作环境中表现出一定的语用能力，并且这些能力可以通过提示和后训练来激发，但它们在不完整信息下的语用交流仍面临挑战，并且某些失败模式确实与未被识别的格赖斯准则违背相关。

Original abstract: Fruitful collaborations rely on cooperative communications, including of contextual cues to incorporate into reasoning. The increasing use of LLMs in collaborative and agentic pipelines raises questions about the extent to which they exhibit these pragmatic capabilities, especially in scenarios where they may not have access to the same information as their collaborators. In this paper, we perform a novel investigation into the pragmatic reasoning capabilities of LLMs in a multi-party collaborative task under partial information conditions. We formalize a notion of collaborative epistemic asymmetry that explicitly connects objective task success to Grice's cooperative principle and empirically assess various LLMs' abilities to act cooperatively as both speakers and listeners, including both prompting and post-training strategies. Our results show that while LLMs exhibit certain pragmatic capabilities in collaborative settings, and these can be elicited through prompting and post-training, they still face challenges in pragmatic communication with incomplete information, and that certain failure modes do correlate with floutings of Grice's maxims that go unrecognized.

</details>


### [89] [ProgramTab: Boosting Table Reasoning of LLMs via Programmatic Paradigm](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11207v1)
*Pei Guo,Enjie Liu,Yunzhi Tan,Mochi Gao,Jianxin Zhang,Ruichao Zhong,Juntao Li,Bo Hu,Zang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 用Python代码进行表格推理，属于LLM代码生成agent，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出ProgramTab框架，通过上下文学习指导LLMs使用Python代码预处理表格并提取关键信息，有效提升表格推理性能并超越所有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法面对大表格时性能下降，文本到SQL方法不适用于结构不一致的网页表格，需要更灵活的方法处理表格推理。

Method: ProgramTab框架利用上下文学习，指导LLMs使用Python代码进行表格数据预处理，并通过行/列提取和SQL生成提取重要内容。

Result: 在表格推理数据集上，ProgramTab框架优于所有基于LLM的基线方法。

Conclusion: ProgramTab框架有效处理基于表格的推理任务，展示了结合代码生成和上下文学习的潜力。

中文摘要：基于表格的推理与大型语言模型（LLMs），需要基于自然语言问题和结构化表格数据进行推理，已获得广泛关注。然而，一系列问题仍制约着该任务的应用。先前的方法在面对大表格时性能显著下降，原因是长文本建模困难和LLMs输入长度限制。文本到SQL方法用于高效提取表格中的关键信息并生成较小的子表。然而，表格数据，尤其是网页表格，往往缺乏必要的结构和一致性，使得不适合使用SQL查询执行数学逻辑运算。我们提出了ProgramTab框架，利用上下文学习指导LLMs使用Python代码进行表格数据预处理，以及通过行和列提取和SQL生成进行重要内容提取。在表格推理数据集上的实验结果表明，ProgramTab框架有效处理基于表格的推理任务，并优于所有基于LLM的基线。

Original abstract: Table-based reasoning with large language models (LLMs), which requires reasoning based on natural language questions and structured tabular data, has gained widespread attention. However, a series of issues still constrain the application of this task. The previous approaches suffered from significant performance degradation when faced with large tables due to the difficulty of long text modeling and the limitation of input length for LLMs. The text-to-SQL approach is used to efficiently extract key information from tables and generate smaller sub-tables. However, tabular data, especially web tables, often lack the necessary structure and consistency, making them unsuitable for performing mathematical logic operations using SQL queries. We propose the ProgramTab framework, which guides LLMs employing in-context learning to perform tabular data preprocessing with Python code, as well as the momentous contents extraction with row and column extraction and SQL generation. The experiment results on table reasoning datasets demonstrate that the ProgramTab framework effectively deals with table-based reasoning tasks and outperforms all LLM-based baselines.

</details>


### [90] [Automated Textbook Auditing with Multi-Agent LLM Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11276v1)
*Ciprian Cristescu,Adrian-Marius Dumitran,Angela-Liliana Dumitran,Gabriel Stefan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent管道审计教材，通用多agent架构和工具使用。

TL;DR: 提出一个基于多智能体管道的AI教科书审核系统，通过事实/技术轨道和语法轨道自动检测教育材料中的各种错误，并由裁判智能体过滤后供人工验证，在罗马尼亚教科书上取得较好效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用语法检查器无法同时处理教科书中事实准确性、技术正确性和语言质量的审核需求，需要专门的自动化工具。

Method: 构建模块化多智能体管道，包括事实与技术轨道（多个LLM智能体检测事实、代码、定义等错误，人文学科结合网络搜索）、语法轨道（PDF原生保持编码）、裁判智能体（基于领域规则过滤误报），支持视觉/文本两种PDF摄取模式，并通过自定义提示适应不同学科。

Result: 在罗马尼亚高中CS教科书上检测56个技术发现（专家验证精确率62.5%），在历史与社会教科书上检测72个发现（含事实错误、意识形态偏见、语法问题）。

Conclusion: 该系统作为分诊工具可减少人工定位候选问题的工作量，但任何编辑行动前仍需人类专家验证。

中文摘要：确保教育材料质量需要的不仅仅是标准的校对：教科书必须同时进行事实准确性、领域特定的技术正确性和语言质量的审核——这是一个通用语法检查器无法解决的任务。我们提出**AI Textbook Auditor**，一个模块化的多智能体管道，用于跨学科领域的教育材料的自动质量保证。该系统接受教科书PDF，并通过两个分析轨道生成结构化、人工可审查的报告：**事实与技术轨道**，其中一组专门的LLM智能体检测事实不准确、代码错误、错误定义和概念不一致，并结合网络搜索用于人文学科领域；以及**语法轨道**，该轨道在PDF原生操作以保留变音符号编码。一个**裁判智能体**使用领域特定规则过滤误报，然后将发现呈现给人工审查员。管道支持两种摄取模式——视觉原生页面渲染和PyMuPDF文本提取——并且可以通过编码特定学科错误分类的自定义提示进行领域适应。我们在两本罗马尼亚高中教科书上演示了该系统：一本CS教科书（7个类别共56个技术发现，专家验证精确率为62.5%）和一本历史与社会教科书（72个发现，涵盖事实错误、意识形态偏见和语法）。该系统设计为一个分诊工具，减少手动定位候选问题的工作量，但在任何编辑行动之前需要人类专家验证。

Original abstract: Ensuring the quality of educational materials requires more than standard proofreading: textbooks must be audited for factual accuracy, domain-specific technical correctness, and linguistic quality simultaneously -- a task that general-purpose grammar checkers cannot address. We present \textbf{AI Textbook Auditor}, a modular multi-agent pipeline for automated quality assurance of educational materials across subject domains. The system accepts a textbook PDF and produces a structured, human-reviewable report via two analysis tracks: a \textbf{Factual and Technical Track} in which an ensemble of specialized LLM agents detects factual inaccuracies, code errors, incorrect definitions, and conceptual inconsistencies, augmented with web search for humanities domains; and a \textbf{Grammar Track} operating PDF-natively to preserve diacritical encoding. A \textbf{Judge Agent} filters false positives using domain-specific rules before presenting findings to a human reviewer. The pipeline supports two ingestion modes -- vision-native page rendering and PyMuPDF text extraction -- and is domain-adaptable via custom prompts encoding subject-specific error taxonomies. We demonstrate the system on two Romanian upper-secondary textbooks: a CS textbook (56 technical findings across seven categories, with an expert-validated precision of 62.5\%) and a history and social sciences textbook (72 findings spanning factual errors, ideological bias, and grammar). The system is designed as a triage tool that reduces the manual effort of locating candidate issues, with human expert validation required before any editorial action.

### [91] [Beyond Sally-Anne: Evaluating Theory of Mind in LLMs using Epistemic Schelling Points](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11363v1)
*Roberta Rocca,Sami Boukortt,Geoff Keeling,Winnie Street*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: ToM评估benchmark，有助于agent社会推理评测。

TL;DR: 提出EAST任务评估LLM的心智理论能力，发现仅前沿模型能处理认知跟踪，存在显著社交推理差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有静态基准易被预训练知识影响，无法测试LLM在自然场景中泛化的功能性心智理论能力。

Method: 设计双玩家对话游戏EAST，要求LLM-LLM二元组在认知透明变化下独立收敛于语义谢林点。

Result: 仅前沿模型成功应对认知需求，失败主因是混淆私有知识与共同知识等认知跟踪错误。

Conclusion: 尽管静态基准表现优异，稳健社交推理仍是关键瓶颈，需针对性改进。

中文摘要：基于文本的大语言模型（LLM）心智理论评估通常采用类似于Sally-Anne任务的认知测试，这些测试可能因模型在预训练中接触过类似任务而被轻易通过，并且无法明显测试模型在自然场景中泛化的功能性心智理论能力。为解决这些问题，我们引入了认知不对称谢林任务（EAST），这是一个双玩家对话游戏，旨在评估稳健且可泛化的心智理论能力。通过要求LLM-LLM二元组在认知透明状态变化下独立收敛于语义谢林点，我们评估模型是否能稳健运用心智理论实现协调。我们的结果显示功能性社交推理存在显著能力差距，仅前沿模型能成功应对任务中变化的认知需求。推理轨迹分析表明，协调失败主要由认知跟踪错误（如混淆私有知识与共同知识）导致。尽管在传统静态基准上表现优异，本研究表明稳健的社交推理和认知跟踪仍是关键瓶颈，为未来LLM评估和发展提供了具体目标。

Original abstract: Text-based evaluations of Theory of Mind (ToM) in Large Language Models (LLMs) often involve cognitive tests akin to the Sally-Anne task that can be gamed due to exposure to relevantly similar tasks in pre-training and do not obviously test models' functional ToM abilities in ways that generalize to naturalistic settings. To address these issues, we introduce the Epistemic Asymmetry Schelling Task (EAST), a two-player dialogue game designed to benchmark robust and generalizable ToM abilities. By requiring LLM-LLM dyads to independently converge on semantic Schelling points under varying states of epistemic transparency, we evaluate whether models can robustly apply ToM to achieve coordination. Our results reveal a significant capability gap in functional social reasoning, with only frontier models successfully navigating the varying epistemic demands of the tasks. Analysis of reasoning traces shows that coordination failures are primarily driven by epistemic tracking errors, such as conflating private knowledge with mutual knowledge. Despite high performance on traditional static benchmarks, our study shows that robust social reasoning and epistemic tracking remain a critical bottleneck, providing concrete targets for future LLM evaluation and development.

### [92] [Agentic Routing: The Harness-Native Data Flywheel](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11399v1)
*Xinchen Liu,Hang Zhou,Yingjie Zong,Yuchuan Tian,Liuyang Song,Shuo Zhang,Yulong Li,Wei He,Mengyu Zheng,Runke Liu,Siyang Cheng,Xiang Kuang,Hailin Hu,Kai Han,Yunhe Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: agent路由与数据飞轮，直接讨论agent系统优化。

TL;DR: 提出Harness-Native代理路由，利用执行框架状态进行步骤级模型选择，并通过路由决策产生的结构化数据形成数据飞轮，持续优化成本-质量权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有路由方法仅优化单次成本-质量，忽略代理执行状态、中间失败和反馈循环，且模型专业化趋势使模型选择成为核心系统问题。

Method: 提出步骤级路由范式，根据完整框架状态选择单模型或多模型；利用环境提供的结构化数据记录构建数据飞轮；在OpenSquilla中实现四层路由栈、LightGBM冷启动排序器和分阶段路由策略。

Result: 在DRACO和PinchBench等代理基准上验证单模型和多模型路由，显示成本-质量改善，并证明数据飞轮的有效性。

Conclusion: 代理路由不仅是成本控制工具，更是代理原生训练的数据引擎，通过执行轨迹持续改进路由策略和模型性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型代理越来越多地不是通过单个模型调用来执行，而是通过一个执行框架来管理观察、上下文、控制、动作、状态和验证。与此同时，前沿模型和开放模型在结构上变得专业化：一个在代码编辑、长上下文恢复、工具使用、数学推理或低延迟响应方面强大的模型可能在其他方面并不占优。这使得代理内部的模型选择成为一个核心系统问题，而不是一个每查询的服务技巧。现有的路由方法大多优化单次成本-质量权衡，因此忽略了使代理与聊天完成不同的执行状态、中间失败和反馈循环。我们提出了Harness-Native代理路由，一种步骤级路由范式，根据完整的框架状态选择单个最适合的模型以进行成本效益的执行，或选择多个互补模型以进行集成式的准确性改进。关键见解是，每个路由决策自然会产生一个结构化数据记录——包括查询、框架状态、模型选择或模型集、执行轨迹、结果和成本——其标签由环境提供，而不是由路由器本身提供。这些记录形成了一个框架原生的数据飞轮：执行轨迹训练出更好的路由器和框架原生模型，从而改善成本-质量权衡，并在相同预算下生成更多轨迹。我们在OpenSquilla中实例化这一想法，包括四层路由栈、一个开放的LightGBM冷启动排序器，以及一个分阶段的路由器-模型路径，将记录的竞技场记录转化为逐步更强的路由策略。该报告研究了在包括DRACO和PinchBench在内的代理基准上的单模型和多模型路由，并主张代理路由不仅仅是成本控制，而是代理原生训练的数据引擎。

Original abstract: Large language model agents are increasingly executed not by a single model call, but by an execution harness that manages observation, context, control, action, state, and verification. At the same time, frontier and open models are becoming structurally specialized: a model that is strong at code editing, long-context recovery, tool use, mathematical reasoning, or low-latency response may not dominate on the other axes. This makes model selection inside an agent a core systems problem rather than a per-query serving trick. Existing routing methods mostly optimize single-turn cost-quality trade-offs and therefore miss the execution state, intermediate failures, and feedback loops that make agents different from chat completion. We propose Harness-Native agentic routing, a step-level routing paradigm that selects either a single best-fit model for cost-effective execution or multiple complementary models for ensemble-style accuracy improvement, conditioned on the full harness state. The key insight is that every routing decision naturally produces a structured data record -- consisting of the query, harness state, model choice or model set, execution trace, outcome, and cost -- whose labels are supplied by the environment rather than by the router itself. These records form a harness-native data flywheel: execution traces train better routers and harness-native models, which improve cost-quality trade-offs and generate more traces under the same budget. We instantiate this idea in OpenSquilla with a four-layer routing stack, an open LightGBM cold-start ranker, and a staged router-model path that turns logged arena records into progressively stronger routing policies. The report studies singleton and multi-model routing on agentic benchmarks including DRACO and PinchBench, and argues that agentic routing is not merely cost control, but a data engine for agent-native training.

</details>


### [93] [LightMem-Ego: Your AI Memory for Everyday Life](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11487v1)
*Yijun Chen,Boyi Xiao,Yixian Zhao,Haoting Xia,Buqiang Xu,Jizhan Fang,Yanya Li,Yaqi Zheng,Xuehai Wang,Zirui Xue,Liuxin Zhang,Hui Li,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 流式记忆系统，对agent长期记忆有启示。

TL;DR: LightMem-Ego是一个轻量级流式多模态记忆系统，通过层次化记忆组织和动态检索，有效支持日常生活中的多模态查询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答关于过去经历的查询需要轻量级的多模态记忆，能够持续积累、组织和检索长期经验，这仍然具有挑战性。

Method: 持续捕获自我中心视觉和音频流，对齐到共享时间线，组织成当前、短期和长期记忆的层次结构，并根据查询动态路由检索到合适的记忆级别。

Result: 可部署于智能手机和AI眼镜，支持物体查找、对话回忆、生活总结、例行发现和个性化辅助。

Conclusion: LightMem-Ego为日常辅助提供了有效的轻量级多模态记忆解决方案，实现了对长期经验的持续积累、组织和检索。

中文摘要：移动和可穿戴设备上的个人AI助手通过视觉和音频流持续感知用户的日常生活。然而，回答关于过去经历的查询需要轻量级的多模态记忆，能够持续积累、组织和检索长期经验，这仍然具有挑战性。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了LightMem-Ego，一个用于日常辅助的轻量级流式多模态记忆系统。该系统持续捕获以自我为中心的视觉和音频流，将其对齐到共享时间线上，并组织成一个由当前记忆、短期记忆和长期记忆组成的层次化记忆。给定用户查询，LightMem-Ego动态地将检索路由到适当的记忆级别，并生成基于多模态证据的答案。该演示可以部署在智能手机和AI眼镜上，支持物体查找、对话回忆、生活总结、例行发现和个性化辅助。代码可在https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem-Ego获取。

Original abstract: Personal AI assistants on mobile and wearable devices continuously perceive users' daily lives through visual and audio streams. However, answering queries about past experiences requires lightweight multimodal memory that can continuously accumulate, organize, and retrieve long-term experiences, which remains challenging. To address this challenge, we present LightMem-Ego, a lightweight streaming multimodal memory system for everyday-life assistance. The system continuously captures egocentric visual and audio streams, aligns them on a shared timeline, and organizes them into a hierarchical memory consisting of current, short-term, and long-term memory. Given a user query, LightMem-Ego dynamically routes retrieval to the appropriate memory level and generates answers grounded in multimodal evidence. The demonstration can be deployed on smartphones and AI glasses, supporting object finding, conversation recall, life summarization, routine discovery, and personalized assistance. Code is available at https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem-Ego.

### [94] [RAGU: A Multi-Step GraphRAG Engine with a Compact Domain-Adapted LLM](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11683v1)
*Mikhail Komarov,Ivan Bondarenko,Stanislav Shtuka,Oleg Sedukhin,Roman Shuvalov,Yana Dementyeva,Matvey Solovyov,Nikolay O. Nikitin*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: GraphRAG引擎，RAG属于LLM agent常用方法，可迁移到coding agent的检索增强。

TL;DR: RAGU是一个开源模块化GraphRAG引擎，通过分离提取与合并改善知识图谱构建，并训练了轻量模型Meno-Lite-0.1，在多项任务上达到或超越更大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GraphRAG系统单次提取构建知识图谱导致噪声和脆弱检索，需分离提取与合并，并利用语言技能与模型规模弱相关的特性训练高效小模型。

Method: RAGU采用两阶段类型化提取、DBSCAN去重、LLM摘要和Leiden社区检测；训练Meno-Lite-0.1（7B）专注于语言技能。

Result: Meno-Lite-0.1在知识图谱构建上相对Qwen2.5-32B提升12.5%调和平均值，在英文GraphRAG任务上持平；RAGU在医学GraphRAG-Bench上证据召回达0.84，超越HippoRAG2。

Conclusion: 分离提取与合并能有效提升GraphRAG性能，小模型通过优化语言技能可达到大模型效果，RAGU开源且易于部署。

中文摘要：图检索增强生成（GraphRAG）通过结构化知识增强了大型语言模型，但现有系统在单次提取过程中构建知识图谱，产生噪声实体和脆弱的检索。RAGU是一个开源模块化GraphRAG引擎，通过将提取与合并分离来解决这一问题：实体和关系经过两阶段类型化提取、基于DBSCAN的去重、LLM摘要和Leiden社区检测。一个关键见解催生了一个紧凑的提取器：管道内LLM所需的技能——理解、提取、上下文推理——是与模型规模弱相关的语言技能，不同于事实性世界知识。据此，我们训练了Meno-Lite-0.1，一个针对语言技能优化的7B模型，它在知识图谱构建上超越了Qwen2.5-32B（相对调和平均值+12.5%），并在英文GraphRAG任务上与之持平。在GraphRAG-Bench（医学）上，RAGU在每一个事实级别检索到最完整的上下文（证据召回率高达0.84，对比≤0.76），并在综合任务上超越HippoRAG2；在多跳事实型问答上，HippoRAG2的表面优势被证明主要是答案格式的伪影。RAGU可通过pip install graph_ragu安装，在单个GPU上运行，并以MIT许可发布。源代码公开在https://github.com/RaguTeam/RAGU，Meno-Lite-0.1模型可从https://huggingface.co/bond005/meno-lite-0.1获取。

Original abstract: Graph retrieval-augmented generation (GraphRAG) enhances large language models with structured knowledge, yet existing systems construct knowledge graphs in a single extraction pass, producing noisy entities and brittle retrieval. RAGU, an open-source modular GraphRAG engine, addresses this by separating extraction from consolidation: entities and relations pass through two-stage typed extraction, DBSCAN-backed deduplication, LLM summarization, and Leiden community detection. A key insight motivates a compact extractor: the skills an in-pipeline LLM needs - comprehension, extraction, reasoning over context - are language skills that grow only weakly with model size, unlike factual world knowledge. Accordingly, we train Meno-Lite-0.1, a 7B model optimized for language skills, which outperforms Qwen2.5-32B on knowledge-graph construction (+12.5% relative harmonic mean) and matches it on English GraphRAG tasks. On GraphRAG-Bench (Medical), RAGU retrieves the most complete context at every factoid level (evidence recall up to 0.84 vs. $\leq$0.76) and overtakes HippoRAG2 on synthesis tasks; on multi-hop factoid QA, the apparent HippoRAG2 advantage is shown to be largely an answer-format artifact. RAGU is installable via $\texttt{pip install graph_ragu}$, runs on a single GPU, and is released under MIT. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/RaguTeam/RAGU, and the Meno-Lite-0.1 model can be obtained from https://huggingface.co/bond005/meno-lite-0.1.

</details>


### [95] [Metacognition in LLMs: Foundations, Progress, and Opportunities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11881v1)
*Gabrielle Kaili-May Liu,Areeb Gani,Jacqueline Lu,Jordan Thomas,Mark Steyvers,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM元认知综述，涵盖自我评估与反思，可迁移至agent规划与改进。

TL;DR: 本文首次全面综述了LLMs的元认知能力，包括评估方法、提升技术和应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对LLMs元认知能力的系统理解，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 通过分析现有文献，分类整理元认知评估方法和提升技术，并总结最新进展。

Result: 提供了一个全面的综述，包括元认知能力的测量基准、改进方法以及未来研究方向。

Conclusion: LLMs的元认知能力研究仍处于早期阶段，但有望提升AI系统的可靠性和智能性。

中文摘要：元认知是智能的基本组成部分，对于有效学习、问题解决、决策、沟通等至关重要。近年来，它越来越被认为是能力强大、透明的AI系统的基石。然而，尽管LLMs在各种现实任务中取得了显著进展，但目前尚不清楚它们何时、如何以及在何种程度上能够展示或被赋予有效的元认知能力，也不清楚如何调整这些能力以提升AI系统的基本能力、可靠性和智能性。本文通过提供关于LLMs元认知当前知识状态的首个全面概述来弥合这一差距。我们分析并分类了这一新兴领域的格局，并总结了近期的技术进展，包括衡量和评估LLMs元认知能力的方法和基准、引发、改进和应用LLMs元认知的技术，以及正在进行的研究的发现和启示。我们还讨论了应用、开放问题与挑战，以及未来工作的有希望方向。我们的目标是提供该主题的详细且最新的综述，并激发有意义的研究和讨论。组织好的论文列表可在https://github.com/yale-nlp/LLM-Metacognition找到。

Original abstract: Metacognition is a foundational component of intelligence critical to effective learning, problem solving, decision-making, communication, and more. In recent years, it has become increasingly recognized as a cornerstone of capable, transparent AI systems. Yet while LLMs have made significant progress across diverse real-world tasks, it is not yet clear when, how, or to what extent they can exhibit or be endowed with effective metacognitive abilities, nor how such abilities can be adapted to advance the fundamental capabilities, reliability, and intelligence of AI systems. This paper bridges this gap by presenting the first comprehensive overview of the current state of knowledge on metacognition for LLMs. We analyze and taxonomize the landscape of this emerging field and summarize recent technical advancements, including methods and benchmarks to measure and evaluate LLMs' metacognitive abilities, techniques to elicit, improve, and apply metacognition in LLMs, and findings and implications of ongoing research. We also discuss applications, open questions and challenges, and promising directions for future work. Our aim is to provide a detailed and up-to-date review of this topic and stimulate meaningful research and discussion. An organized list of papers can be found at https://github.com/yale-nlp/LLM-Metacognition.

</details>


### [96] [RCWT: Measuring Task-Budget Displacement from Coordination Content in LLM Calls](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12216v1)
*Brenda Lelis,Rodrigo Cabral-Carvalho*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出RCWT测量多agent协调内容对任务预算的影响，对agent长程执行和上下文管理有启发

TL;DR: RCWT实验表明，固定上下文预算下协调内容挤占任务预算导致性能悬崖，但消融实验证明该悬崖源于预算位移而非语义干扰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统将协调内容与任务内容共享有限上下文窗口，导致token分配冲突，需量化该位移效应。

Method: 设计RCWT协议，控制总预算、位置等变量，变化协调内容；并引入完整任务消融实验，保持任务证据不变而扩展总长度增加协调token。

Result: 在W=4096召回任务中，模型性能在协调开销适度时稳定，随后急剧下降；消融实验中，高达95%协调比下所有模型仍正确返回所有评分字段。

Conclusion: RCWT悬崖主因是任务预算位移，而非协调内容本身的语义干扰；RCWT是上下文预算分配的测量原语，非完整理论。

中文摘要：多智能体和记忆增强的LLM系统通常将协调内容、共享状态、先前的讨论、工具输出、总结和角色指令放在用于当前任务的相同有限提示中。这产生了一个实际的分配问题：在固定上下文预算下组装调用时，每个用于协调的token都无法用于任务指令或证据。我们引入了圆桌上下文窗口测试（RCWT），这是一个用于测量这种任务预算位移效应的受控协议。RCWT在控制总预算、位置顺序、任务系列和评分的同时，变化协调内容。在W=4096的主要上下文依赖回忆任务中，三个商业模型在适度开销下保持接近基线，然后一旦剩余参考证据降至几百个token时性能急剧下降。窗口缩放总结与任务特定的剩余预算解释一致，而不是固定的百分比阈值，但我们将其视为描述性证据而非普遍规律。为了测试当任务证据保持完整时，固定预算悬崖是否仍然存在，我们添加了一个完整任务消融：保持完整任务/参考块存在，同时通过扩展总提示长度增加协调token。在该设置中，所有测试调用在GPT-4.1-mini、Claude Haiku 4.5和Gemini 2.5 Flash上，直到95%的协调比例下，都能正确返回每个评分字段。这一消融缩小了论断：主要的RCWT悬崖最好理解为任务预算位移，而不是证明协调量本身导致原始开放任务中的语义干扰。因此，RCWT是一个用于上下文分配预算的测量原语，而不是多智能体收益或会话级协调的完整理论。

Original abstract: Multi-agent and memory-augmented LLM systems often place coordination content, shared state, prior discussion, tool outputs, summaries, and role instructions, inside the same finite prompt used for the current task. This creates a practical allocation problem: every token spent on coordination is unavailable to task instructions or evidence when a call is assembled under a fixed context budget. We introduce the Roundtable Context Window Test (RCWT), a controlled protocol for measuring this task-budget displacement effect. RCWT varies coordination content while controlling total budget, position order, task family, and scoring. In the main context-dependent recall task at $W=4096$, three commercial models remain near baseline through moderate overhead and then degrade sharply once residual reference evidence falls to a few hundred tokens. Window-scaling summaries are consistent with a task-specific residual-budget interpretation rather than a fixed percentage threshold, but we treat this as descriptive evidence rather than a universal law. To test whether the fixed-budget cliff persists when task evidence remains intact, we add an intact-task ablation: the full task/reference block is kept present while coordination tokens increase by expanding total prompt length. In that setting, all tested calls return every scored field correctly across GPT-4.1-mini, Claude Haiku 4.5, and Gemini 2.5 Flash up to a 95\% coordination ratio. This ablation narrows the claim: the main RCWT cliff is best read as task-budget displacement, not as proof that coordination volume alone causes semantic interference in the original open-ended task. RCWT is therefore a measurement primitive for context-allocation budgeting, not a complete theory of multi-agent benefit or session-level coordination.

</details>
